pañcaskandhakavibhāṣā /
namo buddhāya /
pañca skandhā ityādi prakaraṇārambhaḥ /
sa ca dharmasvasāmānyalakṣaṇavyutpattyartham /
nanu ca yogācārabhūmyādiṣu śāstreṣu dharmalakṣaṇaṃ nirdhāritam eveti punas tannirdhāraṇāya yatnavaiyarthyam 		/
rgya gar skad du /
panytsa skan dha pra ka ra na bi bh'a shyam /
bod skad du /
phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa bye brag tu bshad pa /
bam po dang po /
sangs rgyas dang sbyang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo /
phung po lnga zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rab tu byed pa ci'i phyir rtsom zhe na /
chos thams cad kyi rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid rtogs par bya ba'i phyir ro /
rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa la sogs pa'i bstan bcos dag las chos kyi mtshan nyid dpyad zin na yang de dpyad pa don med par mi 'gyur ram /
na vaiyarthyam udghaṭitajñavineyārthitvāt don med par mi 'gyur te /
mgo smos pas go ba gdul ba'i don gyi phyir ro /
udghaṭitajñā hi diṅmātreṇa tatsambhavinoviśeṣān niravaśeṣān avaboddhuṃ samarthā iti saṅkṣepoktimeva bahu manyante na vistaroktim mgo smos pas go ba ni phyogs tsam gyis de rtogs pa'i khyad par rnams ma lus par khong du chud par nus pas mdor bshad pa nyid la dga'i /
rgya cher bshad pa la ni ma yin no /
ataś ca saṅkṣiptarucisattvānugrahāyedaṃ prakaraṇam ārabdham iti de'i phyir mdor bsdus pa 'dod pa'i sems can la phan gdags pa'i phyir rab tu byed pa 'di brtsams so /
athavā gṛhasthānāṃ bahukṛtyavyāpṛtatvād vistaragrantheṣv abhiyogāsambhavaḥ /
manasikārābhiyuktānāṃ ca pravrajitānām api vistaragranthābhiyogo vikṣepāyaivety ubhayeṣām api dharmalakṣaṇavyutpattyartham iha prakaraṇe dharmalakṣaṇaṃ samāsenoktam iti nāsti tadārambhavaiyarthyam 		yang na khyim na gnas pa rnams bya ba mang po la zhugs pa'i phyir le'u grangs rgya cher byas pa rnams la mngon par brtson mi srid pa dang rab tu byung ba yid la byed pa la mngon par brtson pa rnams kyang le'u grangs rgya cher byas pa la mngon par brtson par byas na gyeng bar 'gyur bas /
de gnyi gas chos kyi mtshan nyid rtogs par bya ba'i phyir rab tu byed pa 'dir chos kyi mtshan nyid mdor bshad de /
athavā saṅkṣepeṇadharmalakṣaṇavyutpannā ayatnena dharmalakṣaṇavistarapratipattisamarthā bhaviṣyantīty ato yogācārabhūmyādīnāṃ vistaragranthānāṃ praveśabhūtam idam ācāryeṇa prakaraṇaṃ kṛtamiti de ltar na de brtsams pa don med par mi 'gyur ro /
yang na chos kyi mtshan nyid mdor bsdus pa rtogs nas chos kyi mtshan nyid rgyas pa yang bsgrim mi dgos par rtogs nus par 'gyur te /
de'i phyir slob dpon gyis rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa la sogs pa'i le'u grangs rgya cher byas pa rnams la 'jug par 'gyur ba'i rgyur rab tu byed pa 'di mdzad do /
kiṃ punar dharmalakṣaṇavyutpattyā vinā na sidhyati yatrācāryo dharmalakṣaṇanirdeśaṃ praty ādriyate chos kyi mtshan nyid rtogs pa med par ci zhig mi 'grub na /
'di ltar slob dpon gyis chos kyi mtshan nyid bstan par gus par mdzad ce na /
cittaikāgratāsāṅkathyaviniścayeṣu ca praśnavyākaraṇakauśalam sems rtse gcig tu bya ba dang 'bel ba'i gtam brtsal bar nges ba rnams la dris pa lung bstan pa la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir te /
tathā hidharmalakṣaṇakṛtaparicayasya sandehābhāvād yatheṣṭam ālambane cittam ekāgrībhavati nānyathā 'di ltar chos kyi mtshan nyid la byang bar byas na the tshom med pa'i phyir ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du dmigs pa la sems rtse gcig tu 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma yin no /
dharmalakṣaṇapravicayāc ca prajñāprakarṣagamanād vaiśāradyaṃ pratilabhate chos kyi mtshan nyid rab tu rnam par 'byed pas kyang shes rab mchog tu 'gyur bas mi 'jigs pa thob ste /
viśāradaś ca sāṅkathyaviniścayeṣu sarvapraśnatadvyākaraṇanirdeśasamartho bhavati nānyathā 'jigs pa med pa ni 'bel ba'i gtam rnam par nges pa rnams la dris pa de thams cad du lung ston nus par 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma yin no /
pañca skandhā iti nyūnātiriktapratiṣedhena saṅkhyāvadhāraṇam phung po lnga zhes bya ba ni mang nyung dgag pa'i phyir grangs nges par gzung ba'o /
nirviśeṣaṇaskandhaśabdaprayogātsāsravānāsravaskandhopādānam /
pañcaiva skandhā na nyūnā adhikā vā 		phung po'i sgra bye brag med par smos pas zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa'i phung po gzung bar bya'o /
phung po ni lnga kho na ste /
ātmātmīyagrāhavastupradarśanārthamprāyeṇa hi bālānāṃvijñāna evātmagrāhaḥ śeṣeṣu rūpādiṣv ātmīyagrāhaḥ bdag dang bdag gir 'dzin pa'i gzhi rab tu bstan pa'i phyir /
mang ba'am nyung ba ma yin te /
byis pa dag ni phal cher rnam par shes pa nyid la ni bdag tu 'dzin /
gzugs la sogs pa ltag ma rnams la ni bdag gir 'dzin te /
tathā hi bāhyādhyātmikasya rūpasya karaṇatvena karmatvena vātmanā sambandha iti rūpaskandha ātmīyagrāhaḥ 'di ltar phyi dang nang gi gzugs ni byed pa dang las su bya bar bdag dang 'brel to snyam du gzugs kyi phung po la bdag gir 'dzin to /
śubhāśubhānāṃkarmaṇāṃ vedanā vipākaḥ tāṃ cātmā saṃvedayata iti vedanāskandha ātmīyagrāhaḥ las dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'i tshor ba de bdag gis yang dag par myong bar byed do snyam du tshor ba'i phung po la bdag gir 'dzin te /
tatra śubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ sukho'nubhavo vipākaḥ /
aśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ duḥkhaḥ /
ubhayeṣāmaduḥkhāsukhaḥ 		de la bde ba myong ba ni las dge ba rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'o /
sdug bsngal ni las mi dge ba rnams kyi'o /
sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa ni gnyi ga'i'o /
atra cālayavijñānasamprayuktopekṣaivaparamārthataḥ karmavipākaḥ śubhāśubhakarmavipākatvādālayavijñānasya 'dir ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dar mtshungs par ldan pa'i tshor ba btang snyoms nyid yang dag par na las kyi rnam par smin pa ste /
kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid las dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rnam par smin pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
sukhaduḥkhayos tu vipākajatvād vipākopacāraḥ bde ba dang sdug bsngal gnyis ni rnam par smin pa las 'byung ba'i phyir rnam par smin par gdags pa'o /
dṛṣṭaśrutamatavijñāteṣv artheṣv ātmanaḥ sañjñādvāreṇasaṃvyavahāraḥ pravartata iti sañjñāskandha ātmīyagrāhaḥ mthong ba dang thos pa dang bye brag phyed pa dang rnam par shes pa'i don rnams la bdag tu 'du shes pa'i sgo nas tha snyad 'dogs par byed do snyam du 'du shes kyi phung po la bdag gir 'dzin to /
kuśalākuśalādiṣu saṃskārair ātmābhimatasya cittasya preraṇātsaṃskāraskandha ātmīyagrāha iti pañcaiva skandhaḥ bdag tu 'dod pa'i sems ni 'du byed rnams kyis dge ba dang mi dge ba la sogs pa la 'jug par byed pas 'du byed kyi phung po la bdag gir 'dzin te /
phung po ni lnga kho na'o /
atha kasmāt skandhānām iyam evānupūrvī 'o na phung po rnams kyi go rims 'di ci'i phyir zhe na /
yathaudārikataḥ ji ltar rags pa'i rim bzhin te /
tatrasarvaudārikaṃ rūpaṃ sapratighatvātpañcavijñānakāyāśrayatvāt ṣaḍvijñānaviṣayatvāt /
ata ādāv audārikaṃ rūpamuktam 		de la gzugs ni thogs pa dang bcas pa dang rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga'i gnas su gyur pa dang rnam par shes pa drug gi yul yin pa'i phyir thams cad pas ches rags te /
de bas na gzugs dang por brjod do /
tribhyaḥ pracāraudārikatayaudārikatarāvedanā /
tathāhy adeśasthām api sañjñādivat pracāraudārikatvād deśaparicchedena tām eva vyapadiśanti na sañjñādīn haste mevedanā śirasi me vedaneti /
ato rūpānantaram uktā /
dvābhyāmaudārikatarāsañjñānimittodgrahaṇātmakatvena sulakṣyatvāt /
vijñānāt saṃskārā audārikatarāḥsaṃskaraṇalakṣaṇatvenasukhāvabodhatvāt 		tshor ba ni gsum po dag pas rgyu ba rags pa'i phyir ches rags pa ste /
'di ltar 'du shes la sogs pa bzhin du yul na mi gnas kyang nga'i lag par tshor ro /
nga'i klad par tshor ro zhes rgyu ba rags pa'i phyir yul yongs su chad pas de nyid la brjod kyi /
'du shes la sogs pa la ni ma yin te /
de'i phyir gzugs kyi 'og tu brjod do /
'du shes ni mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid yin pas rtogs par sla ba'i phyir gnyis po dag pas ches rags so /
'du byed ni 'du byed pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas khong du chud par sla ba'i phyir /
rnam par shes pa las ches rags so /
sarvaśūkṣmatvād vijñānaṃ sarvapaścāduktam rnam par shes pa ni thams cad pas phra ba'i phyir kun gyi tha mar brjod do /
rūpaskandha iti samānādhikaraṇo vā syāt ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣovā de la gzugs kyi phung po zhes bya ba gzhi mthun pa'am /
de'i skyes bu'i phyir zhes bya bar 'gyur grang na /
na bhavet samānādhikaraṇaḥ adravyatvāt skandhasya gzhi mthun pa ni ma yin te /
phung po rdzas su med pa'i phyir ro /
yasmāt skandhaśabdo rāśiparyāyavacanaḥ tasmād rāśivatprajñaptisantaḥ skandhā iti /
tataś ca sāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvaḥ /
ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo 'pi na prāpnoti 		gang gi phyir phung po'i sgra spungs ba'i rnam grangs su gtogs pa'i tshig yin pa de'i phyir phung po rnams ni spungs pa bzhin du btags pa'i yod pa ste /
de'i phyir na gzhi mthun pa nyid med do /
sambandho hi dvayoḥparasparavibhinnarūpayor bhavati devadattamātulavat de'i skyes bu'i phyir yang mi 'gyur te /
phan tshun tha dad pa'i ngo bo nyid yod na 'brel par 'gyur bas /
lha sbyin gyi zhang po zhes bya ba lta bu yin la /
sambandhārthā ceyaṃ ṣaṣṭhī rūpaskandhayor iti rūpād anya eva skandhaḥ prāpnoti /
nacaitad iṣyate prajñaptisataḥsvopādānāt tattvānyatvenāvācyatvāt 		gzugs kyi phung po zhes bya ba'i kyi [?] 'di ni 'brel ba'i don yang yin pas gzugs las phung po gzhan nyid du 'gyur na /
btags pa'i yod pa ni rang gi rten las de nyid dang gzhan du brjod du me dpa'i phyir de'ang mi 'dod do /
naiṣa doṣaḥ 'di ni nyes pa med de /
abhede 'piṣaṣṭhī dṛṣṭā tattvānyatvenāvācye ca pratimāyāḥ śarīramrūpasya prāgabhāva iti /
na hi pratimā śarīrād anyā 		tha dad pa ma yin pa dang de nyid dang gzhan du brjod du med pa la yang drug pa mthong ste /
gzugs su byas pa'i lus dang gzugs kyi snga na med pa zhes bya'o /
gzugs su byas pa ni lus las gzhan ma yin no /
prāgabhāvo'pi nirūpākhyatvāt tattvānyatvenāvācyaḥ svarūpanibandhanatvāt tattvānyatvayoḥ /
anyavastugrahaṇāpekṣaṃ niḥsvabhāvatvād yatra grahaṇameeCe'e AKBh /
bhidhānaṃ ca tad upādānavyatiriktasvabhāvābhāvātprajñaptisat /
tathaiva ca skandhārtha iti prajñaptisann ucyate /
ataś ca tattvānyatvenāvācyatve 'pi svopādānāt ṣaṣṭhī navirudhyate /
tataś ca ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣa evātra /
rūpaṃ katamat 		snga na med pa yang dngos po med pa'i phyir gzugs las de nyid dang gzhan du brjod du med de de nyid dang gzhan yin pa gnyis kyi rgyu ni rang gi ngo bo yin pa'i phyir ro /
rang bzhin med pa'i phyir dngos po gzhan 'dzin pa la ltos pa ste /
gang zhig gang la 'dzin pa dang brjod pa 'jug pa de ni rten dang tha dad pa'i rang bzhin med pas btags pa'i yod pa nyid de /
don du ma yin pas btags pa'i yod pa nyid ces bya'o /
de'i phyir rang gi rten las de nyid dang gzhan du brjod du med kyang kyir 'gal ba med do /
de'i phyir 'dir de'i skyes bu'i kyi [?] nyid do /
gzugs gang zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānicatvāri ca mahābhūtāny upādāya /
nanu caskandhānāṃ prakṛtatvāt katamad rūpam ity asambaddhaḥpraśnaḥ /
nāsambaddhaḥ skandhānāṃ niḥsvabhāvatvāttatsvabhāvavyapadeśena nirdhāraṇam aśakyam kiṃ tarhitadupādānanirdhāraṇenaiveti /
ato rūpaṃ katamad iti praśnaḥna rūpaskandha iti /
rūpasya kāryakāraṇabhāvena bhedapradarśanārtham āha catvāri mahābhūtānītyādi 		'byung ba chen po bzhi dag dang 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa'o zhes bya ba la phung po smos pa'i skabs su gzugs gang zhe na zhes bya ba'i 'dri ba 'di 'brel ba med do zhe na /
'brel ba med pa ma yin te /
phung po rnams ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir /
de'i ngo bo nyid brjod pas ni dmigs kyis dbye bar mi nus kyi /
'on kyang de'i rten dmigs kyis phye bas 'gyur te /
de'i phyir gzugs gang zhe na zhes 'dri'i /
gzugs kyi phung po ni ma yin no /
rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos por gzugs kyi dbye ba bstan pa'i phyir /
tathā hi sarvāṇimahābhūtāni sarvasyopādāyarūpasya kāraṇam sarvaṃ copādāyarūpaṃ sarveṣāṃ mahābhūtānāṃ kāryam 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te /
'di ltar 'byung ba chen po bzhi po thams cad ni rgyur byas pa'i gzugs thams cad kyi rgyu yin la /
rgyur byas pa'i gzugs thams cad ni 'byung ba chen po thams cad kyi 'bras bu yin no /
mahattvaṃbhūtānāṃ sarvopādāyarūpāśrayatvenaudārikatvāt 'byung ba rnams kyi chen po ni rgyur byas pa'i gzugs thams cad kyi rten yin pas gtos che ba'i phyir ro /
athavāsarvarūpādisamudāyeṣu kāṭhinyādisadbhāvān mahāsanniveśatvādmahattvam /
bhūtatvaṃ tu punar eṣāṃ vividhopādāyarūpanirvṛttau tais taiḥ prakārair bhavantīti bhūtāni 		yang na gzugs la sogs pa 'dus pa thams cad la srab la sogs pa yod pa'i phyir ram /
gnas pa tha gru che ba'i phyir chen po'o /
de dag gi 'byung ba ni rgyur byas pa'i gzugs sna tshogs 'grub pa na de dang de dag gi rnam par 'byung bas 'byung ba rnams so /
sarvasattvakarmādhipatyādvānādau saṃsāre na kadācin nābhūvanniti bhūtāni /
na cānyeṣāṃ bhūtatvaprasaṅgo mahiṣādivad rūḍhiśabdatvāt 		yang na sems can thams cad kyi las kyi dbang gis thog ma med pa'i 'khor ba nas nam yang ma byung ba ma myong bas 'byung ba rnams so /
gzhan dag la yang 'byung ba nyid thal bar mi 'gyur te /
ming grags pa yin pas sa steng nyal la sogs pa bzhin no /
tāni punaś catvāry eva na nyūnādhikāni asāmarthyāpārthakatvaprasaṅgāt /
bhautikasya hy avadhṛtisnehapācanavyūhanamātrakam eva kāryam 		de dag ni bzhi kho na ste /
mi nus pa dang mi dgos pa nyid du thal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir mang ba'am nyung ba ma yin no /
'byung ba'i bya ba ni brten pa dang sdud pa dang smin par byed pa dang skyod par byed pa tsam du zad de /
tasya caitāvadbhir eva parisamāptatvādanyasya ca karaṇīyasyābhāvāt catvāry eva bhūtāni de dag nyid kyis de'i bya ba yongs su rdzogs pa dang bya ba gzhan med pa'i phyir 'byung ba dag ni bzhi kho na'o /
nanu cadhṛtyādivad avakāśam apy upādāyarūpasya kāryam brten pa la sogs pa bzhin du nam mkha'i bya ba ni go 'byed pa yin te /
taccākāśena kriyata iti pṛthivyādivad ākāśasyāpimahābhūtatvaprasaṅgaḥ /
naitad evam /
kiṃ kāraṇam /
na hy ākāśaṃ nāma kiñcid asty anyatra sapratigharūpābhāvamātrāt /
avakāśaṃ ca sapratigham eva vastu svasminn avakāśesapratighasyaiva tasmād apasaraṃ dadāti nākāśam /
na hitasmāt pradeśād rūpavad ākāśam apasṛtam ititasyāvakāśadānaṃ na yujyate 		de yang nam mkhas byed pas na sa la sogs ba bzhin du nam mkha' yang 'byung ba chen po nyid du thal bar 'gyur ram /
de ni de ltar mi 'gyur te /
ci'i phyir zhe na /
thogs pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs med pa tsam ma gtogs par nam mkha' zhes bya ba ci yang med do /
thogs pa dang bcas pa'i rang gi ngo bo nyid de nas song ste /
rang gi go der thogs pa dang bcas pa la go 'byed par zad kyi nam mkhas ni ma yin te /
gzugs ltar nam mkha' phyogs de nas song ba med pas de go 'byed ces byar mi rung ngo /
sapratighaṃ ca rūpaṃ svadeśe 'nyarūpasyotpattiṃ pratibadhnāti /
nākāśam /
tasmād yatra yasyayasmin saty avakāśābhāvaḥ yasminn asati tasya tatrāvakāśa iti tenaiva tasmāt sthānād apasaratā tasyāvakāśo dattaḥnākāśeneti 		thogs pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs ni rang gi phyogs su gzugs gzhan 'byung ba'i bgegs byed kyi nam mkha' ni ma yin no /
de lta bas na 'dir gang na gang yod na ni go phye ba med la /
de na de med na ni der go phye ba yod pas de'i phyir de nyid gnas de nas song nas go phye ba yin gyi nam mkha' ni ma yin no /
tasmān nākāśaṃ pṛthivyādivan mahābhūtam de bas na nam mkha' ni sa la sogs pa ltar 'byung ba chen po ma yin no /
catvāri ca mahābhūtāny upādāyeti catvāri ca mahābhūtānirūpaṃ catvāri ca mahābhūtāny upādāya rūpam iti ubhayatrāpicaśabdaḥ sambadhyate 'byung ba bzhi dag rgyur byas pa zhes bya ba ni 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag gi gzugs dang 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa'i gzugs zhes bya ba'i sgra gnyi gar yang sbyar ro /
pañcaprakāreṇajanananiśrayapratiṣṭhopastambhabṛṃhaṇānāṃ hetubhāvenabhautikaṃbhūtāny upādatta ity upādāyaśabdo hetvarthaḥ tadyathendhanam upādāyāgnir bhavatīti tena nimitteneti gamyate skyed pa dang brten pa dang gnas pa dang ston pa dang 'phel bar byed pa rnams kyi rgyu'i dngos po rnam pa lngas 'byung ba rnams kyis 'byung ba las gyur pa gzung ngo /
rgyur byas pa'i sgra ni rgyu'i don te /
dper na shing rgyur byas nas me byung ngo zhes byas na rgyu de las byung bar shes pa lta bu'o /
tatrajananahetutvaṃ tair vinā tadanutpatteḥ /
niśrayahetutvaṃbhūtavikāre tatpratiṣṭhitopādāyarūpavikṛtyanuvidhānāt 		de la skyed pa'i rgyu ni de dag de med par de mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
rten gyi rgyu ni 'byung ba 'gyur na de la brten pa rgyur byas pa'i gzugs kyang rjes su 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
sthānahetutvaṃ bhūtānāṃ sadṛśasantānotpattau bhautikasyāpisadṛśasantānānucchedahetutvāt /
upastambhahetutvaṃtadvaśenānucchedāt 		gnas pa'i rgyu ni 'byung ba rnams rgyun 'dra bar 'byung ba ni 'byung ba las gyur pa yang 'dra ba'i rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir ro /
rton pa'i rgyu ni de'i stobs kyis rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir ro /
bṛṃhaṇahetutvaṃ bhūtavṛddhautadāśritopādāyarūpavṛddheḥ 'phel bar byed pa'i rgyu ni 'byung ba 'phel na de la rten pa rgyur byas pa'i gzugs kyang 'phel ba'i phyir ro /
pṛthivīdhātur ityādivyākaraṇaṃsvalakṣaṇopādāyarūpadhāraṇātpṛthivyādaya eva dhātavaḥ /
pṛthivyādigrahaṇaṃcakṣurdhātvādibhyaḥ parasparataś ca vyavacchedārtham 		sa'i khams zhes bya ba la sogs pa bshad pa la rang gi mtshan nyid dang rgyur byas pa'i gzugs 'dzin pa'i phyir sa la sogs pa nyid khams so /
sa la sogs pa smos pa ni phan tshun dang mig gi khams la sogs pa dag las rnam par dbye ba'i phyir ro /
dhātugrahaṇaṃ laukikebhyaḥ pṛthivyādibhyo viśeṣaṇārtham khams smos pa ni 'jig rten pa'i sa la sogs pa las bye brag tu bya ba'i phyir ro /
pṛthivyādayo hi laukikaśāstraprasiddhibhedena dvidheṣyante sal sogs pa ni 'jig rten pa dang bstan bcos las grags pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa gnyis su 'gyur te /
tatralaukikā varṇasaṃsthānātmakatvātsāṃvyavahārikā iti nadhātavaḥ de la 'jig rten pa'i ni kha dog dang dbyibs kyi bdag nyid du kun du tha snyad 'dogs pa yin pa'i phyir khams ma yin no /
śāstrīyāḥ punaḥ khakkhaṭādisvabhāvasadbhāvātpāramārthikatvād dhātavaḥ bstan bcos las byung ba rnams la ni sra bal sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid yod pa'i phyir yang dag par na khams yin no /
bhūtavat pṛthivīdhātvādayo 'pisvarūpanirdeśam antareṇa na vijñāyanta iti punar api praśnaḥ pṛthivīdhātuḥ katamaityādi /
khakkhaṭatvam /
iti bhāvapratyayo 'tra svārthikaḥ /
khakkhaṭam eva khakkhaṭatvam na hy atra bhāvāntaram asti /
khakkhaṭaḥ kharaḥ krūra itiparyāyāḥ 		'byung ba bzhin du sa'i khams la sogs pa'i rang gi ngo bo nyid kyang ma bshad par mi shes pas yang sa'i khams gang zhe na zhes bya ba la sogs pa dris so /
sra pa nyid do zhes bya ba la nyid ni sra ba kho na sra ba nyid de 'di la don gzhan ni med do /
sra ba dang mkhrang ba dang 'thas pa ni rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o /
sneho 'bdhāturiti saṃśrayātmakatvād drava /
tvād vā snehaḥ 		chu'i khams gang zhe na /
gsher ba nyid do zhes bya ba ni 'du bar byed pa'i bdag nyid yin pa dang rlan par byed pas gsher ba'o /
dāhakatvādūṣmā tejodhātuḥ /
vāyu /
dhātur laghusamudīraṇatvamiti /
laghutvaṃ vāyudhātur ity ucyamānaupādāyarūpasyāpi bhūtatvaṃ prasajyeta /
īraṇaṃ vāyudhātur ity ucyamāne karmaivāsya nirdiṣṭaṃ syān na svarūpam ity ato 'sya laghutvād upādāyarūpāt karmaṇaś cavyavacchedārtham evam uktaṃ laghusamudīraṇatvaṃ vāyudhātur iti /
samudīraṇatvaṃ punar bhāvasrotaso nairantaryeṇadeśāntarotpattihetutvam /
ete ca pṛthivyaptejovāyudhātavaupādāyarūpeṇeva parasparato 'py avinirbhāgavartina iti kathaṃvijñāyate /
karmataḥ 		me'i khams ni sreg par byed pa yin pas tsha ba'o /
rlung gi khams ni yang zhing gyo ba nyid do zhes bya ba la yang ba nyid rlung gi khams yin no zhes brjod na ni rgyur byas pa'i gzugs la yang 'byung ba nyid thal bar 'gyur ro /
rlung gi khams gyo ba'o zhes brjod pa ni de'i las nyid bstan par 'gyur gyi /
rang gi ngo bo ni ma yin te /
de'i phyir de yang ba rgyur byas pa'i gzugs dang las rnam par gcod pa'i phyir rlung gi khams ni yang zhing gyo ba'o zhes de skad ces brjod do /
g yo ba ni dngos po'i rgyun yul gzhan du 'byung bar byed pa'i rgyu yin no /
sa dang chu dang me dang rlung gi khams de dag dang rgyur byas pa'i gzugs phan tshun tha dad du mi 'jug par ci mngon zhe na /
ata eva caiṣāṃ dhṛtisaṅgrahapaktivyūhanāni kāritram uktam /
kathaṃ nāmaiṣāṃ svarūpato 'nupalabhyamānānām api upalādiṣu kāryataḥ sattvam anumīyeteti 		las las mngon te /
de'i phyir de dag gi las ni brten pa dang sdud pa dang smin par byed pa dang skyod par byed pa brjod do /
de dag gi rang gi ngo bo mi dmigs kyang rdo la sogs pa la yod par las las ji ltar rjes su dpag ce na /
tathā hy upalādiṣu saṅgrahapaktivyūhanebhyo jalānalānilānāṃpṛthivīdhātunā sāhacaryaṃ vijñāyate 'di ltar rdo la sogs pa la 'dus pa dang skam pa dang gyo ba rnams yod pa las chu dang me dang rlung rnams sa'i khams dang lhan cig 'jug par mngon no /
apsu kāṣṭhasandhāraṇapatradalapākoṣṇatāvacalanebhyaḥ kṣityanalānilānāmabdhātunā /
agnau jvālādīnāṃ sthairyasampiṇḍitapreraṇebhyaḥkṣitijalānilānāṃ tejasā 		tshul yang shing 'degs pa dang padma'i 'dab ma rgyas pa dang chu gyo ba rnams yod pa las sa dang me dang rlung rnams chu'i khams dang lhan cig rgyu bar mngon no /
me la yang me lces 'degs pa dang 'dus pa dang gyo ba rnams yod pa las sa dang chu dang rlung rnams me dang lhan cig 'jug par mngon no /
vāyau sandhāraṇavastrādiśoṣaṇāvisārebhyaḥ kṣityudakānalānāṃ vāyudhātunā sāhacaryaṃvijñāyate rlung la yang 'degs pa dang mi 'gyes pa dang gos la sogs bskam bar byed pa yod pa las /
sa dang chu dang me rnams rlung gi khams dang lhan cig 'jug par mngon no /
karmaṇaḥ svabhāvasya ca ko viśeṣaḥ las dang rang gi ngo bo gnyis bye brag ci yod ce na /
kriyamāṇāpekṣaṃ karmavyavasthāpyate /
tathā hy ādhāryadravyasandhāraṇāpekṣayāpṛthivīdhātor dhṛtiḥ karmocyate 		bya ba la ltos nas las rnam par gzhag ste /
'di ltar brten par bya ba'i rdzas brten pa la ltos nas sa'i khams kyi las ni brten pa zhes bya'o /
bsdu bar bya ba la ltos nas chu'i las ni sdud pa'o /
smin par bya ba la ltos nas /
saṅgrāhyāpekṣayāpāṃsaṅgrahaḥ karma pākāpekṣayā tejasaḥ paktiḥ karmavardhanīyakalalāṅkurāpekṣayā vyūhanaṃ vāyoḥ karma /
vyūhanaṃ punar vṛddhiḥ prasarpaṇaṃ ca 		me'i las ni smin par byed pa'o /
'phel bar bya ba nur nur po dang myu gu la sogs pa la ltos nas rlung gi las ni skyod par byed pa'o /
bskyod pa ni 'phel bar byed pa dang 'gyur bar byed pa'o /
svabhāvas tusarvānyabhāvanirapekṣa ity ayaṃ karmaṇaḥ svabhāvasya caviśeṣaḥ /
uktāni bhūtāni sāmānyaviśeṣasañjñābhiḥ svabhāvataśca 		ngo bo nyid ni dngos po gzhan thams cad la mi ltos pa ste /
'di ni las dang ngo bo nyid kyi bye brag go /
'byung ba rnams kyi spyi dang khyad par gyi ming dang rang bzhin bshad zin to /
bhūtānantaroddiṣṭam upādāyarūpaṃ prabhedataḥ svarūpataś ca na vijñāyata ity ataḥ pṛcchati upādāyarūpaṃ kata 'byung ba rnams kyi 'og tu bstan pa rgyur byas pa'i gzugs kyi rab tu dbye ba dang rang gi ngo bo mi shes te /
de'i phyir rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gang zhe na zhes dris te /
maditi /
katiprakāraṃ kiṃsvarūpaṃ cety arthaḥ /
cakṣurindriyaṃ kiṃsvabhāvam 		rnam pa ni du zhig rang gi ngo bo ni ci 'dra zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
mig gi dbang po'i rang gi ngo bo ci 'dra zhe na /
varṇaviṣayo /
rūpaprasādaiti tatsvabhāvāviṣkaraṇam /
catvāri mahābhūtāny upādāyeti prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate 		yul kha dog gzugs dang ba'o zhes bya bas rang gi ngo bor ston te /
skabs yin pas 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
varṇo nīlapītādikaś catuḥprakāraḥ /
varṇālocanād varṇanirbhāsāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvād vā varṇo viṣayo 'syeti varṇaviṣayaḥ /
ayaṃcātra prasādārthaḥ tadyathā prasanna ādarśa udakapātre vābimbaṃ pratītya tatpratibhāsaṃ pratibimbam utpadyate tadvatpañcasu rūpaprasādātmakeṣu cakṣurādiṣu rūpagandhādīn pratītya tatpratibhāsā vijñaptaya utpadyante 		kha dog ni sngon po dang ser po la sogs pa rnam pa bzhi'o /
kha dog la lta ba dang kha dog tu snang ba'i rnam par shes pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir kha dog ni de'i yul yin pas yul kha dog ces bya'o /
'di ni 'dir dang ba'i don te /
dper na gzugs la brten nas de ltar snang ba'i gzugs brnyan me long ngam /
snod kyi chu dang ba'i nang du 'byung ba de bzhin du gzugs dang sgra la sogs pa la brten nas /
de ltar snang ba'i rnam par rig pa mig la sogs pa gzugs dang ba'i bdag nyid lnga po dag las 'byung ngo /
atra cakṣurādīnāṃparasparato viṣayarūpātmakāt prasādān manastaḥ śraddhātaś ca vyavacchedaḥ kāryaḥ /
rūpaprasādātmakatvāviśeṣādvarṇaviṣayatvāviśeṣāc ca ubhayam ucyate varṇaviṣayorūpaprasāda iti ca /
tatra varṇaviṣayatvena śrotrādibhyoviṣayaprasādāc ca vyavacchinatti 		'dir ni mig la sogs pa phan tshun dang yul gzugs kyi bdag nyid dang ba dang yid dang dad pa las rnam par dbye bar bya ste /
gzugs dang ba'i bdag nyid du bye brag med pa dang yul kha dog yin par bye brag med pa'i phyir yul kha dog gzugs dang ba'o zhes gnyis ka brjod do /
de la yul kha dog ces bya bas ni rna ba la sogs pa dang yul gyi gzugs dang ba las rnam par 'byed de /
na hi śrotrādayoviṣayaprasādo vā varṇaviṣayo 'sti rna ba la sogs pa dang yul ni dang ba yin yang kha dog yul ma yin no /
rūpaprasādātmakatvenamanasto vyavacchinatti gzugs dang ba'i bdag nyid kyis ni yid las rnam par 'byed de /
tad dhi saty api varṇaviṣayatve narūpaprasādātmakam /
rūpagrahaṇaṃ śraddhātmakāt prasādādvyavacchedakam /
śraddhāpi hi prasādātmikā rūpādiviṣayā cetyato rūpagrahaṇam /
varṇaviṣayaḥ prasādaś cakṣurindriyam ityucyamāne śraddhāyā api prasaṅga ity ato rūpagrahaṇaṃkriyata iti śraddhāyā arūpātmakatvāt /
cakṣurādīni hiindantītīndriyāṇi /
īśanta ity arthaḥ ādhipatyam asmin saṅghātekurvantīty arthaḥ /
ataś cādhipatyārtha indriyārthaḥindantītīndriyāṇi /
evam indrāṇīti prāpnoti /
nipātanād indriyamiha bhaviṣyati /
evam api dhātvartho vaktavyaḥ /
sa ca nokta ityayaṃ parihāraḥ /
vijñānavad eva kṛt syāt /
tadyathā vijānātītivijñānam iti prāpte lyuḍartham anādṛtya vijñānam uktaṃtadvyatiriktavijñātṛsaṅgrahavyudāsārtham evamihāpīndriyavyatiriktaliṅgakalpanāvyudāsārtham evam uktaṃsyād iti /
yathaiva hi cakṣurādīnāṃ viṣayiṇāṃ parasparatoviṣayabhedena bheda uktaḥ cakṣurindriyaṃ katamat /
varṇaviṣayo rūpaprasādaḥ /
śrotrendriyaṃ katamat /
śabdaviṣayo rūpaprasāda ity evamādi evaṃ rūpādīnām api viṣayāṇāṃ cakṣurādibhir viṣayibhir bhedaucyate /
cakṣuṣa eva viṣayo rūpam na śrotrādīnāmtadviṣayāṇāṃ śabdāditvena vyavasthānāt /
atra ca manaso navidhir na pratiṣedho 'prakṛtatvāt /
evaṃ ca rūpādīnāṃparasparato bheda ukto bhavati cakṣuṣo viṣayo rūpam eva nārūpam iti /
evam api nīlapītādīnāṃ parasparavilakṣaṇānāṃcakṣurindriyaviṣayāṇāṃ rūpatvenābheda ukto bhavatīti /
yadi cakṣurviṣayatvena rūpaṃ viśeṣitam eveti evaṃ sati varṇasaṃsthānaṃ vijñaptiś ceti kimartham /
rūpaprabhedasandarśanārtham 		de'i yul kha dog yin yang gzugs dang ba'i bdag nyid ni ma yin no /
gzugs smos pas ni dad pa dang ba'i bdag nyid las rnam par 'byed de /
dad pa ni dang ba'i bdag nyid kyang yin la yul kha dog kyang yin te /
de'i phyir gzugs smos so /
mig gi dbang po ni dang ba yul kha dog go zhes brjod na dad pa la yang thal bar 'gyur bas de'i phyir gzugs smos te /
dad pa ni gzugs kyi bdag nyid ma yin pa'i phyir /
mig la sogs pa ni dbang byed pa'i phyir dbang po rnams te /
tshogs pa 'di la bdag po byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
de bas na bdag po'i don ni dbang po'i don te /
ji ltar mig la sogs pa yul can rnams phan tshun yul tha dad pas tha dad par brjod de /
mig gi dbang po gang zhe na /
yul kha dog gzugs dang ba'o /
rna ba'i dbang po gang zhe na /
yul sgra gzugs dang ba'o zhes bya ba la sogs pas tha dad par brjod pa de bzhin du gzugs la sogs pa yul rnams kyang mig la sogs pa yul can rnams tha dad pas tha dad par brjod de /
gzugs ni mig nyid kyi yul yin te /
rna ba la sogs pa'i ma yin te /
de dag gi yul rnams ni sgra la sogs par rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir ro /
'dir yid ni skabs ma yin pa'i phyir sgrub pa yang med /
dgag pa yang med do /
de ltar na gzugs la sogs pa phan tshun tha dad par brjod pa yin no /
mig gi yul ni gzugs nyid yin gyi /
gzugs ma yin pa ni ma yin te de ltar na mig gi dbang po'i yul sngon po dang ser po la sogs pa phan tshun mi 'dra ba rnams kyang gzugs su tha dad pa med par bstan pa yin no /
gal te gzugs mig gi yul nyid kyis bye brag tu byas pa yin na kha dog dang dbyibs dang rnam par rig byed do zhes bya ba ci'i phyir smos she na /
rūpaprabhedeṣu hi sandigdhaviparyastāvyutpannānāṃ bhedapradarśanenasandehaviparyāsāvyutpattayo nirākriyante gzugs rab tu dbye ba la the tshom za ba dang nor ba dang mi rtogs pa rnams la rab tu dbye ba bstan na the tshom za ba dang nor ba dang mi rtogs pa sel bar 'gyur ro /
varṇaścatuḥprakāraḥ /
nīlaḥ pīto lohito 'vadātaśca 		kha dog ni rnam ba bzhi ste /
sngon po dang ser po dang dmar po dang dkar po'o /
abhraṃ dhūmorajo mahikā cchāyātapa āloko 'ndhakāramabhyavakāśaṃnabhaśceti te 'pi kasmād atra noktāḥ sprin dang du ba dang rdul dang khug rna dang grib ma dang nyi ma dang snang ba dang mun pa dang mngon par skabs yod pa dang nam mkha' zhes bya ba 'di rnams 'dir ci'i phyir ma smos she na /
varṇasaṃsthānavadrūpabhedatvena noktāḥ kha dog dang dbyibs bzhin du gzugs kyi bye brag tu 'dir ma smos te /
abhrādayo hi paricchinnadeśāaparicchinnadeśāś ca sprin la sogs pa ni yul yongs su chad pa dang yul yongs su mchad pa'o /
tatra ye paricchinnadeśās te saṃsthānaevāntarbhūtāḥ de la gang dag yongs su chad pa de dag ni dbyibs kyi nang du 'dus pa nyid de /
ye 'paricchinnadeśās te varṇaviśeṣā eveti gang dag yul yongs su chad pa de dag ni kha dog gi bye brag yin pas /
navarṇasaṃsthānābhyāṃ pṛthag vyavasthāpayituṃ śakyanta itīhapṛthag noktāḥ kha dog dang dbyibs gnyis las tha dad par rnam par gzhag mi nus te /
de'i phyir 'dir logs shig tu ma smos so /
tatrābhyavakāśastadanyapratighātakartṛspraṣṭavyavirahito yaḥ pradeśaḥ de la mngon par skabs yod pa ni de las gzhan pa thogs par byed pa'i rig bya dang bral ba'i phyogs gang yin pa'o /
nabhoyad upariṣṭān nīlam upalabhyate nam mkha' ni steng na sngon por snang ba gang yin pa'o /
saṃsthānaṃdīrghaṃ hrasvaṃ vṛttaṃ parimaṇḍalam unnatamavanataṃ sātaṃ visātamiti /
kiṃ punar idaṃ saṃsthānaṃnāma 		dbyibs ni ring po dang thung du dang lham pa dang zlum po dang mtho ba dang dma' ba dang phya le ba dang phe le ba ma yin pa'o /
dbyigs zhes bya ba 'di ci zhig /
nanūktaṃ dīrghādir iti ring po zhes bya ba la sogs pa ma smras sam /
tad etad eva na jñāyate /
yatradīrghādibuddhayo bhavanti tad dīrghādisaṃsthānam 		de nyid mi shes so zhe na gang la ring po la sogs pa'i blo 'byung ba de ring po la sogs pa'i dbyibs so /
evaṃtarhi na varṇādivyatiriktaṃ saṃsthānaṃ vidyate /
kiṃ kāraṇam 		de ltar na'o na kha dog la sogs pa las gud na dbyibs med par 'gyur ro /
ci'i phyir zhe na /
yasmādekadiṅmukhapravṛtte bhūyasi varṇādisaṅghātedīrghabuddhir bhavati alpīyasi hrasvabuddhiḥ caturdiśaṃsame vṛttabuddhiḥ sarvataḥ same parimaṇḍalabuddhiḥekadiṅmukhe sātabuddhiḥ nānādiṅmukhe visātabuddhir iti 'di ltar kha dog la sogs pa 'dus pa mang po phyogs gcig na gnas pa la ring po'i blo 'byung /
chung ngu la ni thung du'i blo 'byung /
phyogs bzhir mnyam pa la ni lham pa'i blo 'byung /
kun nas mnyam pa la ni zlum po'i blo 'byung /
dbus su phal che ba la ni mtho ba'i blo 'byung /
nyung ba la ni dma' ba'i blo 'byung /
phyogs gcig gi ngos la ni phya le ba'i blo 'byung /
phyogs tha dad pa'i ngos la ni phya le ba ma yin pa'i blo 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ punar etad gamyate varṇādisamudāye dīrghabuddhirbhavati na punar arthāntarabhūte saṃsthāna iti /
sparśanadvāreṇāpi dīrghādibuddhyutpatteḥ nacendriyāntaraviṣaya indriyāntaradvāreṇa buddhir utpadyate naikendriyavaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt /
naiva tad indriyajñānam kiṃ tarhy anumānajñānamgandhāt puṣpavarṇajñānavat 		kha dog la sogs pa 'dus pa la ring po la sogs pa'i blo 'byung bar zad kyi /
dbyibs don gzhan du gyur pa med par de ji ltar shes she na /
reg pa'i sgo nas kyang ring po la sogs pa'i blo 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
dbang po gzhan gyi yul la gzhan gyi sgo nas blo 'byung du mi rung ste /
dbang po du ma don med par thal bar 'gyur ro /
de ni dbang po'i shes pa ma yin gyi /
rjes su dpag pa'i shes pa ste /
dri las me tog gi kha dog shes pa bzhin no /
yathāgandhaḥ puṣpavarṇaniyataḥ na tv evaṃ sparśaḥ saṃsthāna iti viṣamo 'yam upanyāsaḥ dri me tog gi kha dog la nges pa ltar reg pa ni dbyibs la de ltar ma yin te /
bzhag pa 'di ni mthun pa ma yin no /
tasmād ubhayendriyadvāreṇa ghaṭādivad dīrghādisaṃsthānapravṛtteḥ na tad varṇādibhyo'rthāntaram iti de lta bas na dbang po gnyis kyi sgo nas bum pa la sogs pa bzhin du /
ring po la sogs pa'i dbyibs la shes pa 'jug pa'i phyir de kha dog la sogs pa las don gzhan ma yin no /
na ca niravayavatvāt paramāṇūnāṃ dīrghādirūpeṇa parasparato bhedo yuktaḥ /
tasmān nanīlādiparamāṇuvad dīrghādiparamāṇavaḥ santīty ataś casaṃsthānaparamāṇusamudāyo 'pi dīrghādisaṃsthānam ityayuktam dīrghādisaṃsthānaparamāṇvabhāvāt 		rdul phra rab rnams ni cha shas med pa'i phyir ring po la sogs pa'i ngo bor nang phan tshun tha dad par yang mi rigs so; /
de lta bas na sngon po la sogs pa'i rdul phra rab ltar ring po la sogs pa'i rdul phra rab rnams yod pa ma yin no /
de'i phyir dbyibs kyi rdul phra rab rnams 'dus pa la ring po la sogs pa'i dbyibs shes byar yang mi rung ste /
dbyibs kyi rdul phra rab med pa'i phyir ro /
na casaṃsthānātmakaṃ dravyamarvāṅmadhyaparabhāgasambhavāt /
na ca teṣām abhedaḥyugapat pratyakṣāpratyakṣatvāt /
sambandhibhedāc catasyāvaśyaṃ bhedena bhavitavyam abhede vātatsambandhīnām apy abhinnatvaprasaṅga iti 		dbyibs ni rdzas gcig pa ma yin te /
tshu rol dang dbus dang pha rol gyi cha yod pa'i phyir ro /
de dag tha dad pa med pa ma yin te /
cig car du mngon sum dang mngon sum du ma gyur pa dang 'brel pa can tha dad pa'i phyir de dag gdon mi za bar tha dad par 'gyur ro /
ci ste tha mi dad na yang de dang 'brel pa can rnams kyang phyogs tha dad pa med par thal bar 'gyur ro /
tasmān nāsty evadravyataḥ saṃsthānamkiṃ tarhi varṇādiṣv eva tathā tathāvyavasthiteṣu dīrghādi prajñapyate de lta bas na dbyibs ni rdzas su yod pa ma yin te /
'on kyang kha dog la sogs pa de lta de ltar gnas pa rnams la ring po la sogs par 'dogs so /
atha vijñaptir nāma ka eṣa dharmaḥ 'o na rnam par rig byed ces bya ba'i chos 'di gang zhig yin /
tadālambanacittajaṃkāyamahābhūtāśrayeṇotpannaṃkāyasya saṃsthānaṃsvasamutthāpakacittavijñapanād vijñaptir ity ucyate de la dmigs pa'i sems las skye ba lus kyi 'byung ba chen po la brten nas 'byung ba lus kyi dbyibs te /
rang kun nas slong ba'i sems rnam par rig par byed pas rnam par rig byed ces bya ba'o /
atra ca tadālambanād eva yaj jāyate cittāt saṃsthānam tad evavijñaptiḥ na punar anyālambanāt 'dir ni de la dmigs pa'i sems las skyes pa gang yin pa de nyid rnam par rig byed de /
gzhan la dmigs pa las ni ma yin no /
evaṃ ca punarbruvata oṣṭhādisaṃsthānam atadālambanacittajatvān nirākṛtam pūrvapraṇidhānajaṃca de ltar na smra ba'i mchu la sogs pa'i dbyibs ni de la dmigs pa'i sems las skyes pa ma yin pa dang smon lam las skyes pa yang bkag pa yin no /
tad dhi praṇidhānacittādanyavipākahetucittajam apīti na vijñaptir iṣyate de ni smon lam gyi sems dang gzhan rnam par smin pa'i rgyu'i sems las kyang skyes pa yin te /
de'i phyir rnam par rig byed du mi 'dod do /
tatra yadi vijñaptyākhyaṃsaṃsthānam ekaṃ kāyākhyasamudāyavyāpi tad ekatvād vyāpitvāc ca pratyavayavaṃ gṛhyatesarvasmiṃstadbhāvāt /
na vā tad ekam bhāgato vyavasthānāt 		de la gal te rnam par rig byed ces bya ba'i dbyibs gcig pus lus kyi spyir khyab pa yin na ni gcig yin pa'i phyir dang khyab pa yin pa'i phyir te thams cad na yod pas yan lag so so la yang gzung bar 'gyur ro /
yang na cha shas su rnam par gnas pa'i phyir gcig tu mi rung ngo /
daśa cāyatanāni paramāṇusañcitānīti siddhānto bādhyeta skye mched bcu ni rdul phra rab bsags pa'o zhes 'byung ba'i grub pa'i mtha' la'ang gnod par 'gyur ro /
tasmān nāsti saṃsthānaṃ nāma dravyāntaram /
ataś ca na saṃsthānaṃvijñaptiḥ 		de lta bas na dbyibs zhes bya ba rdzas gzhan du gyur pa med de /
de'i phyir dbyibs ni rnam par rig byed ma yin no /
yadi kāyād arthāntaram na saṃsthānam kā tarhi sā gal te lus las don gzhan du gyur pa'i dbyibs rnam par rig byed ma yin na'o na de gang yin /
tadālambanacetanānimittā kāyasantater nairantaryeṇa deśāntarotpattiḥ /
cetanānimittatvaṃ tu kāyasantater deśāntarotpattihetuvāyudhātunirvartanāt 		de la dmigs pa'i sems pa'i rgyu mtshan can lus kyi rgyud rgyun ma chad par yul gzhan du 'byung ba'i rgyu yin no /
sems pa rgyur gyur pa ni lus kyi rgyud yul gzhan du 'byung ba'i rgyu rlung gi khams bsgrub pa'i phyir ro /
sāca kāyasya deśāntarotpattiḥ svanimittaṃ cetanāṃ vijñāpayatīti vijñaptiḥ /
tasyās tu kuśalākuśalatvaṃ na svābhāvikam 		lus yul gzhan du 'byung ba de ni rang gi rgyu sems pa rnam par rig par byed pa'i phyir rnam par rig byed do /
de ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'i ngo bo nyid ma yin te /
kiṃ tarhikuśalākuśalacetanāpravartitatvāt kuśalākuśalatvam upacaryatekārye kāraṇopacārāt 'on kyang de dge ba dang mi dge ba'i sems pas skyed pa'i phyir 'bras bu la rgyu btags te /
dge ba dang mi dge ba nyid du 'dogs so; /
atra tu rūpavyavasthānaṃ svabhāvataḥsanniveśataḥ kriyālakṣaṇataś ca 'dir gzugs rnam par gzhag pa ni ngo bo nyid dang gnas pa dang byed pa'i mtshan nyid kyis rnam par gzhag ste /
svabhāvato nīlādīnāṃcaturṇāṃ varṇānām tatsvabhāvatvāt ngo bo nyid ni sngon po la sogs pa kha dog bzhi po rnams te /
de'i ngo bo yin pa'i phyir ro /
sanniveśato daśānāṃdīrghādisaṃsthānānām tathā tathā varṇasanniveśāt gnas pa ni ring po la sogs pa dbyibs rnam pa brgyad de /
kha dog de lta de ltar gnas pa'i phyir ro /
kriyālakṣaṇato vijñapteḥ kāyapraspandātmakatvāt byed pa'i mtshan nyid ni rnam par rig byed de /
lus gyo ba'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
dravyasadviṣayatvāc cakṣurādīnām saṃsthānasya vijñapteś caprajñaptisattvāt na cakṣuṣo viṣayatvam asti rdzas su yod pa ni mig la sogs pa'i yul yin la /
dbyibs dang rnam par rig byed ni /
btags pa yod pa'i phyir mig gi yul ma yin pa snyam na ji ltar gzugs mig gi yul zhes brjod /
kathaṃcakṣurviṣayatvena rūpam ucyate /
atra hi lokānuvṛttyā varṇaḥsaṃsthānaviśeṣaṇaś cakṣurviṣayatvena vivakṣitaḥ 		'dir 'jig rten dang mthun par bya ba'i phyir dbyibs kyi khyad par dang bcas pa'i kha dog mig gi yul du 'dod de /
tathā hisaṃsthānaviśiṣṭaś cakṣuṣā varṇo gṛhyate na kevalaṃsaṃsthānaṃ varṇo vādīrghādisaṃsthānaviśiṣṭavarṇanirbhāsacakṣurvijñānotpatteḥ 'di ltar dbyibs kyi khyad par can du gyur pa'i kha dog la mig gis 'dzin gyi /
dbyibs sa ma kha dog gcig pu la ni ma yin te /
ring po la sogs pa'i dbyibs kyi khyad par du gyur pa'i kha dog tu snang ba'i mig gi rnam par shes pa skye ba'i phyir ro /
ato varṇaḥ saṃsthānaṃ cacakṣuṣo viṣaya iti loke prasiddhiḥ de'i phyir kha dog dang dbyibs ni mig gi yul lo zhes 'jig rten na grags so /
tathā deśāntarotpattiviśiṣṭakāyasantatigrahaṇād vijñaptir api cakṣuṣo viṣaya iti prasiddhiḥ de bzhin du yul gzhan du 'byung bas khyad par du gyur pa'i lus kyi rgyud 'dzin pa'i phyir rnam par rig byed kyang mig gi yul zhes grags so /
paramārthatas tu saṃsthānavanna varṇo 'pi cakṣuṣo viṣayaḥ saṃsthānavat paramāṇoraniṣpannatvād vijñānasya bāhyārthāviṣayatvāt don dam par ni dbyibs bzhin du kha dog kyang mig gi yul ma yin te /
dbyibs bzhin du rdul phra rab ma grub pa'i phyir dang phyi rol gyi don rnam par shes pa'i yul ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
tasmāl lokaśāstraprasiddhir evātrācāryeṇānuvṛtteti gamyate de lta bas na slob dpon gyis 'dir 'jig rten dang bstan bcos las grags pa dang mthun par mdzad par shes so /
rūpānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt tannirdeśānantaram eva śabdasyanirdeśo nyāyya iti praśnaḥ śabdaḥ katamaḥ gzugs kyi 'og tu sgra bstan pa'i phyir de bshad ma thag tu sgra bshad par rigs pas na /
śrotrasya viṣaya iti śrotrasyaiva viṣayonānyasyendriyasyeti sgra gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang rna ba'i yul de zhes bya ba ste /
rna ba nyid kyi yul yin gyi /
dbang po gzhan gyi ma yin no /
evaṃ hy upādāyarūpatvāviśeṣe 'pianyendriyaviṣayebhyo rūpādibhyo 'sya viśeṣa ukto bhavati de ltar na rgyur byas pa'i gzugs yin par khyad par med kyang dbang po gzhan gyi yul gzugs la sogs pa las de bye brag tu bstan pa yin no /
śrotraviṣayaś ca śabda eveti parasparabhinnānāṃśabdabhedānāṃ śabdāyatanatvenābheda ukto bhavati rna ba'i yul ni sgra nyid do zhes bya bas kyang sgra'i bye brag phan tshun tha dad pa rnams sgra'i skye mched nyid du bye brag med par bstan pa yin no /
tadbhedapradarśanārtham āha upāttānupāttobhayamahābhūtahetukaiti de'i dbye ba bstan pa'i phyir ro /
zin pa dang ma zin pa dang gnyi ga'i ste /
'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba'o zhes bya ba smos so /
tatropāttāny ātmabhāvaparyāpannāni cittacaittair adhiṣṭhānabhāvenopagṛhītāni /
viparyayād anupāttāni 		de la zin pa'i ni lus su gtogs pa rnams te /
sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyis gnas kyi dngos por gzung ba rnams so /
bzlog pa ni mi zin pa rnams so /
tāni heturasyety upāttānupāttobhayamahābhūtahetukaḥ de dag ni 'di'i rgyu yin pas 'byung ba chen po zin pa dang ma zin pa dang gnyi ga'i ste /
'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba'o /
tatropāttamahābhūtahetuko hastavācchabdaity evamādi de la zin pa'i 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba ni lag pa dang ngag gi sgra la sogs pa'o /
anupāttamahābhūtahetuko vāyuvanaspatinadīśabdaityevamādi /
ubhayamahābhūtahetuko mṛdaṅgaśabdaity evamādigandhaḥ katamaḥ /
ghrāṇasyaiva viṣayaḥ 		mi zin pa'i 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba ni rlung dang nags tshal dang 'bab chu'i sgra la sogs pa'o /
gnyi ga'i 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba ni rnga'i sgra la sogs pa'o /
dri gang zhe na /
ghrāṇaviṣayaś ca gandha eveti pūrvavat sna nyid kyi yul zhes bya ba dang sna'i yul ni dri nyid do zhes bya ba yang snga ma bzhin no /
samagandhas tutenendriyamahābhūtānāṃ nānugraho nopaghātaḥ /
sa cagandhaḥsahajaḥ sāṃyogikaḥ pāriṇāmikaśca 		dri mnyam pa ni dbang po'i 'byung ba chen po rnams la phan pa yang mi 'dogs gnod pa yang mi byed pa'o /
dri ni lhan cig skyes pa dang sbyar ba las byung ba dang gyur pa las byung ba'o /
tatra sahajaścandanakuṅkumādīnām de la lhan cig skyes pa ni tsandan dang gur gum la sogs pa'o /
sāṃyogiko dhūpavartigandhādīnām /
pāriṇāmikaḥ pakvāmraphalādīnāmrasaḥ katama ityādi 		sbyar ba las byung ba ni bdug spos ri lu la sogs pa'i dri'o /
gyur pa las byung ba ni aa mra smin pa la sogs pa rnams kyi'o /
jihvāyā eva viṣayaḥjihvāviṣayaś ca rasa eveti pūrvad vistareṇa vaktavyam ro gang zhe na zhes bya ba la sogs pa lce nyid kyi yul zhes bya ba dang lce'i yul ni ro nyid do zhes bya ba yang /
snga ma bzhin du rgya cher brjod par bya'o /
prakṛtibhedāt ṣaḍbheda uktaḥ rang bzhin gyis tha dad pa'i phyir tha dad pa drug smos te /
anyas tu bhedastatsaṃyogabhedāt anantaś ca bhavati gzhan du dbye na ni de'i sbyar ba tha dad pa mtha' yas bar 'gyur ro /
atra hy upādāyarūpanirdeśaḥ prastutaḥ rasānantaraṃtuspraṣṭavyaikadeśa upādāyarūpatvenoddiṣṭa ity atorasanirdeśānantaraṃ spraṣṭavyaikadeśanirdidikṣayā praśnaḥ spraṣṭavyaikadeśaḥ katamaiti /
spraṣṭavyaṃ hi /
dvividham bhūtāni tāni copādāya rūpam /
bhūtāni ca pūrvam uddiṣṭāninirdiṣṭāni ca 		'dir ni rgyur byas pa'i gzugs bstan pa'i skabs yin pas ro'i 'og tu rgyur byas pa'i gzugs reg bya'i phyogs gcig bstan pas de'i phyir ro bshad pa'i 'og tu reg bya'i phyogs gcig bshad par 'dod nas /
reg bya'i phyogs gcig gang zhe na zhes dris so /
reg bya ni rnam pa gnyis te /
'byung ba rnams dang de dag rgyur byas pa'i gzugs so /
'byung ba rnams ni sngar bstan pa dang bshad pa rnams so /
iha tūpādāyarūpaṃ prakṛtam iti /
ataḥspraṣṭavyaikadeśaḥ katama upādāyarūpam iti sambadhyate 		'dir ni rgyur byas pa'i gzugs [?] kyi skabs yin pas de'i phyir reg bya'i phyogs gcig gang zhe na zhes bya ba ni rgur byas pa'i gzugs zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro /
kāyasya viṣaya iti kāyasyaiva viṣayo na cakṣurādīnām itirūpaśabdādibhyo 'sya bheda ukto bhavati lus kyi yul te zhes bya ba ni lus nyid kyi yul yin gyi /
mig la sogs pa'i ni ma yin no /
de ltar na gzugs dang sgra la sogs pa las de tha dad par bstan pa yin no /
kāyasya ca viṣayaḥsparśa eveti bhūtabhautikayoḥ parasparavilakṣaṇatve 'pi sparśatvenābheda ukto bhavati lus nyid kyi yul reg bya nyid ces bya bas ni 'byung ba dang 'byung ba las gyur pa gnyis phan tshun mi 'dra yang reg bya nyid du bye brag med par bstan pa yin no /
kāyasya viṣaya iti bhūtānām api kāyaviṣayatvād upādāyarūpaprasaṅga ity ata āha mahābhūtāni sthāpayitveti lus kyi yul te zhes bya ba 'byung ba rnams kyang lus kyi yul yin pas rgyur byas pa'i gzugs su thal bar 'gyur ro /
de'i phyir 'byung ba chen po rnams gzhag ste zhes bya ba smos so /
spraṣṭavyaikadeśapradarśanārtham āha ślakṣṇatvaṃkarkaśatvamityādi reg bya'i phyogs gcig rab tu bstan pa'i phyir /
'jam pa nyid dang rtsub pa nyid dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
nanu ca kāyendriyeṇa spṛśyata iti ślakṣṇatvādi spraṣṭavyam ucyate lus kyi dbang por reg par bya bas na 'jam pa nyid la sogs pa reg bya zhes brjod na ni /
yac ca yena spṛśyate niyogāttad api tat spṛśatīti kāyendriye 'pi sparśatvaprasaṅgaḥ /
na hikenacit kiñcit spṛśyate 		gang gis gang la reg pa des kyang de la reg par gdon mi za bar 'gyur bas lus kyi dbang po yang reg khyar thal bar mi 'gyur ram /
sarvātmanā sparśane hi sarvapiṇḍāḥparamāṇupramāṇāḥ syuḥ gang gis kyang ci la yang reg pa med de /
bdag nyid thams cad kyis reg na ni gong bu thams cad rdul phra rab kyi tshad tsam du 'gyur ro /
pradeśena sparśane paramāṇūnāṃsāvayavatvaprasaṅgāt paramāṇutvam avahīyate phyogs kyis reg na ni rdul phra rab rnams cha shas dang bcas par thal bar 'gyur bas rdul phra rab nyid nyams par 'gyur ro /
tasmādviṣayendriyayor nirantarotpattau yadāśritaṃ vijñānaṃ viṣayamupalabhate tena sa viṣayaḥ spṛṣṭa ity upacaryate na tuviṣayeṇa vijñānāśrayaḥ de bas na yul dang dbang po gnyis bar ma chad par skye ba na gang la brten nas rnam par shes pas yul dmigs pa des yul la reg ces bya bar gdags kyi yul gyis rnam par shes pa'i gnas pa ni ma yin no /
ata eva kāyendriyeṇa bhūtāny evaspṛśyanta ity upacaryate na tadāśritā rūpādayaḥkāyavijñānenāgrahaṇāt de'i phyir lus kyi dbang pos 'byung ba rnams nyid la reg go zhes gdags kyi /
de dag la gnas pa'i gzugs la sogs pa la ni ma yin te /
puṣpādiṣu ca varṇādyupaghātastadāśrayopaghātāt na kāyasaṃsparśād iti lus kyi rnam par shes pas mi 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
me tog la sogs pa'i kha dog la sogs pa la gnod pa ni de'i gnas la gnod pa'i phyir gyi lus kyis reg pa'i phyir ni ma yin no /
varṇādyāśrayasyāpikāyenāspṛṣṭasya katham upaghāta iti /
cintyam etat 		kha dog la sogs pa'i gnas la yang lus kyis reg pa ma yin na ji ltar gnod par 'gyur zhe na /
'di ni bsam par bya ba ste /
tasmāllokavyavahāra evātrānusartavyaḥ na paramārthaḥ de lta bas na 'dir 'jig rten gyi tha snyad du 'brang bar bya'i don dam par ni ma yin no /
ślakṣṇatvaṃ mṛdv aparūṣamāliṅganakṣamam ity arthaḥ 'jam pa nyid ni ma nyen pa dang mi rtsub dang spyad du bzod pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ślakṣṇam eva ślakṣṇatvam 'jam pa kho na 'jam pa nyid do /
karkaśatvam iti karkam asyāstītikarkaśam lomaśavat rtsub pa nyid ces bya ba ni 'di la rtsub pa yod pas rtsub pa zhes bya ste /
spu can bzhin no /
karkam iti balasyākhyā rtsub pa zhes bya ba ni stobs zhes bya ba'o /
karkaśam evakarkaśatvam rtsub pa kho na rtsub pa nyid de /
rūkṣaṃ paruṣam asukumāram ity arthaḥ /
guruḥsāndra ity arthaḥ 		rud rud po dang hrud hrud po dang shin tu 'jam pa ma yin pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
lci ba ni lcid gnon zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
gurv evagurutvam /
yena bhāvāstulyanteavanamanti 		lci ba kho na lci ba nyid de /
dngos po rnam pa 'jam pa na gang gis dma' bar byed pa'o /
laghutvaṃyena bhāvā nāvanamanti /
saṃsthānapṛthutve 'pi yasya sadbhāvāt sukham āhriyate 		yang ba nyid ni gang gis dngos po rnams 'jam pa na dma' bar mi 'gyur ba ste /
dbyibs cher zin kyang gang yod na gdeg bla ba ste /
tulāyājaghanāvanatikāraṇam ity arthaḥ /
yadabhyāhatasyoṣṇābhilāṣobhavati tacchītam /
nanu ca grīṣme śaradi ca saty api śītauṣṇābhilāṣo na bhavati 		srang mda'i rtse mo dma' bar 'gyur ba'i rgyu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
gang gis nyen na dro ba 'dod pa de ni grang ba nyid do /
dpyid dang ston grang ba yod kyang dro ba mi 'dod pa ma yin nam /
uṣṇābhilāṣasyānyathābhāvāt śītamevoṣṇābhilāṣakṛd ity avadhāryate dro ba 'dod pa ni gzhan du mi 'byung bas grang ba nyid dro ba 'dod par byed pa zhes nges par gzung ngo /
evaṃ ca tatkāryam apitajjātīyatvāl lakṣyate lākṣaṇikaiḥ de ltar na de'i 'bras bu yang de dang rigs gcig pa'i phyir mtshan nyid pa rnams kyis rtogs so /
jighatsābhojanābhilāṣakṛt bkres pa ni zas 'dod par byed pa'o /
pipāsāpānābhilāṣakṛt skom pa ni skom 'dod par byed pa'o /
na hi caitasikodharmaḥ kāyendriyaviṣayo 'stīti sems las byung ba'i chos ni lus kyi dbang po'i yul ma yin no zhe na /
ataḥ kāraṇe kāryopacāraṃkṛtveha nirdeśo jighatsā pipāseti de'i phyir rgyu la 'bras bu gdags pa byas nas 'dir bkres pa dang skom pa bstan te /
vāyudhātubhūyiṣṭho hi kaścit spraṣṭavyaviśeṣo jighatsāhetuḥ koṣṭha utpadyate /
sajighatsākāraṇatvāj jighatsety uktaḥ 		rlung gi khams kyi shas che ba ni bkres pa'i rgyu reg bya'i bye brag 'ga' zhig 'byung ba de ni bkres pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir /
bkres pa zhes brjod do /
evaṃ tejodhātubhūyiṣṭhaḥ pipāsākāraṇatvāt pipāsety uktaḥ de bzhin du me'i khams kyi shas che na skom pa'i rgyu yin ba'i phyir skom pa zhes brjod do /
anye 'pimūrchābaladaurbalyādayaḥ spraṣṭavyaviśeṣā vidyante /
eteṣvevāntarbhutāiti pṛthag noktāḥ 		gzhan nas brgyal ba dang nyams yod pa dang nyam chung ba la sogs pa reg bya'i bye brag smos pa rnams kyang 'di dag gi nang du 'dus pas logs shig tu ma brjod do /
mūrchā ślakṣṇatvān na bhidyate /
balaṃ karkaśagurutvābhyām 		brgyal ba ni 'jam pa nyid las gud na med do /
nyams yod pa ni rtsub pa dang lci ba nyid las logs shig na med de /
evam anye 'pispraṣṭavyaviśeṣā yathāsambhavam antarbhāvayitavyāḥ /
ślakṣṇatvādīnāṃ tv āśrayaviśeṣāt parasparato viśeṣaḥ 		de ltar gzhan nas reg bya'i bye brag 'byung ba rnams kyang 'di dag gi nang du mthun mthun du bsdu bar bya'o /
'jam pa la sogs pa yang gnas kyi bye brag gis phan tshun tha dad de /
aptejodhātūtsadatvācchlakṣṇatvam /
pṛthivīvāyudhātūtsadatvātkarkaśatvam /
pṛthivyabdhātūtsadatvād gurutvam /
tejovāyudhātūtsadatvāl laghutvam 		chu nyid las gud na med do /
nyams yod pa ni rtsub pa dang lci ba rlung gi khams kyi shas che ba ni rtsub pa nyid do /
sa dang chu'i khams kyi shas che ba ni lci ba nyid do /
me dang rlung gi khams kyi shas che ba ni yang ba nyid do /
ata eva mṛtaśarīreṣvadhikaṃ gurutvam de nyid kyi phyir shi ba'i lus la lci ba nyid kyi shas che ba'o /
abdhātūtsadatvāc chītam chu'i khams kyi shas che ba ni grang ba'o /
vāyudhātūtsadatvāj jighatsā rlung gi khams kyi shas che ba ni bkres pa'o /
tejodhātūtsadatvāt pipāsā me'i khams kyi shas che ba ni skom pa'o /
evamanyasminn apy upādāyarūpe yathāsambhavam āśrayaviśeṣātparasparaviśeṣo 'vagantavya iti /
atra tu diṅmātraṃ pradarśitaṃgranthagauravaparihārārtham iti /
rūpaskandhād upādāyarūpād vāvijñaptir evāvaśiṣyata itipraśnaḥ avijñaptiḥ katameti 		de bzhin du gnas kyi bye brag gis phan tshun bye brag tu gyur par rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gzhan la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du khong du chud par bya ste /
'dir ni tshig mang du 'gyur ba spangs pa'i phyir phyogs tsam zhig bstan to /
gzugs kyi phung po'am rgyur byes pa'i gzugs las rnam par rig byed ma yin pa 'ba' zhig lus pas /
tannirdeśaḥ /
vijñaptisamādhijaṃkuśalākuśalaṃrūpamanidarśanam apratighamiti 		rnam par rig byed ma yin pa gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang rnam par rig byed dang ting nge 'dzin las byung ba'i gzugs te /
bstan du med pa thogs pa med pa'o zhes bya bas de bstan to /
tatra vijñaptir dvividhā de la rnam par rig byed ni rnam pa gnyis te /
kāyavijñaptir vāgvijñaptiś ca lus kyi rnam par rig byed dang ngag gi rnam par rig byed do /
sā punaḥ pratyekaṃ tridhābhidyate kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtabhedāt de re re la yang dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du mi ston pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa gsum gsum du 'gyur ro /
avijñaptir api trividhaivakāmāptā rūpāptānāsravā ca rnam par rig byed ma yin pa yang rnam pa gsum nyid do /
'dod par gtogs pa dang gzugs su gtogs pa dang zag pa med pa'o /
tatra kāmāvacary avijñaptiḥ kuśalākuśalavijñaptijā de la 'dod pa na spyod pa'i rnam par rig byed ma yin pa ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rnam par rig byed las byung ba ste /
sā punaḥ prātimokṣasaṃvarobodhisattvasaṃvaro 'saṃvaras tadviyuktā ca de yang so sor thar pa'i sdom pa dang byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa dang sdom pa ma yin pa dang de dag ma rtogs pa'o /
tatraprātimokṣasaṃvaro bhikṣuśrāmaṇeropāsakopavāsasthabhedādravyataś caturvidhaḥ de la so sor thar pa'i sdom pa ni dge slong dang dge tshul dang dge bsnyen dang bsnyen gnas la gnas pa'i bye brag gis rdzas su rnam pa bzhi'o /
nāmatas tv aṣṭavidhaḥbhikṣubhikṣuṇyādibhedāt dge slong dang dge slong ma la sogs pa'i bye brag gis ming du ni rnam pa brgyad do /
tatra prātimokṣasaṃvaraḥ sanidānātsarvākārāt paropaghātān nivṛttiḥ de la so sor thar pa'i sdom pa ni gzhan la gnod pa byed pa las gzhi dang bcas par rnam pa thams cad du ldog pa'o /
bodhisattvasaṃvaraḥkāyajīvitopāttavastunirapekṣaṃ kāyavākcittaiḥsarvākāraparopakārapravṛttiḥ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa ni lus dang srog gis bsdus pa'i dngos po la mi lta bar /
lus dang ngag dang sems kyis rnam pa thams cad du gzhan la phan 'dogs par zhugs pa'o /
asaṃvaraḥsarv ākār apar opag hāta prav ṛtti ḥ sdom pa ma yin pa ni rnam pa thams cad du gzhan la gnod pa byed par zhugs pa'o /
dekadeśenānugrahopaghātapravṛttir naiva saṃvaro nāsaṃvaraḥ phyogs gcig gis phan 'dogs pa dang gnod pa byed par zhugs pa ni sdom pa yang ma yin sdom pa ma yin pa yang ma yin pa'o /
tatra rūpāptānāsravā ca esamādhijā /
sā punar yathākramaṃ dhyānasaṃvaro 'nāsravasaṃvaraś ca 		de la gzugs su gtogs pa dang zag pa med pa ni ting nge 'dzin las byung ba ste /
de yang bsam gtan gyi sdom pa dang zag pa med pa'i sdom pa go rims bzhin no /
e ftatra caturṣu dhyāneṣvanāgamye dhyānāntare ca sāsravasamādhijo dhyānasaṃvaraḥ de la bsam gtan bzhi po dag dang mi lcogs pa med pa dang bsam gtan khyad par can dag na zag pa dang bcas pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang lhan cig byung ba ni bsam gtan gyi sdom pa'o /
anāsravasamādhijo 'nāsravasaṃvaraḥ /
tasyāstūpādāyarūpatvaṃ bhūtāny āśritya pravṛtter anuvṛtteś ca /
idamihāmutrety ayam eva vyapadeśo nidarśanam /
so 'tra nāstītyanidarśanam 		zag pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang lhan cig byung ba ni zag pa med pa'i sdom pa'o /
de yang 'byung ba rnams la brten nas 'byung ba dang rjes su 'jug pa'i phyir rgyur byas pa'i gzugs nyid do /
'di ni 'di na'o /
pha bi ni pha bi na'o zhes brjod pa 'di ni bstan pa'o /
de 'di la med pas bstan du med pa'o /
svapradeśe parasyotpattipratibandhaḥpratighātaḥ /
sa cāvijñapter adeśatvān na sambhavatītyapratigham /
sarvaṃ hirūpaṃ trividham 		rang gi phyogs su gzhan 'byung ba'i gegs byed pa ni thogs pa'o /
rnam par rig byed ma yin pa ni yul na mi gnas pa'i phyir de mi srid pas thogs pa med pa'o /
gzugs thams cad ni rnam pa gsum ste /
bstan du yod la thogs pa dang bcas pa dang bstan du med la thogs pa dang bcas pa dang bstan du yang med la thogs pa yang med pa'o /
sanidarśanaṃsapratigham cakṣurindriyaviṣayaḥ de la bstan du yod la thogs pa dang bcas pa ni mig gi dbang po'i yul lo /
anidarśanaṃ sapratigham cakṣurādayaḥ pañca śabdagandharasasparśāś catvāraḥanidarśanam apratighaṃ ca dharmāyatanikaṃ rūpam /
tatpunaḥpañcaprakāram ābhisaṅkṣepikam ābhyavakāśikaṃsāmādānikaṃ parikalpitaṃ vaibhūtvikaṃceti 		bstan du med la thogs pa dang bcas pa ni mig la sogs pa lnga dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya bzhi'o /
bstan du yang med la thogs pa yang med pa ni chos kyi skye mched kyi gzugs so /
de yang rnam pa lnga ste /
bsdus pa las gyur pa dang mngon par skabs yod pa dang yang dag par blangs pa las byung ba dang kun brtags pa dang dbang 'byor pa'o /
iha tvekādaśadravya eva rūpaskandho vivakṣita iti sāmādānikam evarūpam anidarśanam apratigham ity uktaṃ nānyat /
kimarthaṃpunas tan noktam 		'dir gzugs kyi phung po ni /
rdzas bcu gcig kho nar 'dod pas yang dag par blangs pa las byung ba'i gzugs nyid du bstan du yang med la thogs pa yang med par bshad de /
gzhan ni ma yin no /
ci'i phyir de dag mi bstan zhe na /
ābhisaṅkṣepikaṃ paramāṇavaeva nīlādikādvarṇān na bhidyante bsdus pa las gyur pa ni rdul phra rab rnams nyid de /
de dag ni sngon po la sogs pa'i kha dog las gud na med de /
na ca varṇanibhā anyā nīlādikād varṇāt sngon po la sogs pa'i kha dog las kha dog tu snang ba gzhan rnams ni med do /
ābhyavakāśikaṃ paramāṇava evatadanyapratighātikaspraṣṭavyavirahitāḥ mngon par skabs yod pa yang rdul phra rab rnams nyid de /
de las gzhan pa thogs par byed pa'i reg bya dang bral ba rnams so /
te ca varṇātmakatvādihopāttā eveti punar na nirdiṣṭāḥ de dag kyang kha dog gi bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir 'dir 'dus pa nyid pas yang ma bshad do /
parikalpitaṃ pratibimbarūpamasthisaṅkalikādikam kun brtags pa ni gzugs brnyan gyi gzugs keng rus la sogs pa'o /
vaibhūtvikaṃvimokṣadhyāyigocaraṃ yad rūpamtad vikalpātmakatvād iha nopāttam dbang 'byor pa ni rnam par thar pa la bsam gtan pa'i spyod yul gyi gzugs gang yin pa ste /
de ni rnam par rtog pa'i bdag nyid yin pas 'dir ma 'dus te /
na hi tat tadākāravijñānapratyavabhāsād bahirvidyate de ni de'i rnam pa can gyi rnam par shes pa la so sor snang ba las phyi rol na med do /
pratibimbaṃ ca viṣayapratyavabhāso vijñānasyaivetina vijñānāt pratibimbaṃ pratibimbād vā vijñānaṃ pṛthag asti /
tasmāt sāmādānikam evoktam nānyat 		gzugs brnyan yang yul du snang ba'i rnam par shes pa nyid do /
rnam par shes pa las gzugs brnyan nam gzugs brnyan las rnam par shes pa gud na med do /
de lta bas na yang dag par blangs la las byung ba nyid 'dir bshad kyi /
ko vāprabhāvamahatām asmadvidho buddhivispanditāny avagāhituṃ samarthaḥ gzhan ni ma yin no /
mthu stobs kyis che ba'i blos bskyod pa ni bdag lta bu gang gis kyang rtogs par ga la nus te /
tasmāt tadanabhidhāna ācāryābhiprāyo'nveṣyaḥ de lta bas na de dag ma bshad pa ni slob dpon gyi dgongs pa btsal bar bya'o /
etad uktaṃ bhavati vijñaptisamādhisambhūtaṃkuśalākuśalam upādāyarūpam vikṣiptāvikṣiptacittasyācittasyaca yad anubadhnātitat parityāgakāraṇābhāve uktaṃ bhavati avijñaptir iti de ni 'di skad du rnam par rig byed dang ting nge 'dzin las byung ba dge ba dang mi dge ba las byung ba rgyur byas pa'i gzugs ni sems gyeng ba dang ma gyeng ba dang sems med pa na yang rjes su 'brang ba gang yin pa ste /
de stong pa'i rgyu med na yod pa ni rnam par rig byed ma yin pa'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
rūpakriyāsvabhāvāpi satīsvasamutthāpakaṃ cittaṃvijñaptivat paraṃ na vijñapayatītyavijñaptiḥ gzugs dang byed pa'i ngo bo nyid yin du zin kyang rang kun nas slong ba'i sems rnam par rig par byed pa bzhin du gzhan la rnam par rig par mi byed pas rnam par rig byed ma yin pa'o /
atra ca vaibhāṣikaparikalpitavijñaptivad avijñaptirapi naivāsti pramāṇāviṣayatvāt /
na caprātimokṣasaṃvarādyabhāvaḥ /
tathā hiyayā cetanayākṛtābhyupagama upasampadādividhānapūrvakaṃ pratiṣiddhātkarmaṇaḥ kāyavācau saṃvṛṇotitayā cetanayālayavijñāne'nāgatatajjātīyacetanotpattaye bījam āhitam yata uttarakālamahaṃ prāṇātipātādibhyaḥ prativirata iti samādānasmṛtirutpadyate /
rtasyāṃ samutpannāyāṃ yo lajjī na sa śikṣāṃbhinatti 		'dir ni bye brag tu smra bas kun brtags pa'i rnam par rig byed bzhin du rnam par rig byed ma yin pa yang med de /
tshad ma'i yul du ma gyur pa'i phyir ro /
so sor thar pa'i sdom pa la sogs pa ni med pa ma yin te /
'di ltar sems pas bya bar khas blangs nas bsnyen par rdzogs par bya ba la sogs pa'i cho ga sngon du btang ste /
sems pa gang gis lus dang ngag gi las bkag pa las sdom pa'i sems pa des ma 'ongs pa na de dang rigs gcig pa bskyed pa'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la sa bon btab nas /
de'i 'og tu bdag ni srog gcod pa la sogs pa spangs pa'o zhes yang dag par blangs pa dran pa 'byung ste /
de byung nas gang 'dzem pa de bslab pa mi 'dral lo /
evaṃ ca sānubandhā samādānacetanā saṃvara ityuktam bhavati de ltar na yang dag par blang ba'i sems pa rgyun chags pa dang bcas pa ni sngom pa zhes bstan pa yin no /
tathā dhyānaṃ mārgaṃ vā samāpanno vināpyavijñaptyā tadrūpaṃ mārgam āśrayaṃ ca pratilabhate yasyapratilambhād vyutthito 'pi na punar mithyāvāgādiṣu pravartatesaṃyagvāgādiṣv eva pravartate de bzhin du bsam gtan nam lam la snyoms par zhugs na rnam par rig byed ma yin pa med par yang gang thob na langs nas log pa'i ngag la sogs pa la mi 'jug pa dang yang dag pa'i ngag la sogs pa la 'jug pa de lta bu'i bsam pa dang gnas thob ste /
ato nimitte naimittikopacāraṃkṛtvā aṣṭau mārgāṅgāni dhyānasaṃvaraś ca vyavasthāpyate de'i phyir rgyu la rgyu can gdags par byas nas lam gyi yan lag brgyad rnams dang bsam gtan gyi sdom pa yang rnam par gzhag go /
asaṃvaro 'pi vadhakaprayogakriyācetanā tatkulīnānāmtatkarmābhyupagamacetanā 'nyakulīnānām sdom pa ma yin pa yang de'i rigs su skyes pa rnams kyi gsad par sbyor bar bya ba'i sems pa dang gzhan gyi rigs su skyes pa rnams kyi las de bya bar khas len pa'i sems pa ste /
na cataccetanāpagame 'samvaratyāgaḥ sattveṣudrohāśayasyāvinivṛttatvāt sems pa de med kyang sdom pa ma yin pa btang ba ma yin te /
sems can rnams la gnod pa bya bar bsam pa las ma log pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ cakriyācetanābhyupagamacetanā ca sattveṣudrohāśayānugatāsaṃvara ity uktaṃ bhavati de ltar bya ba'i sems pa dang khas len pa'i sems pa sems can rnams la gnod pa bya ba'i bsam pa dang ldan pa ni sdom pa ma yin pa'o zhes bstan pa yin no /
atra cavijñaptisamādhijatvaṃ subodham eveti na punar ihaprapañcitam 'dir rnam par rig byed dang ting nge 'dzin las byung ba nyid ni brda phrad par sla bas yang ma spros so /
kuśalākuśalatvaṃ tu saṃvarāsaṃvaracetanānāṃsvata eva tadanubandhasya kuśalākuśalacetanākṣiptatvāt kuśalākuśalacetanāphalatvāc ca sdom pa dang sdom pa ma yin pa'i sems pa rnams kyi dge ba dang mi dge ba ni bdag nyid kho nas so; /
de'i rgyun chags pa ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'i sems pas 'phangs pa dang dge ba dang mi dge ba'i sems pa'i 'bras bu yin pa'i phyir ro /
dhyānānāsravasaṃvarayor apidhyānānāsravamārganimittatvāt saṃyagvāgādiphalatvāc cakuśalatvam /
rūpatvaṃ punaḥ kāyavāgviṣayatvāt viṣayiṇi viṣayopacārāt /
anidarśanāpratighatvaṃ tu subodham iti 		bsam gtan dang zag pa med pa'i sdom pa yang bsam gtan dang zag pa med pa'i lam rgyu yin pa dang yang dag pa'i dag la sogs pa 'bras bu yin pa'i phyir dge ba'o /
gzugs ni lus dang ngag yul yin pa'i phyir te /
yul can la yul btags pa'i phyir ro /
bstan du med pa thogs pa med pa ni /
brda phrad par sla bas ma bshad do /
kasmāt punar ayam avijñaptiparyanto rūpaskandho rūpam ityucyate de'i ci'i phyir rnam par rig byed ma yin pa la thug pa'i gzugs kyi phung po 'di gzugs zhes bya zhe na /
uktaṃ hi bhagavatā t urūpyate rūpyata iti bhikṣavastasmād rūpopādānaskandhaity ucyate /
kena rūpyate 		bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang dge slong dag gzugs su rung bas de'i phyir gzugs nye bar len pa'i phung po zhes pa'o /
ci gzugs she na /
pāṇisaṃsparśenāpi spṛṣṭo rūpyata iti vistaraḥ lag pa'i 'dus te reg pas reg na gzugs su rung ba'o zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
sūtre hi vpāṇyādisaṃsparśena rūpaṇād rūpamity uktam /
kā punar iyaṃ rūpasya rūpaṇā 		mdo las kyang lag pa la sogs pa'i 'dus te reg pas gzugs yod pa'i phyir gzugs so zhes gsungs so /
gzugs kyi gzugs su yod pa 'di gang zhe na /
hastādisaṃsparśanapūrvāvasthāto'nyathotpādanā /
iyaṃ ca santānam adhikṛtyocyate nakṣaṇamkṣaṇasyotpādavināśakālayor adhikṛtatvāt 		lag pa la sogs pa'i 'dus te reg pa snga ma'i gnas las gzhan du skyed pa ste /
'di yang rgyun gyi dbang du byas te brjod kyi /
skad cig la ni ma yin te /
skad cig ni skye ba dang 'jig pa'i dus kyi dbang du byas pa dang gnas pa med pa'i phyir ro /
rūpaskandhānantaraṃ vedanāskandhanirdeśāvasarastadanantaram uddiṣṭatvād iti praśnaḥ vedanā katameti /
trividho 'nubhavaiti nirdeśaḥ 		gzugs kyi phung po'i 'og tu tshor ba'i phung po bshad pa'i skabs yin te /
de'i 'og tu bstan pas de'i phyir /
tshor ba gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang myong ba rnam pa gsum ste zhes bya bas bstan to /
anubhūtir anubhavoastu n ohlādaparitāpatadubhayākāravinirmuktasvarūpasākṣātkaraṇaḥ nyams su myong ba ni myong ba ste /
dngos po'i sim pa dang gdung ba dang gnyi ga'i rnam par ma gtogs pa'i rang gi ngo bo mngon sum du byed pa'o /
atha vā hlādaparitāpobhayākāravinirmuktaṃ vastusvarūpamanubhavatīty anubhavaḥ /
sa ca svabhāvabhedāt trividhaḥsukho duḥkho 'duḥkhāsukhaś ca 		yang na sim pa dang gdung ba dang gnyi ga'i rnam par ma gtogs pa'i dngos po'i rang gi ngo bo myong bar byed pas myong ba'o /
de yang ngo bo nyid kyi bye brag gis rnam pa gsum ste /
kathaṃ punaḥ /
sukhaduḥkhavyatirikto 'nyas tṛtīyo 'nubhavo 'stīti vijñāyate /
āgamād yuktitaś ca 		bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'o /
bde ba dang sdug bsngal ma gtogs par myong ba gsum pa yod pa ji ltar zhe na /
lung dang rigs pas mngon te /
uktaṃ hi sūtre tisro vedanāiti /
punaścoktam sukhasya ca prahāṇād duḥkhasya ca prahāṇādaduḥkhāsukhasya ceti 		mdo las tshor ba rnam pa gsum zhes gsungs so /
yang bde ba yang spangs sdug bsngal yang spangs te /
bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin zhes gsungs so /
yuktir api vedanāvirahitacittotpattyabhāvādapetasukhaduḥkhacittopalabdheś ceti rigs pa ni tshor ba dang bral ba'i sems skye ba med pa dang bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang bral ba'i sems kyang mi dmigs so /
vedanānubhavaḥsparśasyety ācāryasaṅghabhadraḥ reg pa myong ba ni tshor ba zhes slob dpon 'dus bzang gsungs te /
iṣṭāniṣṭobhayaviparītānāṃ sparśānām anubhavaḥ sā vedanā /
tathā coktam sukhavedanīyaṃ sparśaṃpratītyotpadyate sukhā vedanetivistaraḥ 		'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa dang gnyi ga las ldog pa'i reg pa rnams myong ba gang yin pa de tshor ba'o /
de ni 'di skad du /
bde ba myong bar 'gyur ba'i reg pa la brten nas bde ba'i tshor ba 'byung ngo zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
sukhavedanādijanakatvena tadvibhaktatvāt bde ba la sogs pa bskyed pa yin pas de rnam par dbye ba'i phyir ro /
yadi ca viṣayānubhavo vedanā syātekālambanebhyo'sya ko viśeṣaḥsyāt gal te yul myong ba tshor ba yin du zin na dmigs pa gcig pa rnams las 'di khyad par ci yod de /
yena sparśānubhavo vedaneti vyavasthāpyate de'i phyir reg pa myong ba ni tshor ba'o zhes rnam par gzhag go /
evaṃ tarhisañjñādhimokṣasmṛtiprajñādīnām ālambanadvārako vedanāvatsvabhāvo na vaktavyaḥ de lta na 'o na ni 'du shes dang mos pa dang dran pa dang; shes rab la sogs pa yang tshor ba bzhin du dmigs pa'i sgo nas ngo bo nyid brjod par mi bya'o /
athaikālambanebhyonimittodgrahaṇādibhiḥ sañjñādīnāṃ viśeṣa ucyate vedanāyā viṣayānubhavena kiṃ neṣyate ji ste 'du shes la sogs pa mtshan mar 'dzin pa la sogs pas dmigs pa gcig pa rnams las khyad par du 'dod na ni tshor ba yang yul myong bar ci'i phyir mi 'dod /
sparśānubhavaś catatsamprayogaḥ kāraṇabhāvo vā parikalpyeta tadālambanatvāsambhavāt de la dmigs par mi srid pa'i phyir reg pa myong ba yang mtshungs par ldan pa'am /
rgyu'i dngos por yongs su brtag grang na /
tatra na bhavet samprayogaḥsarvacaittānāṃ sparśasamprayogāviśeṣāt de la mtshungs par ldan pa ni ma yin te /
sems las byung ba thams cad reg pa dang mtshungs par ldan par bye brag med pa'i phyir ro /
nāpi kāraṇabhāvaḥsarvacaittānāṃ sparśasya kāraṇatvāviśeṣāt rgyu'i dngos por yang mi rung ste /
sems las byung ba thams cad kyi rgyu reg pa yin par bye brag med pa'i phyir ro /
na ca loke śāstre vānubhavaśabdaḥ kārye kāraṇe vā prasiddhaḥ /
prasiddhas tusākṣātkāre 		'jig rten dang bstan bcos las kyang myong ba'i sgra ni 'bras bu'am rgyur grags pa med kyi mngon sum du byed par grags so /
evaṃtu manyante śubhāśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃphalavipākaṃ pratyanubhavanty anenety anubhavaḥ 'di snyam du sems te las dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa 'dis myong ba ste /
tatraśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ sukho 'nubhavaḥ phalavipākaḥ /
aśubhānāṃ duḥkhaḥ /
ubhayeṣām aduḥkhāsukhaḥ 		de la bde ba myong ba ni las dge ba rnams kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa'o /
sdug bsngal ni mi dge ba rnams kyi'o /
bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa ni gnyi ga'i'o snyam mo /
atracālayavijñānam eva śubhāśubhakarmavipākaḥ 'dir ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid las dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rnam par smin pa ste /
tatsamprayuktaivopekṣā paramārthataḥ śubhāśubhānāṃkarmaṇāṃ vipākaḥ don dam par na de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i btang snyoms nyid las dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rnam par smin pa'o /
sukhaduḥkhayos tu vipākajatvādvipākopacāraḥ bde ba dang sdug bsngal ni rnam par smin pa las byung ba'i phyir rnam par smin pa zhes btags pa'o /
tatra sukho 'nubhavoyasya nirodhaityādi de la bde ba myong ba ni gang 'gags na zhes bya ba la sogs pa yin na /
yat tarhy uktaṃ pratītyasamutpāde yasyāmutpannāyām aviyogecchā jāyatesā sukhā vedaneti tat katham 'o na rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba las gang 'byung na bral bar mi 'dod pa skye ba de bde ba'i tshor ba'o zhes 'byung ba de ji lta bu /
nāsty atra virodhaḥ arthata itaropādānāt 'di la 'gal ba med de /
don du na cig shos kyang zin pa'i phyir ro /
yasyām utpannāyāmaviyogecchā jāyata ity arthata uktaṃ bhavati tasyāṃniruddhāyāṃ punaḥ saṃyogecchāpi bhavatīti gang byung na 'bral bar mi 'dod ba skye ba zhes bya ba ni don du na de 'gags na phrad par 'dod par yang 'gyur ro zhes bstan pa yin no /
yasyanirodhesaṃyogacchandobhavatīty atrāpy arthata uktambhavati tasyotpāde 'viyogacchandobhavati gang 'gags na phrad par 'dod par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba yang 'dir don du na de byung na 'bral bar mi 'dod pa'o zhes bstan pa yin no /
yat tarhyanicchopagatarāgaparyavasthānānāṃ yatīnāṃ rāgaje sukha utpanne viyogecchā jāyate nirodhe cāsaṃyogacchandaḥ tatkatham /
nāsau tata eva jāyate tadvidūṣaṇāt 		'o na dka' thub can rnams mi 'dod bzhin du 'dod chags kyi kun nas dkris pa dang phrad pa rnams 'dod chags las byung ba'i bde ba skyes pa'i tshe 'bral bar 'dod pa skye zhing /
'gags pa na phrad par mi 'dod pa gang yin pa de ji lta bu zhe na /
de ni sun 'byin pa'i phyir de nyid las skye ba ma yin te /
śīlasamādhiparipanthitvaṃ tasya sukhasya paśyatāṃ tadubhayaṃbhavatīti nāsti virodhaḥ bde ba de tshul khrims dang ting nge 'dzin gyi bar du gcod par mthong ba rnams la gnyi ga mi 'byung bas 'gal ba med do /
duḥkhoyasyotpādeviyogacchanda iti nirodhe ca punar /
asaṃyogacchandaḥ 		sdug bsngal ni gang byung na bral bar 'dod pa'o zhes bya ba ni gang 'gags na yang phrad par mi 'dod pa'o /
viyogas taducchedaḥ /
chando 'bhilāṣaḥprārthanā 		bral na ni de'i rgyun chad pa'o /
'dod pa ni mngon par 'dod pa dang smon pa'o /
duḥkhāsukho yasyotpādaubhayaṃ /
na bhavatītyādi 		sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa ni gang byung na gnyi gar 'dod par mi 'gyur ro /
tatra kāyacittopacayapravṛttatvān manojñasvabhāvatvāc ca sukho 'nubhava iti nirodhe punas tatsaṃyogābhilāṣaḥ pravartate de la lus dang sems rgyas par byed pa dang yid du 'ong ba'i ngo bo nyid yin pa'i phyir /
bde ba myong ba ni gang 'gags na de dang phrad par 'dod pa'o /
kāyacittāpacayapravṛttatvāsvabhāvataś ca pratikūlo duḥkho'nubhava iti tasyotpādetadviyogacchando bhavati lus dang sems nyams dams [?] par byed pa dang ngo bo nyid kyi mi mthun pa'i phyir /
sdug bsngal myong ba ni de byung na de dang bral bar 'dod pa yin no /
yas tu nobhayapravṛtto 'sti ca so'nubhavo 'duḥkhāsukhaḥ akṛṣṇāśuklakarmavat gnyi ga ni mi 'byung ba la yang myong ba gang yin pa de yod de /
bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa ste /
nag po yang ma yin dkar po yang ma yin pa'i las dang 'dra'o /
ata evacānanugrahānupaghātapravṛttatvāt tadaduḥkhāsukhotpādaubhayecchābhāvaḥ de'i phyir phan 'dogs pa yang med la gnod pa byed pa yang med par zhugs pa'i phyir ro /
de byung na gnyi gar 'dod pa med do /
eṣa tu trividho 'nubhavaḥ pratyekam āśrayabhedāt punaḥṣaḍvidho bhavaticakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanakāyamanaḥsaṃsparśajatvāt /
punarādheyasaṅkalanato dvidhā bhidyatekāyikaś caitasikaśceti 		myong ba rnam pa gsum po 'di ni re re la yang gnas kyi bye brag gis rnam pa drug tu gyur te /
mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i phyir ro /
yang brten par bsdu na ni rnam pa gnyis su 'gyur te /
tatra kāyāvinirbhāvavartitvāt sapratighatvāccakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanendriyāṇi kāye 'ntarbhāvyakāyaśabdenoktānīty ataścakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanakāyasaṃsparśānubhavaḥ kāyika ityuktaḥ lus kyi dang sems kyi'o /
de la mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce'i dbang po rnams ni lus la tha dad du mi 'jug pa dang thogs pa dang bcas pa dang bsags pa bzhin pa'i phyir lus kyi nang du bsdus te lus kyi sgrar brjod do /
de'i phyir mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i myong ba ni lus kyi zhes bstan to /
manaḥsaṃsparśajas tu caitasika ity uktaṃmanomātrāśrayatvāt yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba ni yid tsam la gnas pa yin pa'i phyir sems kyi zhes bya'o /
punaḥ vipakṣapratipakṣabhedena pratyekam anubhavasyadvidhā vyavasthānam sāmiṣo nirāmiṣa iti gredhāśritonaiṣkramyāśritaśceti yang mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po'i bye brag gis myong ba re re la yang rnam pa gnyis gnyis su 'gyur te /
zang zing dang bcas pa dang zang zing med pa dang zhen pa brten pa dang mngon par 'byung ba brten pa'o /
āmiṣa rātmabhāvatṛṣṇā /
ātmabhāva ādhyātmikā upādānaskandhāḥ 		zang zing ni lus la sred pa'o /
lus ni nang gi nye bar len pa'i phung po'o /
tasmiṃs tṛṣṇāpriyaikaputropagūḍhanyāyenāviyogam ivecchantī yā pravartatesā āmiṣam /
tayā saha vartata iti sāmiṣā /
tayā tṛṣṇayāvisaṃyuktā viyogānukūlāca nirāmiṣā /
pañceṣṭā rūpādayaḥ kāmaguṇāḥ 		de la sred pa bu gcig pa phongs pa la 'khyud pa'i tshul gyis mi 'brel bar 'dod pa lta bur 'jug pa gang yin pa de ni zang zing ste /
de dang ldan pas zang zing dang bcas pa'o /
sred pa de dang ldan pa ma yin pa dang bral ba'i rjes su mthun pa ni zang zing med pa'o /
apekṣābhiṣvaṅgaprārthanālakṣaṇena kāmenaguṇyante punaḥ punar abhyasyanta iti kāmaguṇāḥ /
teṣvabhiṣvaṅgaḥ prārthanā ca gredhaḥ 		gzugs la sogs pa 'dod pa'i yon tan sdug pa lnga la lta ba dang mngon par chags pa dang smon pa'i mtshan nyid kyi 'dod pas zlos shing yang dang yang goms par byed pas 'dod pa'i yon tan rnams te de dag la mngon par chags pa dang smon pa ni zhen pa'o /
tadāśritas tena vāśritogredhāśritaḥ de la brten pa'am zhen pa de brten pas na zhen pa brten pa'o /
naiṣkramyaṃ kāmavairāgyaṃ tanmārgo vā mngon par 'byung ba ni 'dod pa'i yon tan las 'dod chags dang bral ba'am de'i lam ste /
tadāśritas tena vāśrito naiṣkramyāśritaḥ de la brten pa'am de brten pas mngon par 'byung ba la brten pa'o /
tatra satkāyavairāgyaṃ purodhāya vipakṣapratipakṣabhāvenasāmiṣanirāmiṣayor vyavasthānam de la 'jig tshogs dang 'dod chags dang bral ba'i dbang du byas te mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po'i dngos por zang zing dang bcas pa dang zang zing med pa gnyis rnam par gnas so /
laukikavairāgyam adhikṛtyagredhanaiṣkramyāśritavyavasthānam 'jig rten pa dang 'dod chags dang bral ba'i dbang du byas te zhen pa brten pa dang mngon par 'byung ba la brten pa rnam par gzhag go /
kimarthaṃ punar atrasvarūpata eva bheda ukto nāśrayādibhedena yathānyatra ci'i phyir 'dir rang gi ngo bo'i bye brag bstan gyi ji ltar gzhan nas 'byung ba bzhin du gnas la sogs pa'i bye brag gis ma yin zhe na /
iha saṅkṣepasya vivakṣitatvāt sarvabhedānāṃ ca svarūpād apṛthaktvād āśrayādibhedena nokta iti 'dir ni mdor bsdu bar bzhed pa dang tha dad pa thams cad kyang rang gi ngo bo las gud na med pa'i phyir ro /
'dir gnas la sogs pa'i bye brag ma bshad do /
vedanāskandhanirdeśānantaraṃ sañjñāskandhanirdeśāvasaraity ataḥ praśnaḥ sañjñā katameti /
tviṣayanimittodgrahaṇamiti tannirdeśaḥ /
viṣayaālambanam 		tshor ba'i phung po bshad pa'i 'og tu 'du shes kyi phung bo bshad pa'i skabs su bab ste /
de'i phyir 'du shes gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang yul la mtshan mar 'dzin pa zhes bya ba de bstan to /
nimittaṃ viṣayaviśeṣaḥ nīlapītādyālambanavyavasthākāraṇam yul ni dmigs pa'o /
mtshan ma ni yul gyi bye brag sngon po dang ser po la sogs pa dmigs pa rnam par gzhag pa'i rgyu'o /
tasyodgrahaṇaṃ nīlanirūpaṇaṃnīlam etatpītam etad iti de la mtshan mar 'dzin pa ni 'di ni sngon po'o /
'di ni ser po'o zhes rtog pa'o /
evaṃ tarhicakṣurādivijñānasamprayuktā sañjñāviṣayanimittodgrahaṇātmikā na syāt viśeṣāsaṃlakṣaṇāt de lta na 'o na ni /
mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i 'du shes bye brag rtog pa med pa'i phyir yul la mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid du mi 'gyur ro zhe na /
sāpinimittodgrahaṇātmikaiva na paricchedikā mandatvāt de ni mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kho na yin par shes pa yin gyi /
zhan pa'i phyir yongs su gcod pa ni ma yin no /
anyathāpūrvam agṛhīte viśeṣe paścād api nirūpaṇaṃ na syāt nīlametat pītam etad iti gzhan du na sngar ma zin pa'i bye brag las phyis kyang 'di ni sngon po'o /
'di ni ser po'o zhes rtog par mi 'gyur ro /
svarūpābhede 'pi bhedaḥ sañjñāyā āśrayataālambanataś ca veditavyaḥ rang gi ngo bo tha dad pa med kyang gnas dang dmigs pas 'du shes tha dad par rig par bya'o /
āśrayataḥṣaṭ sañjñākāyāḥcakṣuḥsaṃsparśajā sañjñā evaṃ yāvanmanaḥsaṃsparśajāsañjñā gnas las 'du shes kyi tshogs drug ste /
mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i 'du shes dang de bzhin du yid kyi bar du 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i 'du shes so /
ālambanaṃ punaḥsanimittam animittam parīttammahadgatam apramāṇam ākiñcanyāyatanaṃca dmigs pa ni mtshan ma dang bcas pa dang mtshan ma med pa dang chung du dang rgya chen por gyur pa dang tshad med pa dang ci yang med pa'i skye mched do /
tatraśabdadvāreṇa yad artharūpam adhyāropitam tena nimittenavastusvarūpaṃ sanimittam de la sgra'i sgo nas gang don gyi ngo bor sgro btags pa de ni mtshan ma ste /
mtshan ma de dang lhan cig pa'i dngos po'i rang gi ngo bo ni mtshan ma dang bcas pa'o /
tasmin vastuny adhyāropitaṃrūpam etac chabdo 'sāv iti yā sañjñā sā sanimittālambanā dngos po de la sgro btags pa'i ngo bo de dang de ni sgra'o snyam pa'i 'du shes gang yin pa de ni mtshan ma dang bcas pa la dmigs pa'o /
animittaṃ punar anadhyāropitākāraṃ vastusvarūpam nirvāṇam bhavāgraṃ ca mtshan ma med pa ni sgro btags pa'i mtshan ma med pa ste /
dngos po'i rang gi ngo bo dang mya ngan las 'das pa dang srid pa'i rtse mo'o /
tatrādhyāropitanimittābhāvādrūpavedanānimittābhāvād apaṭutvāc caitat trayam animittamucyate de la sgro btags pa'i mtshan ma med pa dang gzugs dang tshor ba'i mtshan ma med pa dang gsal ba ma yin pa'i phyir /
'di gsum ni mtshan ma med pa zhes bya'o /
avyutpannaśabdārthasambandhasya hi rūpasvarūpa eva sañjñā bhavati na tu rūpam iti sgra dang don du 'brel ba mi shes pa ni ngo bo la rang gi ngo bo kho na'i 'du shes 'byung mod kyi /
gzugs yin no zhes bya bar ni ma yin te /
atas tadviṣayasañjñāanimittālambanā de'i phyir yul de la 'du shes pa ni mtshan ma med pa la dmigs pa'o /
nirvāṇadhātur apisarvasaṃskṛtanimittapratyastamitasvarūpa iti tadālambanenāpisamādhinā samprayuktā sañjñā animittālambanā mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings kyang 'dus byas thams cad kyi mtshan mar rab tu nub pa'i ngo bo yin pas de la dmigs pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i 'du shes ni mtshan ma med pa la dmigs pa'o /
bhavāgramapaṭutvād animittam srid pa'i rtse mo ni gsal ba ma yin pa'i phyir mtshan ma med pa ste /
tatsamāpannasya sañjñālambanaṃ na nimittīkarotīty animittālambanā /
bhavāgrasyātrāsphuṭanimittatvāt tadālambanam animittamucyate 'nudarākanyānyāyena na punas tatra nimittaṃnaivāstīty animittam /
anyathā sañjñābhāvaprasaṅga itinimittābhāve nimittodgrahaṇābhāvāt 		de la snyoms par zhugs pa'i 'du shes ni /
dmigs pa la mtshan mar mi byed pas mtshan ma la dmigs pa'o /
'dir ni mtshan ma gsal ba ma yin pa'i phyir /
de la dmigs pa yang bu mo lto med ces bya ba'i tshul du mtshan ma med pa zhes bya'i de ni mtshan ma med pa nyid kyi phyir mtshan ma med pa zhes ni mi bya'o /
gzhan du na ni 'du shes par thal bar 'gyur te /
mtshan ma med pas mtshan mar 'dzin pa yang med par 'gyur ro /
parīttaṃ kāmadhātur nikṛṣṭatvāt /
mahadgato rūpadhātuḥ utkṛṣṭatvāt 		chung ngu ni 'dod pa'i khams te ngan pa'i phyir ro /
rgya chen por gyur pa ni gzugs kyi khams te /
mchog tu gyur pa'i phyir ro /
apramāṇaākāśavijñānānantyāyatane aparyantatvāt tshad med pa ni nam mkha' mtha' yas dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched dag ste /
mu thug pa med pa'i phyir ro /
parigrahakiñcanābhāvād ākiñcanyāyatanam ākiñcanyam yongs su gzung ba ci yang med pa'i phyir ci yang med pa ni ci yang med pa'i skye mched do /
tasmāt kāmadhātvādyālambanā sañjñā parīttādisañjñāityucyate /
sañjñāskandhanirdeśānantaraṃ saṃskāraskandhanirdeśonyāyyas tadanantaram uddiṣṭatvād ity ataḥ praśnaḥ saṃskārāḥ katame iti /
vedanāsañjñābhyām /
anye caitasikā dharmāś cittaviprayuktāś ceti 		de lta bas na 'dod pa'i khams la sogs pa la dmigs pa ni chung ngu la sogs pa'i 'du shes zhes bya'o /
'du shes kyi phung po bshad pa'i 'og tu 'du byed kyi phung po bshad par rigs te /
de'i 'og tu bstan pas na de'i phyir /
'du byed rnams gang zhen zhes dris pa dang tshor ba dang 'du shes las gzhan pa sems las byung ba'i chos rnams dang sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa rnams so zhes bya bas de bstan to /
tannirdeśaḥ /
sametya sambhūya pratyayaiḥ kṛtatvāt sarva evarūpādiskandhasaṅgṛhītā dharmāḥ saṃskārā ity ucyante 		rkyen rnams 'dus shing tshogs nas byas pa'i phyir gzugs la sogs pa'i phung por bsdus pa'i chos thams cad ni 'du byed rnams zhes bya'o /
iha tusaṃskāraskandhasaṅgṛhītā eva saṃskārā abhipretāḥ 'dir ni 'du byed kyi phung por bsdus pa nyid 'du byed rnams su 'dod de /
rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṅgṛhītānām uktatvādvijñānaskandhasaṅgṛhītānāṃ ca vakṣyamāṇatvāt /
ata evavedanāsañjñayoḥ sparśamanaskārādibhiś caitasikatvāviśeṣe 'pyāha vedanāsañjñābhyām anye caitasikā iti 		gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes kyi phung por bsdus pa rnams ni bshad zin la /
rnam par shes pa'i phung por bsdus pa rnams ni 'og nas 'byung ba de'i tshor ba dang 'du shes gnyis reg pa dang yid la byed pa la sogs pa rnams dang sems las byung ba nyid du bye brag med kyang /
tshor ba dang 'du shes pa las gzhan pa'i sems las byung ba rnams zhes smos pa ni /
vedanāsañjñayoścaitasikatve saty api vedanāsañjñāskandhasaṅgṛhītatvān nasaṃskāraskandhe 'sti saṅgraha iti pradarśanārtham tshor ba dang 'du shes gnyis sems las byung ba nyid yin du zin kyang tshor ba dang 'du shes gnyis phung por bsdus pas 'du byed kyi phung por ma bsdus par bstan pa'i phyir ro /
vedanā hyupabhogavastu tshor ba ni nye bar spyod pa'i dngos po ste /
