tasya vijñaptirgrahaṇam avabodhaḥ pratipattir ityarthaḥ de yang rnam par rig pa ni 'dzin pa dang rtog pa dang khong du chud pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
sā punaḥṣaṭ pravṛttivijñānāni cakṣurvijñānaṃ yāvanmanovijñānaṃ de ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa drug ste mig gi rnam par shes pa nas yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o /
tatracakṣurvijñānaṃ cakṣurindriyāśrayārūpaprativijñaptiḥ de la mig gi rnam par shes pa ni mig gi dbang po la brten nas yul so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
evaṃ yāvan manovijñānaṃmanaindriyāśrayā sarvadharmaprativijñaptiḥ de bzhin du yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i bar du yang yid kyi dbang po la brten nas chos thams cad so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
vijñānasvarūpam uktvā tatparyāyapradarśanārtham āha cittaṃ mano 'pitad iti /
tad vijñānaṃ cittam apy ucyate /
mana ity apīti /
paryāyārthapradarśanārtham āha citratāṃ manaḥsanniśrayatāṃ copādāyeti /
citratāmupādāya cittam ity ucyate /
samanantaracittasanniśrayatāmupādāya mana iti 		rnam par shes pa'i rang gi ngo bo bshad nas /
de'i rnam grangs bstan pa'i phyir /
sems dang yid kyang de yin te /
zhes bya ba smos te /
rnam par shes pa de ni sems zhes kyang bya /
yid ces kyang bya'o /
rnam grangs kyi don bstan pa'i phyir /
sna tshogs pa dang yid rten byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba smos te /
sna tshogs pa'i phyir sems zhes bya'o /
de ma thag pa'i sems kyi rten byed pas yid ces bya'o /
tatrapravṛttivijñānasyālambanaprativijñaptisvarūpatvādālambanasya ca prativijñānam anekākāratvācakṣurādivijñānaṃ citram utpadyate de la 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni dmigs pa so sor rig pa'i rang bzhin yin pa dang dmigs pa so sor rnam par rig pa yang rnam pa du ma yin pa'i phyir /
mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa ni sna tshogs zhes bya'o /
ata eva tadindriyāśrayeṇāpy utpadyamānaṃ viṣayaṃ vijānātīty ucyatenendriyam de'i phyir de'i dbang po la brten nas 'byung ba na yul rnam par shes pa zhes bya'i /
dbang po rnams ni ma yin no /
tathāṣaṇṇāṃ cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ yad yannirudhyatetat tad anantarasyavijñānasyotpadyamānasyāśrayabhāvena vyavatiṣṭhata ity ataḥsamanantaracittasanniśrayatām upādāya mana ity ucyate 'di ltar mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa drug po gang dang gang 'gags pa de dang de ni de ma thag pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i rten gyi dngos por gnas te /
de'i phyir de ma thag pa'i sems kyi rten byed pas yid ces bya'o /
yadetac citratvāc cittam ity uktam taj jātim adhikṛtya nalakṣaṇam sna tshogs pa'i phyir sems zhes bya'o zhes gang bshad pa de ni rigs kyi dbang du byas pa yin gyi skad cig la ni ma yin no /
lakṣaṇaṃ tu pratiniyatālambanākāratvān na citramiti na tat prādhānyena cittam /
prādhānyena punaś /
cittam ālayavijñānam 		skad cig ni dmigs pa so sor nges pa'i rnam pa yin pas sna tshogs zhes mi bya ste /
de ni dngos su sems ma yin no /
dngos su na sems ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ste /
atraiva kāraṇam āha tathāhitac citaṃ sarvasaṃskārabījairiti 'dir rgyu bstan pa'i phyir /
'di ltar de'i 'du byed thams cad kyi sa bon bsags pa'o zhes bya ba smos so /
pratikṣaṇaṃ /
lsarvasaṃskārabījaiś citatvāc cittam itiprādhānyena tad evacittam 		skad cig re re la 'du byed thams cad kyi sa bon bsags pas sems zhes bya ste /
dngos su na de nyid sems so /
cayas tu paunaḥpunyena bījaparipoṣaḥsaṃskārabījānusyūtir vā bsags pa ni yang dang yang sa bon yongs su gsos pa'am /
'du byed kyi sa bon rjes su 'brel ba'o /
saṃskāro 'tra sāsravā dharmāabhipretāḥ /
teṣāṃ punar utpattiś caturbhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ 		'du byed rnams ni 'dir zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams su 'dod de /
de dag kyang rkyen bzhi las 'byung ngo /
tatra hetupratyaya ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā vāsanā de la rgyu'i rkyen ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa'i bag chags te /
paunaḥpunyena saṃskārāṇāṃ samudācārād bījapuṣṭir vāsanety ucyate yang dang yang 'du byed rnams kun du 'byung bas sa bon brtas pa la bag chags zhes bya'o /
adhipatipratyayaś cakṣurādīnīndriyāṇi /
samanantarapratyayaḥ samanantaraniruddhaṃ vijñānam 		bdag po'i rkyen ni mig la sogs pa'i dbang po rnams so /
de ma thag pa'i rkyen ni rnam par shes pa 'gags ma thag pa'o /
ālambanapratyayo rūpādikaḥ dmigs pa'i rkyen ni gzugs la sogs pa'o /
tathā hi sūtre 'py uktam cakṣuraparibhinnaṃ bhavati rūpāṇy ābhāsagatāni tajjaś camanasikāraḥ pratyupasthito bhavati evaṃ tajjasya cakṣurvijñānasya prādurbhāvo bhavatīti 'di ltar mdo las kyang mig nyams par ma gyur la gzugs rnams kyang snang bar gyur pa dang de skyed pa yid la byed pa yang nye bar gnas par gyur na de las byung ba'i mig gi rnam par shes pa 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so /
evaṃśrotrādivijñāneṣv api yathāsambhavaṃ vācyam de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du brjod par bya'o /
hetupratyayastu sadā sannihitatvād durvijñeyatvāc ca noktaḥ rgyu'i rkyen rtag tu gnas pa dang shes par dka' ba'i phyir ma smos so /
de'i 'og tu kun du tshol ba'i yid kyi rnam par shes pa'o /
tadanantaraṃ paryeṣakaṃ manovijñānamparyeṣakād anantaraṃvyavasthāpakam evaṃ vyavasthāpakānantaraṃ vikalpakaṃ manovijñānam utpadyate /
tatra ca viṣayāt saṅkliśyatevyavadāyate vā /
tadavasthaś ca puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyānsaṃskārāṃś cetanātmakān abhisaṃskaroti 		kun du tshol ba'i 'og tu rnam par 'jog pa'o /
rnam par 'jog pa'i 'og tu rnam par rtog pa'i yid kyi rnam par shes pa 'byung ste; de'i tshe yul las kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar 'gyur ro /
de'i tshe bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i 'du byed sems pa'i bdag nyid can rnams mngon par 'du byed do /
te 'bhisaṃskṛtānirudhyamānāālayavijñāne vipākavāsanāṃ vā puṣṇantiniṣyandavāsanāṃ vā mngon par 'du byas pa de dag 'gag pa na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la rnam par smin pa'i bag chags so /
rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags gso bar byed do /
tatra niṣyandavāsanāmāgamyālayavijñānāt puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyāḥ saṃskārāḥpravartante de la rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags la brten nas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i 'du byed rnams 'byung ngo /
vipākavāsanām āgamyālayavijñānānnikāyasabhāgāntareṣv ālayavijñānam eva vipākātmakaṃnirvartate rnam par smin pa'i bag chags la brten nas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid rnam par smin pa'i bdag nyid du 'grub bo /
tatra ye 'py anye 'kuśalāḥ kuśalasāsravāś ca dharmāsteṣām apy ayam eva nayaḥ de la mi dge ba dang dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos gzhan gang yin pa de dag la yang tshul 'di nyid do /
avyākṛtās tu niṣyandavāsanām evapuṣṇanti na vipākavāsanām teṣām avipākatvāt lung du ma bstan pa ni rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags nyid gso bar byed kyi /
rnam par smin pa'i bag chags ni ma yin te /
de dag la rnam par smin pa med pa'i phyir ro /
tad evamālayavijñānaṃ dviprakāram de ltar na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa de rnam pa gnyis te /
niṣyandavāsanām upādāyakāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags la brten nas rgyu dang 'bras bu ste /
tathā hi sarvasaṃskārāḥ svabījādhānevartamānā ālayavijñānātmātiśayahetubhāvena vyavatiṣṭhantaitisarvasaṃskārāṇāṃ tat kāryam 'di ltar 'du byed thams cad rang gi sa bon bskyed pa ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa rang bzhin bye brag tu 'gyur ba'i rgyu'i dngos por gnas pas de ni 'du byed rnams kyi 'bras bu'o /
sarvasaṃskārāś catadbījopādānād ālayavijñānād utpadyanta itisarvasaṃskārāṇām ālayavijñānaṃ kāraṇam 'du byed thams cad de dag gi sa bon nye bar len pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las 'byung ba'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni 'du byed thams cad kyi rgyu yin no /
vipākavāsanāṃ tvadhikṛtya kuśalākuśalānāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ kāryam eva tatnakāraṇam rnam par smin pa'i bag chags kyi dbang du byas te /
dge ba dang mi dge ba'i 'du byed rnams kyi 'bras bu yin gyi rgyu ni ma yin no /
kāraṇaṃ tu tad vipākavāsanām upādāyanikāyasabhāgāntareṣu vipākavijñānasyaiveti rgyu ni rnam par smin pa'i bag chags la brten nas ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa'i rgyu'o /
pravṛttivijñānaṃ hi rūpaśabdādyālambanatvātsvasāmānyalakṣaṇākāratvāc caparicchinnālambanaṃ paricchinnākāraṃ ca 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni gzugs dang sgra la sogs pa la dmigs pa dang rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid kyi rnam pa yin pa'i phyir dmigs pa yongs su chad pa dang rnam shes yongs su chad pa'o /
ālayavijñānaṃ punaraparicchinnālambanākāram kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni dmigs pa dang rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa ste /
na hy asyālambanaṃ paricchettuṃ śakyatenākāraḥ /
kiṃ kāraṇam 		'di'i dmigs pa dang rnam pa yongs su gcad par mi nus so /
ci'i phyir zhe na /
yasmādālayavijñānaṃ dvābhyām ālambanābhyāṃ pravartate 'di ltar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni dmigs pa gnyis la 'jug pa ste /
adhyātmam upādānavijñaptitaḥbahirdhāparicchinnākārabhājanavijñaptitaś ca nang gi nye bar len pa'i rnam par rig pa dang phyi rol gyi snod la rnam par rig pa rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa'o /
tatrādhyātmamupādānaṃ parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśavāsanā sādhiṣṭhānaṃ cendriyarūpam de la nang gi nye bar len pa ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la mngon par zhen pa'i bag chags dang gnas dang bcas pa'i dbang po'i gzugs so /
etaccālambanaṃ sūkṣmatvāllokapaṇḍitair apiduravadhāram ity ato 'paricchinnālambanākāram ity ucyate napunar anālambanam eva dmigs pa 'di gnyis ni phra ba'i phyir 'jig rten gyi mkhas pa rnams kyis kyang rtogs par dka' bas de'i phyir dmigs pa dang rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa zhes bya'i /
pravṛttivijñānaṃ kuśalakliṣṭāvyākṛtajātīyam ālayavijñānaṃ tvekajātīyam dmigs pa med pa nyid ni ma yin no /
'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni dge ba dang nyon mongs pa can dang lung du ma bstan pa'i rang bzhin no /
kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni rigs gcig pa yin no /
tatra na tāvat kuśalākuśalajātīyaṃ /
kuśalākuśalair asamprayogāt 		de la dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rang bzhin ni ma yin te /
de dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
tad dhi pañcabhir evasarvatragaiś caitasaiḥ samprayujyatemanaskārasparśavedanāsañjñācetanābhiḥ de ni sems las byung ba kun du 'gro ba yid la byed pa dang reg pa dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa lnga po kho na dang mtshungs par ldan no /
ālayavijñānaṃsasamprayogaṃ pūrvakarmasaṃskārahetukatvād ekāntenavipāka evety avyākṛtajātīyam eva /
santānānuvṛtti ca 		kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas par sngon gyi las kyi 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung bas gcig tu rnam par smin pa nyid yin pa'i phyir lung du ma bstan pa'i rigs so /
atra hyālayavijñānaṃnikāyasabhāgāntareṣu pratisandhim upādāya yāvac cyutiṃtāvat kṣaṇaprabandhapravāhena vartate na tv antarāntarāvicchidyate pravṛttivijñānavat rgyun chags par 'jug pa'o /
de la kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu nying mtshams sbyor ba nas bzung ste /
ji tsam na 'chi 'pho ba de'i bar du skad cig rgyun mi 'chad par 'jug gi /
'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa bzhin du bar skabs bar skabs su chad pa ni ma yin te /
tathā hi cakṣurvijñānānantaraṃśrotrādivijñānāny utpadyante śrotravijñānānantaraṃcakṣurādivijñānāni /
evaṃ ghrāṇādivijñānānantaram itivistareṇa vācyam 		'di ltar mig gi rnam par shes pa'i 'og tu rna ba la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung ba dang rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'i 'og tu mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung ba dang de bzhin du sna la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i 'og tu zhes bya ba rgya cher brjod par bya'o /
tathā kuśalānantaram akuśalam utpadyateakuśalānantaraṃ kuśalam tadubhayānantaram avyākṛtamhīnadhātukānantaraṃ madhyadhātukammadhyadhātukānantaraṃ praṇītadhātukampraṇītadhātukānantaram apraṇītadhātukamapraṇītadhātukānantaraṃ madhyadhātukam iti vistareṇavācyam de bzhin du dge ba'i 'og tu mi dge ba 'byung ba dang mi dge ba'i 'og tu dge ba dang de gnyis ka'i 'og tu lung du mi ston pa dang khams dman pa'i 'og tu khams bar ma dang khams bar ma'i 'og tu khams gya nom pa dang khams gya nom pa'i 'og tu gya nom pa ma yin pa dang khams gya nom pa ma yin pa'i 'og tu khams bar ma zhes bya ba rgya cher brjod par bya ste /
nāpy ekaṃ dravyam ā maraṇād anuvartata iti shi ba la thug gi bar du rdzas gcig tu 'jug pa ni ma yin no /
ṣaṭprakārapravṛttivijñānavyatiriktam anyad ālayavijñānamastīti katham vijñāyate /
āgamato yuktitaś ca 		'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa drug po ma gtogs par gzhan kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yod par ci mngon zhe na /
lung dang rigs pas mngon no /
tatrāgama uktaṃbhagavatābhidharmasūtre anādikāliko dhātuḥ sarvadharmasamāśrayaḥ de la ni 'di ni lung yin te /
bcom ldan 'das kyis chos mngon pa'i mdo las /
thog ma med pa'i dus kyi dbyings /
chos rnams kun gyi gnas yin te /
tasmin sati gatiḥ sarvā nirvāṇādhigamo 'pica de yod pas na 'gro kun dang /
mya ngan 'das pa'ang thob par 'gyur /
zhes gsungs so /
punaś ca sandhinirmocane 'py uktam ādānavijñāna gambhīrasūkṣmo ogho yathā vartati sarvabījaḥ /
bālāna eṣo mayi na prakāśito mā haiva ātmā parikalpayeyuḥ 		yang dgongs ba nges par 'grel ba'i mdo las kyang /
len pa'i rnam par shes pa zab cing phra /
sa bon thams cad chu bo'i rgyun bzhin 'bab /
bdag tu rtog par gyur na mi rung zhes /
'di ni byis pa rnams la ngas ma bstan /
zhes gsungs so /
yuktim apy adhikṛtyāha yatonirodhasamāpattyasañjñisamāpattyāsañjñik /
ebhyo vyutthitasya punarviṣayavijñaptyākhyaṃ pravṛttivijñānam /
utpadyate 		rigs pa'i dbang du byas te /
'di ltar 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa po rnams las langs nas yang yul rnam par rig pa zhes bya ba 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung /
tad ālayavijñānaṃ pravṛttivijñānebhyo'rthāntaram iti vākyaśeṣaḥ zhes bya ba smos te /
kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams las don gzhan du gyur pa'o zhes bya ba tshig gi lhag ma'o /
nirodhāsañjñisamāpattisamāpannasyāsañjñike ca prādurbhūteniravaśeṣeṣu pravṛttivijñāneṣu niruddheṣu punarvyutthānakālaālayavijñānam antareṇa pravṛttivijñānotpattir na yujyate /
na hisamāpatticittāt tasyotpattir yuktā tasya ciraniruddhatvānniruddhasya cāsattvāt asac ca na kāryaṃ na kāraṇaṃpradhānātmādivat /
yo 'pi manyate anapāyopādānavikāraṃbhāvasvarūpam /
anāgatavartamānātītatvaṃ tu bhāvānāṃkāritradvārakam /
tathā hy akurvatkāritro 'nāgataḥkurvatkāritro vartamānaḥ uparatakāritro 'tīta ity ucyate /
evaṃtarhi kāritraṃ bhāvād anyad ityabhyupagantavyamatītānāgatāvasthayoḥkāritre 'saty api bhāvābhyupagamāt /
evaṃ ca kāritrasyaivotpādo vyayaś ca na bhāvānām abhūtvābhāvād bhūtvā cābhāvāt na carūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānām sarvadāsvarūpādhyāsitatvāt 		'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa par gyur pa na 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams ma lus par 'gag pa las yang ldang ba'i tshe kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung du mi rung ngo /
snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems las de 'byung du mi rung ste /
de 'gags nas ring du lon pa dang 'gags pa de med pa'i phyir ro /
med pa ni rgyur yang mi rung 'bras bur yang mi rung ste /
gtso bo dang bdag la sogs pa bzhin no /
gang yang 'di snyam du dngos po'i rang gi ngo bo la skye ba dang 'jig par 'gyur ba'i dngos po med kyi ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar dang 'das pa ni dngos po rnams kyi byed pa'i sgo nas yin te /
'di ltar bya ba mi byed pa ni ma 'ongs pa'o /
bya ba byed pa ni da ltar ro /
byed ba rgyun chad pa ni 'das pa'o zhes bya'o snyam du sems pa de lta bu yin na ni byed pa las dngos po gzhan yin par khas blang bar bya ste /
'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa gnyis kyi dus na byed pa med kyang dngos po khas len pa'i phyir ro /
de ltar na med pa las byung ba dang byung nas kyang med par 'gyur ba'i phyir 'byung ba dang 'jig pa ni byed pa yin gyi /
dngos po rnams kyis ni ma yin no /
gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams kyis ma yin pa nyid de /
tataś cotpādavyayābhāvān nirodhavannānityā rūpādayaḥ skandhāḥ syuḥ rtag tu rang gi ngo bo dang ldan pa dang de yang 'byung ba dang 'jig pa med ba'i phyir te /
gzugs la sogs pa'i phung po rnams ni 'gog pa bzhin du mi rtag pa ma yin par 'gyur ro /
tataś ca duḥkhā api na syuḥ de'i phyir sdug bsngal bar yang mi 'gyur te /
uktaṃ hi sūtre yad anityaṃ tad duḥkhamiti mdo las ni mi rtag pa gang yin pa de sdug bsngal ba'o zhes gsungs so /
evaṃ caskandhān anityato duḥkhataś ca cintayato viparyāsa evasyāt de lta na ni phung po rnams la ni mi rtag pa nyid dang sdug bsngal ba nyid du sems pa phyin ci log nyid du 'gyur ro /
na ca viparyāsāt kleśaprahāṇaṃ yuktam anitye duḥkhe canityasukhaviparyāsavat phyin ci log gis ni nyon mongs pa spang bar mi rigs te /
mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba la rtag pa dang bde bar phyin ci log pa bzhin no /
kāritrasya cotpādavyayasambhavāt saṃskṛtatvam rūpādiṣu ca skandheṣusaṅgrahābhāvāt ṣaṣṭhaḥskandho 'bhyupagantavyaḥ byed pa la ni 'byung ba dang 'jig pa yod pas 'dus byas nyid yin te /
gzugs la sogs pa'i phung po rnams su ni ma 'dus pas phung po drug par khas blang bar bya'o /
na ca sāsravā dharmāupādānaskandhaiḥ sarve vā saṃskṛtāḥ skandhaiḥ saṅgṛhītā itivaktavyam yang nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams kyis zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad dang phung po rnams kyis 'dus byas thams cad bsdus so zhes ma zer cig /
anyaḥ punar āha kāritraṃ nāma phalaparigrahaḥ yang gzhan na re byed pa zhes bya ba ni 'bras bu yongs su 'dzin pa'o /
dharmo hi yasya dharmasya hetubhāvena vyavatiṣṭhatesa dharmas taṃdharmaṃ phalatvena gṛhṇātīty ato hetubhāvavyavasthānaṃbhāvānāṃ phalaparigrahaḥ /
hetubhāvena ca sa eva dharmo vyavatiṣṭhata itidharmebhyaḥ kāritram ananyat 		chos gang zhig chos gang gi rgyu dngos por gnas pa ste /
chos dang chos de 'bras bur 'dzin pa de'i phyir rgyu'i dngos por gnas pa ni dngos po rnams kyi 'bras bu yongs su 'dzin te /
chos de nyid rgyu'i dngos por gnas pas na chos rnams las byed pa gzhan ma yin no /
ataś canānantaroktadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ /
ananyo hi nāma sa eva /
etad uktaṃ bhavati nānyat kāritraṃ dharmāt kiṃ tarhi dharma eva kāritram /
tathā kāritrān nānyo dharmaḥ /
kāritram evadharma iti /
evaṃ cātītānāgatayor adhvanoḥ kāritravaddharmābhāvaḥ 		de bas na gong du smos pa'i skyon du mi 'gyur ro zhes zer ro /
gzhan ma yin zhes bya ba ni de nyid de /
de ni 'di skad du chos las byed pa gzhan ma yin te /
chos nyid byed pa'o /
de bzhin du byed pa las kyang chos gzhan ma yin te /
byed pa nyid chos yin no zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
de lta na ni 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa gnyis kyis chos rnams byed pa bzhin du med par 'gyur te /
tataś cātītānāgatāstitvavādaḥ parityaktobhavati de'i phyir 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa yod do zhes smras pa btang ba yin no /
kāritrasya vā dharmasvarūpavad dharmād ananyatvāttraiyadhvakatvam abhyupagantavyam yang na byed pa yang chos kyi rang gi ngo bo bzhin du chos las gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir dus gsum par khas blang dgos te /
evam apikāritreṇādhvāno vyavasthitā iti vādahāniḥ /
kāritraṃ ca kurvanvartamāna iṣyate /
anyac cānyena kriyate na svātmanaivatasya kṛtatvāt /
akṛtaṃ ca kriyate na kṛtam 		de lta na yang byed pa las dus rnams rnam par gzhag par smra ba nyams par 'gyur ro /
bya ba byed pa ni da ltar du 'dod de /
gzhan ni gzhan gyis byed pa la /
de byas zin pa'i phyir bdag nyid kyis ni ma yin no /
ma byas pa ni byed dgos kyi byas zin pa la ni ma yin no /
ataś cadharmakāritrayoḥ kṛtākṛtatvāt spaṣṭam anyatvam /
tasmātpūrvoktadoṣas tadavastha eva 		de'i phyir byed pa dang chos gnyis ni byas pa dang ma byas pa ma yin pas tha dad par mngon no; /
de lta bas na gong du smos pa'i skyon de yod do /
dharmakāritrayoś cānanyatvehetuphalābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ chos dang byed pa gnyis kyang tha dad pa ma yin na ni rgyu dang 'bras bu med par 'gyur te /
tathā hi phalasya kāraṇavat pūrvameva pariniṣpannatvāt phalasya kiṃ kurvat kāraṇaṃ bhavatiakurvad vā kathaṃ kāraṇam /
phalam api tenākriyamāṇaṃkathaṃ tasya kāryaṃ bhavati 		'di ltar 'bras bu yang rgyu bzhin du thog ma nyid nas yongs su grub pa'i phyir 'bras bu la ji zhig byed na rgyur 'gyur /
mi byed na yang rgyu zhes ji skad du bya 'bras bu yang des ma byas na de'i 'bras bur ji ltar 'gyur /
kāritrāṇām eva ca parasparatohetuphalabhāvaḥ na dharmāṇām byed pa rnams nyid phan tshun rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos por 'gyur gyi /
chos rnams kyi ni ma yin te /
tathā hi kāritre satikāritrāntaraṃ bhavatināsati 'di ltar byed pa yod na byed pa gzhan 'byung gi med na ni ma yin te /
na tu dharmasvarūpam nāpidharmasvarūpād dharmasvarūpam sarvadāstitvāt /
tathā cayasmin sati yad bhavati asati ca na bhavatitat tasya kāraṇamitarac ca kāryam 		chos kyi rang bzhin la ni ma yin no /
chos kyi rang bzhin las kyang chos kyi rang bzhin ma yin te /
rtag tu yod pa'i phyir ro /
de ltar na gang yod na gang 'byung gi med na ni mi 'byung ba de ni de'i rgyu yin no /
lokaprasiddham etat /
evaṃ ca nadharmasvarūpaṃ kāraṇaṃ na kāryam iti lokaśāstravirodhaḥ /
kāritraṃ dharmasya tattvānyatvenāvācyam ity anye /
kimarthaṃ tattvenāvācyam /
dharmasvabhāvaṃ na bhavatīti 		cig shos ni 'bras bu yin no zhes bya ba 'di ni 'jig rten gyi grags pa'o /
de ltar na chos kyi rang bzhin ni rgyu yang ma yin 'bras bu yang ma yin pa ni 'jig rten pa dang bstan bcos dang 'gal lo /
gzhan dag na re chos rnams las byed pa de nyid dang gzhan du brjod par bya ba ma yin no zhes zer te /
ci'i phyir de nyid ces mi brjod ce na /
chos kyi rang bzhin ma yin pa'i phyir ro; /
kimartham anyatvena nocyate /
anyasvabhāvam api tan naivetyanyatvenāpi nocyate 		ci'i phyir gzhan zhes mi brjod ce na /
chos kyi rang bzhin de'i ngo bo nyid yang ma yin pas gzhan zhes mi bya'o /
evaṃ tarhi yan na tatsvabhāvaṃ nānyasvabhāvam tac chaśaviṣāṇavan niḥsvabhāvatvān nāstyeveti /
katham avidyamānam adhvavyavasthānimittaṃbhaviṣyati 		de lta na ni gang de'i ngo bo nyid kyang ma yin la gzhan gyi ngo bo nyid kyang ma yin pa de ni ri bong gi rva bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir med pa nyid yin te /
med pa ni dus rnam par gzhag pa'i rgyur ji ltar 'gyur /
evaṃ kāritrāt sarvathāpy adhvavyavasthā nasidhyati /
tasmād anutpanno bhāvo 'nāgataḥ niruddho 'tītaḥutpannāniruddho vartamāna ity abhyupeyam 		de ltar na byed pa las dus rnam par gzhag pa ni rnam pa thams cad du mi 'grub bo /
de lta bas na dngos po ma byung ba ni ma 'ongs pa yin /
'gags pa ni 'das pa yin /
byung lam 'gags pa ni de ltar yin par khas blang bar bya'o /
na punar akurvatkāritro 'nāgataḥ kurvatkāritro vartamānaḥuparatakāritro 'tīta iti bya ba mi byed pa ni ma 'ongs pa /
bya ba byed pa ni da ltar /
byed pa rgyun chad pa ni 'das pa'o zhes khas blang bar mi bya'o /
anyaḥ punar āha sendriyaṃ rūpaṃ cittaṃ cānyonyabījakamity ato nirodhāsañjñisamāpattibhyām asañjñikāc cavyuttiṣṭhataḥ sendriyād rūpāc cittam utpadyate yang gzhan dag na re dbang po dang bcas pa'i gzugs dang sems ni gcig gi sa bon gcig yin te /
de'i phyir 'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa las ldang ba na dbang po dang bcas ba'i gzugs las sems 'byung ste /
yathārūpyadhātoś cyavamānasya cittād eva ciraniruddham api sendriyaṃ rūpam utpadyata iti /
tasmān nātra kiñcid ālayavijñānena prayojanam iti 		dper na gzugs med pa'i khams nas 'chi 'pho ba'i sems las kyang 'gags nas ring du lon ba dbang po dang bcas pa'i gzugs 'byung ba lta bu'o /
de lta bas na 'di la kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ca dgos zhes zer te /
evaṃ tarhy ekaikasya sattvasyadvau cittasantānau syātām /
ekaḥ sendriyād rūpāt aparaś cittāt 		de ltar na sems can re re'i sems kyi rgyud kyang gnyis gnyis su 'gyur te /
gcig ni dbang po dang bcas pa'i gzugs las byung /
cig shos ni sems las 'byung bar 'gyur ro /
ārūpyeṣu ca nirodhasamāpannasya rūpābhāvādvyutthānābhāvaḥ gzugs med pa'i sems su 'gog pa la snyoms par zhugs pa ni gzugs med pas ldang ba yang med do /
tataś cāsya parinirvāṇam eva syād ityakalpaneyam de'i phyir 'di ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa nyid du 'gyur bas rtog pa 'di ni mi rung ngo /
ekaṃ ca kāraṇaṃ svasattādhyāsitaṃ nirīhamanityaṃ śaktaṃ ceṣyate na viparyāsāt rgyu ni bdag yod pa dang ldan zhing gyo ba med la mi rtag cing nus pa yod pa gcig pur 'dod kyi /
bzlog pa ni ma yin no /
tathā hy uktaṃbhagavatā asmin satīdaṃ bhavati asyotpādād idamutpadyate /
yad utāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā iti /
tasmān na nityohetuḥ nāpy asan na sadvyāpāro nāpy aśaktaiti /
ālayavijñānaṃhi sarvasaṃskṛtadharmabījānugatam ā maraṇāt santānavṛtticety ālayavijñānād evācittakāvasthāto vyuttiṣṭhataḥpravṛttivijñānam utpadyata iti 		de skad du bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'di yod pa'i phyir 'di 'byung /
'di skye ba'i phyir 'di skye ste /
'di ltar ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes gsungs te /
de lta bas na rgyu rtag pa ma yin zhing med pa yang ma yin la /
byed pa yod pa yang ma yin zhing nus pa med pa yang ma yin no /
kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni 'dus byas kyi chos thams cad kyi sa bon dang ldan pa ste /
shi ba la thug gi bar du rgyun chags par 'byung ba'o /
sems med pa'i gnas las ldang ba na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid las 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ste /
sūtre ca nirodhasamāpannasyavijñānaṃ kāyād anapakrāntamity uktam /
na cālayavijñānādanyasya nirodhasamāpattyavasthāyāṃ vijñānasya kāyādanapakramo yujyate /
kiṃ kāraṇam 		mdo las kyang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa lus las mi 'da'o zhes gsungs so /
snyoms par zhugs pa'i dus na rnam par shes pa lus las mi 'da' ba ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las gzhan mi rung ngo /
ci'i phyir zhe na /
nirodhasamāpannasyālayavijñānād yadyanyavijñānasamudācāra iṣyate tataś catrayāṇāṃ sannipātaḥsparśaḥ sparśasahajā vedanā sañjñā cetaneti sūtre vacanātsañjñāvedanayor api samudācāro 'bhyupagantavyaḥ gal te 'gog pa la snyoms par zhugs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las gzhan zhig kun du 'byung bar 'dod na /
de lta na ni gsum 'dus pa'i rig pa dang reg pa dang lhan cig skyes pa'i tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa zhes mdo las gsungs pa'i phyir 'du shes dang tshor ba gnyis kyang kun du 'byung bar khas blang dgos so /
tataś cavedanāsañjñāsadbhāvāt sañjñāveditanirodha eva na syāt de'i phyir 'du shes dang tshor ba yod pas 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa nyid du mi 'gyur ro /
yo 'pimanyate sūtrevedanāpratyayā tṛṣṇāuktā na ca sarvā vedanātṛṣṇāyāḥ pratyayaḥ gang yang mdo las tshor ba'i rkyen gyis sred pa zhes gsungs pa yang tshor ba thams cad sred pa'i rkyen ma yin te /
evaṃ sparśo 'pi na sarvaḥsañjñāvedanāpratyaya iti nāyaṃ doṣaḥ /
naitad evam 		de bzhin du reg pa thams cad kyang 'du shes dang tshor ba'i rkyen ma yin pas nyes pa med do snyam du sems pa de yang de lta ma yin te /
viśeṣitā hivedanā sūtrāntare avidyāsaṃsparśajaṃ veditaṃpratītyotpannā tṛṣṇeti /
na tv evaṃ kvacit sparśo viśeṣita ity asamānam etat 		mdo gzhan las ma rig pa dang ldan pa'i reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba la brten nas sred pa 'byung zhes bye brag tu mdzad kyi reg pa ni gang du yang de ltar bye brag mi mdzad pa 'di mtshungs pa ma yin no /
tasmād avaśyam ālayavijñānād evasarvabījakāt sarvāsv avasthāsu santānena vartamānānnirodhāsañjñisamāpattyāsañjñikebhyo vyutthānacittamutpadyata ity abhyupeyam de lta bas na 'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa pa rnams las ldang ba na gdon mi za bar kun gzhi rnam par shes pas sa bon thams cad gnas skabs kun du 'byung ba las skye bar khas blang bar bya'o /
punaś cālambanapratyayāpekṣāṃ prakārāntaravṛttitām upādāyapravṛttivijñānād /
ālayavijñānam anyad iti pratipattavyam /
upādāyety ante 'padiṣṭam ihāpi sambadhyate 		dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltos nas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid kyi phyir 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yod par khong du chud par bya'o /
phyir ro zhes tha mar bstan pa ni 'dir yang sbyar ro /
ālambanapratyayaḥ pañcānāṃcakṣurādivijñānānāṃ rūpādayaḥ pañca viṣayāḥmanovijñānasya sarvadharmāḥ dmigs pa'i rkyen ni mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa lnga dang yul gzugs la sogs pa lnga'i yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i chos thams cad do /
rūpādyākārāc chabdādyākāraḥ prakārāntaram gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam pa las sgra la sogs pa'i rnam pa ni rnam pa gzhan no /
evaṃ śabdādyākārād rūpādyākāraḥ /
pītādyākārān nīlādyākāraḥ prakārāntaram 		de bzhin du sgra la sogs pa'i rnam pa las gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang ser po la sogs pa'i rnam pa las sngon po la sogs pa'i rnam pa ni rnam pa gzhan no /
evaṃ sarvatravistareṇa vācyam de ltar kun du yang rgya cher brjod par bya'o /
prakārāntareṇa vṛttir ātmalābho'syavijñānasyeti tad vijñānaṃ prakārāntaravṛtti /
tadbhāvaḥprakārāntaravṛttitā 		rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa bdag thob pa ni rnam par shes pa 'di'i yin pas rnam par shes pa de ni rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa ste de yod pas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid do /
ālambanapratyayāpekṣā kāraṇaṃ yasyāḥprakārāntaravṛttitāyāḥ sālambanapratyayāpekṣā tādṛśīṃprakārāntaravṛttitām upādāya gṛhītvā pravṛttivijñānād anyadālayavijñānaṃ pravṛttivijñānabījabhūtam astīti vijñāyate de dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltos pa'i rgyus rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa gang gi yin pad de dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltos nas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid do /
nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni bzung nas 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yod par shes so /
atrahi vijñānaṃ pratyavabhāsabhedāt parasparato bhidyate nasamanantarādhipatipratyayabhedāt /
ata etad evam uktam ālambanapratyayāpekṣāṃ prakārāntaravṛttitām upādāya 		'dir ni rnam par shes pa rnams dmigs pa so sor snang ba tha dad pas phan tshun tha dad kyi de ma thag pa dang bdag po'i rkyen tha dad pas ni ma yin no /
de'i phyir 'di skad du dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltas nas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bshad do /
sācaprakārāntaravṛttitā yathā nālambananirapekṣā yujyate tathāhetupratyayanirapekṣāpi naiva yujyate rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid de yang ji ltar dmigs pa la mi ltos par mi rung ba de bzhin du rgyu'i rkyen la mi ltos par mi rung ba nyid do /
yaś ca yeṣāṃ bījairanugataḥ sa teṣāṃ hetupratyayaḥ gang dag gi sa bon rnams dang ldan pa gang yin pa de ni de dag gi spyi'i rkyen te /
na ca pravṛttivijñānānāṃparasparabījatvaṃ yujyate kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtānāṃhīnamadhyapraṇītadhātūnāṃ laukikalokottarāṇāṃsāsravānāsravāṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ paryāyeṇa bhāvāt 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams ni gcig gi sa bon du gcig mi rung ngo /
dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams dang dman pa dang 'bring dang gya nom pa'i khams pa rnams dang 'jig rten pa rnams dang 'jig rten las 'das pa rnams dang zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams la rim pa yod pa'i phyir ro /
de nyid kyi bag chags bsgo ba yang ma mthong la /
na hitenaiva tasya vāsanā dṛṣṭā nāpy anyenabhinnakālenāsambaddhena vā kiṃ tarhi sahotpādavināśair evapuṣpādibhis tilādīnāṃ vāsanā dṛṣṭā gzhan gyi dus gzhan na yang ma yin zhing 'brel pa med par yang ma yin no /
'on kyang lhan cig 'byung ba dang 'jig pa nyid kyi me tog la sogs pas 'bru mar rnams la bsgo bar mthong ste /
ato vipākavāsanāvijñānena samakālaṃ tata evotpadyamānāninirudhyamānāni capravṛttivijñānāni svānurūpakāryotpādanasamarthaṃvipākavijñānaṃ kurvanti de'i phyir rnam par smin pa'i bag chags kyi rnam par shes pa dang dus mtshungs pa de nyid las 'byung ba dang 'gag pa ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams rang dang mthun pa'i 'bras bu skyed nus ba rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa la byed do /
tasya sāmarthyaṃ vāsanety ucyate de'i nus pa ni bag chags zhes bya'o /
taiś ca prakārāntaravṛttibhiḥ pravṛttivijñānair vāsitādvipākavijñānāt punar apy ālambanāpekṣāṇi kuśalākuśalādiprakārāntaravṛttīni pravṛttivijñānāny utpadyantaity avaśyam abhyupagantavyam /
tataś ca vipākavijñānaṃsarvasaṃskṛtadharmabījānugataṃ pravṛttivijñānebhyo 'nyad itisiddham 		'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa dang dus rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa de dag gis bsras [?] pa rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa las yang dmigs pa la ltos pa dge ba dang mi dge ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung bar gdon mi za bar khas blang bar bya'o /
de'i phyir 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams las rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa 'dus byas kyi chos thams cad kyi sa bon dang ldan pa gzhan yin par grub pa'o /
chinnapunarvṛttitāṃ copādāyālayavijñānaṃ pravṛttivijñānebhyo 'nyad astīti pratipattavyam chad nas 'byung ba'i phyir 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yin par khong du chud par bya'o /
acittakamiddhamūrchādyavasthāsu cchinnepravṛttivijñānasantāne punar acittakamiddhamūrchāpagataālayavijñānam antareṇa pravṛttivijñānotpattir na yujyate /
nirodhasamāpattyādivyutthānacittavad ihāpi vicāraḥkartavyaḥ 		sems med pa'i gnyid kyis log pa dang brgyal ba la sogs pa 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rgyun chad pa las yang sems med pa'i nyid kyis log pa dang brgyal ba las sangs pa na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med pa'i 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung bar mi rung ngo /
'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa las ldang ba'i sems dang 'dra bar 'dir yang dpyad par bya'o /
saṃsārapravṛttinivṛttitāṃcopādāya /
pravṛttivijñānād anyad ālayavijñānam yannimittāsaṃsārapravṛttir nivṛttiś ca gamyate 		'khor bar 'jug pa dang ldog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni gang gi rgyu las byung ba'i 'khor bar 'jug pa dang ldog pa yod pas 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yin par shes so /
kṣaṇāvasthānikāyasabhāganairantaryaprabandhenopādānaskandhotpādaḥ saṃsāra ity ucyate skad cig kyang mi gnas par ris mthun pa rgyun mi 'chad ba'i rgyun gyi nye bar len pa'i phung po 'byung ba ni 'khor ba zhes bya'o /
tasya punaḥpravṛttirnikāyasabhāgāntareṣu pratisandhiḥ de'i 'jug pa ni ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu nying mtshams sbyor ba'o /
nivṛttiḥ sopadhiśeṣonirupadhiśeṣaś ca nirvāṇadhātuḥ ldog pa ni phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa dang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings so /
tatr ālay avij ñānā nabh yupa gamesaṃskārapratyayavijñānābhāvāt saṃsārapravṛttir na yujyate de la kun gzhi rnam par shes pa khas mi len na 'du byed kyi rgyu rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba med pa'i phyir 'khor bar 'jug bar mi rung ngo /
kun gzhi rnam par shes pa khas mi len na /
ālayavijñānānabhyupagame hi pratisandhivijñānaṃ vāsaṃskārapratyayaṃ parikalpyeta saṃskāraparibhāvitā vā ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥsaṃskārapratyayaṃ vijñānam 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa zhes 'byung ba nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes pa 'am /
'du byed kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug 'du byed kyi rkyen las byung bar brtag grang na /
tatra napratisandhivijñānaṃ pūrvajanmopacitasaṃskārapratyayampūrvajanmopacitasaṃskārāṇāṃciraniruddhatvāt niruddhasya cāsattvāt asataś ca pratyayābhāvāt de'i tshe nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes pa ni tshe snga ma la bsags pa'i 'du byed kyi rkyen las byung ba ma yin te /
tshe snga ma la bsags pa'i 'du byed ni 'gags nas ring du lon pa'i phyir ro /
'gags pa ni med pa'i phyir ro /
yadi niruddhasyapratyayatvaṃ neṣyate evaṃ ca saty aphalam eva karma syātna hi vartamānāt karmaṇo vipāko nirvartate /
naitad evam tajjabhāvanāvasthānāt /
karmāhitāyāś cittasantāne vāsanāyāḥparipākaviśeṣaṃ gatāyā vipāko nirvartate 		med pa ni rkyen du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
gal te 'gags pa rkyen du mi 'dod na de ltar na /
da ltar gyi las las ni rnam par smin pa mngon par mi 'grub pa las kyi 'bras bu med pa nyid du 'gyur ro /
de ni de lta ma yin te /
de las byung ba'i bsgos pa gnas pa'i phyir ro /
gang las 'gyur ba bye brag tu gyur nas rnam par smin pa 'grub pa'i bag chags las kyis bskyed pa sems kyi rgyud la yod do /
tasmān na viphalaṃkarma na ca niruddhāt karmaṇo vipāka iti /
pratisandhau canāmarūpam eva na kevalaṃ vijñānam 		de lta bas na las kyi 'bras bu med pa ma yin la /
las 'gags pa las rnam par smin pa 'byung ba yang ma yin no /
nying mtshams sbyor ba'i tshe ni ming dang gzugs kyi yin te /
tatra vijñānam evasaṃskārapratyayam na ca nāmarūpam iti kātra yuktiḥ rnam par shes pa 'ba' zhig ni ma yin na /
de la rnam par shes pa nyid 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung gi /
ming dang gzugs ni ma yin no zhes bya ba 'di la rigs pa ci yod /
tasmāt saṃskārapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam iti vaktayam natu vijñānamiti /
katamad vānyad vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam 		de lta bas na 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs zhes brjod par bya'i /
rnam par shes pa ma yin no zhes brjod pa'o /
rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs zhes bya ba gzhan gang zhe na /
yatpratisandhikṣaṇād uttarakālam /
tasya prātisandhikānnāmarūpāt ka ātmātiśayo yatas tad eva vijñānapratyayaṃ napūrvam pūrvaṃ ca saṃskārapratyayaṃ nottaram ity ataś ca saṃskārapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam evāstu /
kiṃpratisandhivijñānenāṅgāntareṇa parikalpitena /
tasmān napratisandhivijñānaṃ saṃskārapratyayaṃ yujyate /
gsaṃskārās tv avidyāpratyayāḥ /
tadadhivāsitaṃ ca vijñānaṃsaṃskārapratyayam /
tatpratyayaṃ pratisandhau ca nāmarūpamevety eṣaiva nītir niravadyā 		nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i skad cig las dus phyi ma gang yin pa'o zhe na /
de nying mtshams sbyor ba'i ming dang gzugs las rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa ci yod na /
'di ltar de nyid rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis byung ba yin la /
snga ma ni 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung ba yin la /
phyi ma ni ma yin te de'i phyir 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs nyid du 'gyur gyi /
nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes ba'i yan lag gzhan kun du brtags pas ci zhig bya /
de lta bas na nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes pa ni 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung bar mi rung ngo /
'du byed rnams ni ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis byung ba yin la des bsgos pa'i rnam par shes pa ni 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung ba dang de'i rkyen gyis byung ba nying mtshams sbyor ba ni ming dang gzugs nyid do zhes bya ba'i tshul 'di la ni nyes pa med do /
ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥsaṃskāraparibhāvitāḥ saṃskārapratyayam vijñānam ity ayamapi pakṣo durghaṭita eva /
kiṃ kāraṇam 		rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po 'du byed kyis yongs su bsgos pa dag 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i phyogs 'di yang sbyar ma legs pa nyid de /
ci'i phyir zhe na /
na hi vijñānaṃvipākavāsanāṃ niṣyandavāsanāṃ vātmany ādhātuṃsamartham ātmani kāritravirodhāt rnam par shes pa ni rnam par smin pa'i bag chags dang rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags bdag la skyed par mi nus te /
bdag la byed pa 'gal ba'i phyir ro /
nāpy anantare tasyatadānutpannatvād anutpannasya cāsattvāt /
nāpy utpannepūrvasya tadā niruddhatvāt 		de ma theg pa la yang ma yin te /
de ni de'i tshe ma byung ba'i phyir ro /
ma byung ba ni med pa'i phyir ro /
byung ba la yang ma yin te /
de ni de'i tshe sngar 'gags pa'i phyir ro /
acittakāsu ca middhādyavasthāsupunaḥ saṃskāraparibhāvitacittotpattyasambhavādvijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpaṃ na syāt sems med pa'i gnyid kyis log pa la sogs pa'i dus na ni 'du byed kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i sems 'byung mi srid pa'i phyir rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs med par 'gyur ro /
tadabhāvātṣaḍāyatanaṃna syāt de med par skye mched drug kyang med par 'gyur ro /
evaṃ yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ na syāt /
tataś casaṃsārapravṛttir evavirudhyate 		de bzhin du rga shi'i bar du yang med par 'gyur ro /
saṃsāranivṛttir apyālayavijñāne 'satinopapadyate de'i phyir 'khor bar 'jug pa nyid dang 'gal lo /
'khor ba las ldog pa yang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na mi 'thad de /
saṃsārasya hi karmakleśāḥkāraṇam 'khor ba'i rgyu ni las dang nyon mongs pa rnams so /
tayoḥ kleśāḥ pradhānam de gnyis las kyang nyon mongs pa ni gtso bo ste /
tathā hi kleśādhipatyātkarma punarbhavākṣepasamarthaṃ bhavatinānyathā 'di ltar nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis na las kyis yang srid pa 'phen nus par 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma yin no /
ata evana dṛṣṭasatyānāṃ karmāṇi punarbhavam ākṣipantidarśanaprahātavyakleśābhāvāt de'i phyir bden pa mthong ba rnams kyi las las yang srid pa mi 'phen te /
mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
ākṣiptapunarbhavam api karmakleśābhāvān na punarbhavībhavatīti de bzhin du yang srid pa 'phangs pa'i las kyang nyon mongs pa med na yang srid pa 'byung bar mi 'gyur te /
tathā hitraidhātukavītarāgāṇām ākṣiptapunarbhavam api karmakleśābhāvād bhavībhavituṃ notsahate 'di ltar khams gsum gyi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams kyi yang srid pa 'phangs pa'i las kyang nyon mongs pa med pa'i phyir yang srid pa 'byung bar byed mi nus so /
ataś ca teṣāṃpunarbhavo nābhinirvartate de'i phyir de dag gi yang srid pa mngon par mi 'grub bo /
evaṃ ca pradhānatvāt kleśā evasaṃsārapravṛtter mūlam de ltar na gtso bo yin pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa nyid 'khor bar 'jug pa'i rtsa ba ste /
atas teṣu prahīṇeṣu saṃsāro nivartatenānyathā de'i phyir de dag spangs na 'khor ba las ldog par 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma yin no /
na cālayavijñānam antareṇa tatprahāṇaṃ yujyate kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med par de dag spang du mi rung ste /
sammukhībhūto vā kleśaḥ prahīyeta bījāvastho vā nyon mongs pa mngon du gyur pa'am /
sa bon gyi tshe spang grang na /
tatrasammukhībhūtaḥ prahīyata ity aniṣṭir eveyam tadātatprahāṇamārgābhāvāt de la mngon du gyur pa spang ngo zhe na ni /
de mi 'dod pa nyid de /
de'i tshe de dag spong ba'i lam med pa'i phyir ro /
bījāvastho 'pi naiva prahīyate na hipratipakṣāt tadānīṃ kiñcid anyad abhyupagamyate yatrakleśabījaṃ vyavasthitaṃtatpratipakṣeṇa prahīyeta /
atha pratipakṣacittameva kleśabījānuṣaktam iṣyate na hi kleśabījānuṣaktam eva tatpratipakṣo yujyate 		sa bon gyi tshe yang spang du mi rung ste /
gang la nyon mongs pa'i sa bon gnas pa de gnyen pos spong na /
de'i tshe ni gnyen po las ci yang khas ma blangs pa'i phyir ro /
ji ste gnyen po'i sems nyid nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang 'dres na ni nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang 'dres pa nyid pas gnyen por mi rung ste /
nacāprahīṇakleśabījānāṃ saṃsāravinivṛttiḥsambhavatīti tasmādavaśyam ālayavijñānaṃ tadanyavijñānasahabhūtaiḥ kleśopakleśair bhāvyatesvabījapuṣṭyādhānata ity upeyam nyon mongs pa'i sa bon ma spangs pa rnams ni 'khor ba las ldog mi srid do /
de lta bas na gdon mi za bar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la de las gzhan pa'i rnam par shes pa dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyis rang gi sa bon gso bar bya ba'i phyir bag chags bsgo bar khas blangs so /
punaś ca tata eva santatipariṇāmaviśeṣād yathābalaṃbhāvanāvṛttilābhe sati kleśopakleśāḥ pravartante rgyun 'gyur ba'i bye brag gi stobs ji lta ba bzhin du bsgos pa 'jug pa rnyed nas /
yang de nyid las nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams 'byung ste /
teṣāṃcālayavijñānavyavasthitaṃ bījaṃtatsahabhuvākleśapratipakṣamārgeṇāpanīyate de dag gi sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa ni de dang lhan cig 'byung ba nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po lam gyis sel to /
tasmiṃś cāpanīte punastenāśrayeṇa kleśānām anutpattir iti sopadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhātuḥprāpyate de bsal nas gnas de nas nyon mongs pa rnams mi 'byung bas phung po lhag ma dang bcas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings thob bo /
pūrvakarmākṣiptajanmanirodhe ca tato'nyajanmāpratisandhānān nirupadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhātuḥ sngon gyi las kyis 'phangs pa'i skye ba ni 'gags la /
de las gzhan pa'i skye ba dang nying mtshams mi sbyor ba ni lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings te /
na hikarmavidyamānam api kleśeṣu prahīṇeṣusahakārikāraṇābhāvātpunarbhavam abhinirvartayituṃsamartham las yod du zin kyang nyon mongs pa rnams spangs na lhan cig byed pa'i rgyu med pa'i phyir /
yang srid pa mngon par 'grub par byed mi nus so /
ata evālayavijñāne sati saṃsārapravṛttir nivṛttiś canānyathety avaśyam ālayavijñānam abhyupagantavyam de ltar na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yod na 'khor bar 'jug pa dang ldog par rung gi gzhan du ni ma yin te /
gdon mi za bar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa khas blang bar bya'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃtad ālayavijñānam ity ucyate ci'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya zhe na /
ālayavijñānatvaṃ punas tasyasarvabījālayatām kun gzhi rnam par shes pa 'di ni sa bon thams cad kyi gzhi nyid do /
upādāyety ante 'padiṣṭaṃsarvatrābhisambadhyate /
ālayavijñānabhāva ālayavijñānatvam /
tat punar ālayavijñānaśabdapravṛttinimittam 		phyir ro zhes bya ba tha mar gang bstan pa de ni thams cad du sbyar bar bya'o /
kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i dngos po ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid do /
de ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba 'jug pa'i rgyu'o /
tatravijānātītivijñānaṃ de la rnam par shes par byed pas rnam par shes pa ste /
tadvyatiriktavijñātrabhāvapradarśanārthaṃbhāvamātre kartṛvyapadeśaḥ de las ma gtogs par shes par byed pa po med par bstan pa'i phyir dngos po tsam la byed par bstan to /
sarvabījālayatāsarvasāṅkleśikadharmabījasthānatā /
ālayaṃ sthānam itiparyāyaḥ 		sa bon thams cad kyi gzhi nyid ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos kyi sa bon thams cad kyi gnas nyid do; /
gzhi ni gnas kyi rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o /
athavālīyanta upanibadhyante 'smin sarvadharmāḥkāryabhāvena tad vālīyata upanibadhyate kāraṇabhāvenasarvadharmeṣv ity ālayaḥ /
ātmabhāvālayanimittatāṃ copādāya /
ātmabhāvo /
nāmarūpam /
ālīyate 'sminn ātmabhāvaḥ tadbalenānuvṛttita ity ālayaḥ 		yang na 'dir chos thams cad 'bras bu'i dngos por sbyor zhing nye bar 'brel ba'am /
de chos thams cad la rgyu'i dngos por sbyor zhing nye bar 'brel bas kun gzhi'o /
lus kyi kun gzhi nyid dang rgyu nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba la lus ni ming dang gzugs so /
der lus sbyor te /
de'i stobs kyis 'byung bas kun gzhi nyid do /
tadbhāva ālayatā /
ātmabhāvanimittaṃ tadbījaparipoṣātpratisandhāv ātmabhāvanirvartanāt 		de'i dngos po ni kun gzhi nyid do /
lus kyi rgyu ni de'i sa bon yongs su gsos pas nying mtshams sbyor ba ni lus mngon par 'grub pa'i phyir te /
ātmabhāvālayatāmātmabhāvanimittatāṃ copādāyālayavijñānatvamabhyupagantavyam /
anye punar anyathā paṭhanti ātmamānālayanimittatāṃ copādāyeti 		lus kyi gzhi nyid dang lus kyi rgyu nyid yin pas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid khas blang bar bya'o gzhan nas de bzhin du 'byung ste /
bdag tu nga rgyal gyi gzhi dang rgyu nyid kyi phyir ro zhes 'byung ngo /
ālayavijñānam ātmatvenālambamānasya yo mānaḥsa ātmamāna kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la bdag tu dmigs pa'i nga rgyal gang yin pa de bdag tu nga rgyal lo /
ālīyatetasmin viṣayibhāvenātmamāna ityālayavijñānamātmamānālayaḥ bdag tu nga rgyal ni 'di la yul can gyi dngos por sbyor bas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni bdag tu nga rgyal gyi kun gzhi'o /
ālīyate vā tannimittabhāvenātmamāna ity ālayaucyate /
śeṣaṃ pūrvavat /
kāyālīnatāṃ copādāyeti /
caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ 		yang na de dag tu nga rgyal la rgyu'i dngos por sbyor bas kun gzhi zhes bya'o /
lhag ma ni snga ma bzhin no /
lus la gnas pa nyid kyi yang phyir ro zhes bya ba la yang zhes bya ba ni bsdu ba'i don to /
kāyo 'tra sendriyaṃ śarīram /
samantaṃ hi śarīraṃvyāpyālayavijñānaṃ vartate 		lus ni 'dir dbang po dang bcas pa'i khog pa'o /
kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni khog pa thams cad la khyab pa'o /
ataḥ kāyapratibaddhavṛttitvāt tatkāye ālīnam iti kāyālīnam /
tadbhāvaḥkāyālīnatā 		de'i phyir lus dang 'brel bar 'jug pas lus la gnas pa'i phyir lus la gnas pa'o /
de'i dngos po ni lus la gnas pa nyid de /
tāṃkāyālīnatām upādāya gṛhītvālayavijñānatvam asyapratipattavyam lus la gnas pa nyid kyi phyir bzung nas 'di kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid du khong du chud par bya'o /
na kevalam ālayavijñānam etad ucyate kiṃ tarhyādānavijñānam apīti /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃ tad ādānavijñānam /
ity ucyate /
ataḥ kāraṇam āha kāyopādānatāmupādāyeti /
ādīyate kāyo 'nenety ādānavijñānam ity ucyate 		de ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba 'ba' zhig tu ma zad kyi /
len pa'i rnam par shes pa yang de yin te /
ci'i phyir de len pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya zhe na /
de'i phyir lus len pa'i phyir ro zhes rgyu smos so /
'dis lus len bas len pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya ste /
cittena kāyasyopādānaṃ nānyeneti prasiddham sems kyis lus len gyi bdag gis ni ma yin no zhes bya bar rab tu grub bo /
tac ca yatpūrvasaṃskārahetukaṃśukraśoṇitasammūrchitāvasthāyāṃ bhavam upādatte de yang sngon gyi 'du byed kyi rgyu las 'byung ba ste /
khu ba dang khrag gi nang du brgyal ba'i dus na srid pa len te /
tad evāmaraṇāt kāyopādātṛtveneṣyate de nyid shi ba la thug gi bar lus len par byed par 'dod kyi /
na cakṣurādivijñānānitatpṛṣṭhalabdhaṃ vā manovijñānam teṣāṃ tata ūrdhvaṃvartamānacakṣurādipratyayanimittatvāt mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams dang de'i rjes las byung ba yid kyi rnam par shes pas ni ma yin te /
de dag ni de'i 'og tu mig la sogs pa rkyen rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
na ca tatrānyanmanovijñānaṃ saṃskārahetukaṃ tasya kuśalākuśalatvāt de la yid kyi rnam par shes pa gzhan 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung ba ni ma yin te /
de dag dge ba dang mi dge ba'i phyir ro /
saṃskārahetukaṃ hy ekāntenāvyākṛtam vipākatvāt 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung ba ni rnam par smin pa yin pa'i phyir gcig tu lung ma bstan pa'o /
vipākaśca na vicchinnaḥ sandhīyate cakṣurādivat rnam par smin pa la yang mig la sogs pa bzhin du rgyun chad nas yang nying mtshams sbyor ba ma yin no /
na cālayavijñānāanyad ekāntenāvyākṛtajātīyam upalabhyateyadvipākavijñānatvena parikalpyeta gang rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa nyid kun du rtag pa gcig tu lung ma bstan pa'i rang bzhin can ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las gzhan ma mthong ngo /
api capratiniyatāśrayapravṛttatvāt ṣaṇṇāṃ vijñānakāyānāṃvicchedapravṛttatvāc ca na sarvasyāśrayasyopādānaṃprasajyate yang rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po dag ni gnas so sor nges pa las 'byung ba dang rgyun chad nas 'byung ba'i phyir gnas thams cad len par mi rung ste /
tathā hiyena yenāśrayeṇa yad vijñānaṃ pravartatesa eva tenopāttaḥ syāt avaśiṣṭasyānupāttatvaṃvijñānavirahitatvāt 'di ltar gnas gang dang gang las rnam par shes pa gang 'byung ba des de nyid zin par 'gyur gyi /
lhag ma ni rnam par shes pa dang bral ba'i phyir zin pa ma yin no /
tathā cakṣurādivijñānaṃ vicchedena punaḥ punaḥ pravartata ititadāśrayasya punaḥ punarupādānadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ de ltar mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rgyun chad nas yang dang yang 'byung ba'i phyir gnas de yang dang yang nye bar len pa'i skyon du 'gyur ro /
tasmād ālayavijñānam evapratisandhau kāyam upādatte ā maraṇāc ca samastakāyāśrayeṇa pravartata iti tad eva rpratisandhibandhātprabhṛty ā maraṇāt kāyam upādātta ity ādānavijñānam ity ucyate /
prādhānyena mana ālayavijñānālambanam /
iti /
kliṣṭaṃ hi mana ālayavijñānam ātmatvena nityam ālambateātmālambanair mohadṛṣṭimānasnehaiḥ samprayuktatvāt /
tac canityakālaṃmanyanātmakatvān manaḥ /
prādhānyena tad eva mana ucyate 		de lta bas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid nying mtshams sbyor ba'i dus nas lus bzung nas shi ba la thug gi bar du lus mtha' dag la brten te 'byung bas de nyid nying mtshams sbyor ba nas shi ba la thug gi bar du lus 'dzin pas na len pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o /
dngos su na yid kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la dmigs zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi yid kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la rtag par bdag tu dmigs te /
bdag tu rmongs pa dang lta ba dang nga rgyal dang chags par dmigs pa rnams dang mtshungs bar ldan pa'i phyir ro /
de yang rtag par rlom sems pa'i bdag nyid yin pas yod do /
dngos su na de yid ces bya'o /
yat ṣaṇṇāṃ cakṣurādivijñānakāyānāṃ samanantaraniruddhaṃ vijñānaṃ mana ity uktam tat ṣaṣṭhasyamanovijñānasyāśrayaprasiddhyartham na tumanyanākāratvāt /
ato na tasya prādhānyena manastvam 		mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po dag 'gags ma thag pa'i rnam par shes pa la yid ces brjod pa gang yin pa de ni drug pa yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i gnas sgrub pa'i phyir yin gyi ngar sems pa'i rna ba'i phyir ni ma yin no /
de'i phyir dngos su na de ni yid nyid ma yin no /
taccaturbhiḥ kleśairnityaṃ samprayuktam /
vātmamohātmadṛṣṭyātmamānātmasnehaiḥ 		de yang bdag tu rmongs pa dang bdag tu lta ba dang bdag tu nga rgyal dang bdag la chags pa ste /
nyon mongs pa bzhi dang rtag par mtshungs par ldan te /
atra tv ātmagrahaṇaṃ na mohamātreṇa samprayujyate kiṃtarhy ātmaniyo mohaḥ /
evaṃ yāvad ātmasnehe vaktavyam 		de la bdag tu rmongs pa ni gti mug tsam dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin gyi /
bdag tu rmongs pa gang yin pa'o /
de bzhin du bdag la chags pa'i bar dag la yang brjod par bya'o /
ādigrahaṇāt pañcabhiḥsarvatragaiś casparśamanaskārādibhiḥ sadā samprayuktam sogs pa ni reg pa dang yid la byed pa la sogs pa kun du 'gro ba lnga po dag dang yang rab tu mtshungs par ldan pa'o /
tasyāpratītatvāccaittānām api caittaiḥ samprayogāc catatsvarūpanirdhāraṇārtham āha vijñānam iti de yang ma grags pa dang sems las byung ba rnams dang mtshungs par ldan pas na de'i rang gi ngo bo dmigs kyis dbye ba'i phyir /
rnam par shes pa ste zhes bya ba smos so /
ekajātīyam iti kliṣṭajātīyam na kuśalam avyākṛtaṃ vānityam ātmamohādibhiś caturbhiḥ kleśaiḥ samprayuktatvāt rigs gcig pa zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi rigs yin gyi /
dge ba'am /
lung du ma bstan pa ni ma yin te /
bdag tu rmongs pa la sogs pa nyon mongs pa bzhi dang rtag tu mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir ro /
santānānuvṛtti cety avicchedena vartata ity arthaḥ rgyun chags par 'jug pa ste zhes bya ba ni rgyun mi 'chad par rjes su 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
asyotsargasyāpavādam ārabhatearhattvāryamārganirodhasamāpattyavasthāṃ sthāpayitvā /
arhattvāvasthāyāṃ na pravartate arhato /
nira vaśe ṣatr aidh ātuk akli ṣṭad harm apra hīṇa tvāt 		spyir btang ba 'di'i dmigs kyis bsal ba rtsom ste /
dgra bcom pa dang 'phags pa'i lam dang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i dus ma gtogs so /
dgra bcom pa ni khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa can gyi chos spangs pa'i phyir dgra bcom pa'i dus ni mi 'byung ngo /
āryamārgāvasthāyām api na pravartate paramārthajñānasyātmadṛṣṭisamudācāreṇātyantavirodhāt 'phags pa'i lam gyi dus na yang mi 'byung ste /
de na dam pa shes pa ni bdag tu lta ba kun du 'byung ba dang shin tu mi mthun pa'i phyir ro /
tataūrdhvam asyālayavijñānāt pravṛttiḥ śaikṣasyāprahīṇatvāt /
nirodhasamāpattyavasthāyām api na pravartate 		de'i 'og tu kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las 'byung ste /
slob pa'i dus na ma spangs pa'i phyir ro /
'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i dus na yang mi 'byung ste /
asañjñisamāpattito nirodhasamāpatteḥśāntataratvaṃ tadasamucāratvād eva veditavyam 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bas [?] 'gog pa'i snyoms par zhugs pa ches zhe ba'i phyir /
de kun du mi 'byung bar rig par bya'o /
atra ca mano nirvacanataālambanataḥ samprayogataḥ pravṛttikālataś ca nirdiṣṭaṃveditavyam /
kenārthena rūpādiskandhā ity ucyante 		'dir ni nges pa'i tshig dang dmigs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang 'byung pa'i dus kyi yid bstan par rig par bya'o /
ci'i phyir phung po zhes bya zhe na /
rāśyarthena /
rāśiḥ skandha iti paryāyaḥ /
etad uktaṃ bhavati rūparāśī rūpaskandhaḥ 		spungs pa'i phyir te zhes bya ba la spungs pa ni phung po zhes bya ba'i grangs su gtogs pa'o /
de ni 'di skad du gzugs spungs pa ni gzugs kyi phung po ste /
evaṃ yāvad vijñānarāśirvijñānaskandha iti /
yasmāt sūtre adhvasantānaprakāragatideśabhedabhinnān /
āṃ rūpādīnāṃ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatāmupādāya rūpādayaḥ skandhā uktāḥ /
y zyat kiñcid rūpam aatītānāgatapratyutpannam ādhyātmikaṃ vā bāhyaṃ vāaudarikaṃ vā sūkṣmaṃ vā hīnaṃ vā praṇītaṃ vā yad vā dūre yad vāntikesarvam aikadhyam abhisaṅkṣipya rūpaskandhaitisaṅkhyāṃ gacchatītyevaṃ yāvad vijñānam 		de bzhin du rnam par shes pa'i bar du sbungs pa la rnam par shes pa'i phung po zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
'di ltar mdo las dus dang rgyu dang rnam pa dang 'gro ba dang yul tha dad pa'i gzugs la sogs pa mdor bsdus pa'i phyir /
gzugs la sogs pa phung por bstan te /
gzugs gang yin pa ci yang rung 'das pa'am ma 'ongs pa'am da ltar byung pa'am /
nang gi'am phyi'i'am /
rags pa'am /
phra ba'am /
ngan pa'am /
gya nom pa'am /
thag nye ba gang yin pa'am /
rgyang ring ba gang yin pa thams cad gcig tu bsdus nas gzugs kyi phung po zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro'o /
de bzhin du rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o zhes 'byung ste /
atītānāgatapratyutpannā ity adhvabhedena bhinnāḥ 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba zhes bya ba'i bye brag gis dus tha dad pa'o /
ādhyātmikā vā bāhyā veti santānabhedena yasmādādhyātmikāḥ svāsāntānikāḥ bāhyās tato 'nye nang ngam phyi zhes bya ba ni rgyu tha dad pas so /
'di ltar nang gi rnams ni rang gi rgyud du gtogs pa dag go /
phyi'i rnams ni de las gzhan pa dag go /
audārikā vāsūkṣmā veti prakārabhedena rags pa'am /
phra ba zhes bya ba ni rnam pa'i bye brag gis so /
tatra rūpasyāpekṣikamaudārikasūkṣmatvam de la gzugs kyi rags pa dang phra ba nyid ni ltos ba can no /
sapratigham audārikam apratighaṃsūkṣmaṃ yang na thogs pa dang bcas pa ni rags pa'o /
thogs pa med pa ni phra ba'o /
vedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānāni tupañcendriyāśrayotpannāny audārikāṇi mānasāni sūkṣmāṇi tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams kyang dbang po lnga la brten te /
byung ba dag ni rags pa'o /
yid la brten te byung ba dag ni phra ba'o; /
hīnā vā praṇītā veti gatibhedena bhinnāḥ ngan pa'am gya nom pa zhes bya ba ni 'gro ba'i bye brag gis tha dad pa rnams te /
tathā hihīnagatisaṅgṛhītā hīnāḥpraṇītagatisaṅgṛhītāḥ praṇītāḥ 'di ltar 'gro ba ngan pas zin pa dag ni ngan pa rnams so /
'gro ba gya nom pas zin pa dag ni gya nom pa rnams so /
yad vādūre yad vāntika iti deśabhedena bhinnāḥ thag nye ba gang yin pa'am /
rgyang ring po gang yin pa zhes bya ba ni yul gyi bye brag gis tha dad pa rnams so /
vedanādīnāṃ tudūrāntikatvam āśrayavaśena tshor ba la sogs pa ni gnas kyi dbang gis nye ba dang ring ba'o /
rūpādīnām iti rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānām gzugs la sogs pa zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams so /
saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatām upādāyetydhva sant ānap rakā raga tide śabh edab hinn ānāṃrūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānāṃ pratyekaṃ saṅkṣepeṇasaṅgrahaḥ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahaḥ /
tadbhāvaḥ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatā 		mdor bsdus pa nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni dus dang rgyu dang rnam pa dang 'gro ba dang yul tha dad pa rnams kyi gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams so sor mdor bsdus pa ni mdor bsdus pa'o /
de'i dngos po ni mdor bsdus pa nyid do /
tāṃ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatām upādāya sūtre rāśyarthaḥskandhārtho vijñāyate de dag mdor bsdus pa'i phyir mdo las sbungs pa'i don zhes 'byung ba ni phung po'i don ni zhes bya bar shes te /
tathā hy uktam /
tat sarvam atītādikaṃrūpam ekadhyam abhisaṅkṣipya rūpaskandha itisaṅkhyāṃ gacchatīti /
evaṃ yāvad vijñānam /
uktāḥ pañca skandhāḥ skandhārthaś ca 		'di ltar 'das pa la sogs pa'i gzugs de dag thams cad ni gcig tu bsdus nas gzugs kyi phung po zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro ba zhes bya ba nas /
de bzhin du rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i bar du bstan to /
phung po lnga po rnams dang phung po'i don bshad zin to /
phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa bye brag tu bshad pa /
bam po bzhi pa ste tha ma'o /
sarvasaṃskārāḥpañcaskandhasaṅgraheṇoktāḥ sarvadharmāḥsaṃskṛtā asaṃskṛtāś cāyatanadhātusaṅgraheṇa /
tatraskandhanirdeśānantaram āyatanāni vaktavyāni /
kaścāyatanārtha ity ata āha dvādaśāyatanānīti /
tāni punaḥ 		'dus byas thams cad ni phung po lngas bsdus la /
'dus byas dang; 'dus ma byas kyi chos thams cad ni skye mched dang khams su bsdus par bstan pa de la phung po bshad pa'i 'og tu skye mched rnams brjod dgos pas du zhig gang dang gang skye mched kyi don ni ci zhe na /
de'i phyir /
skye mched bcu gnyis zhes bya ba smos so /
katamāni /
cakṣurāyatanaṃ rūpāyatanaṃ yāvadmanaāyatanaṃ dharmāyatanaṃ caiti /
cakṣurādīnāṃ pūrvavan nirdeśa iti 		de dag kyang gang zhe na; mig gi skye mched dang gzugs kyi skye mched dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa nas /
yid kyi skye mched dang chos kyi skye mched do zhes bya ba'i bar du'o /
rūpaskandhavibhāge yathā cakṣurādayaḥ svarūpato nirdiṣṭāḥtathehāpi svarūpatonirdeṣṭavyā iti mig la sogs pa ni snga ma bzhin du bshad do zhes bya ba ni gzugs kyi phung po rnam par phye ba ni ji ltar mig la sogs pa'i rang gi ngo bo bstan pa de bzhin du 'dir yang rang gi ngo bo bstan par bya'o /
tatra hy uktaṃ catvāri mahābhūtāny upādāya varṇaviṣayo rūpaprasādaścakṣurindriyam iti de la mig gi dbang po ni 'byung ba chen po bzhi rgyur byas pa ste /
yul kha dog gzugs dang ba'o zhes bstan to /
evaṃ śabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyaviṣayāyathākramaṃ rūpātmakāḥ prasādāḥśrotrādayaḥ de bzhin du sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya yang yul te; go rims bzhin no /
rna ba la sogs pa yang gzugs kyi bdag nyid dang ba'o /
rūpaśabdagandharasāyatanānāṃ ca pūrvavan /
nirdeśa iti sambadhyate 		gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro'i skye mched rnams kyang snga ma bzhin du bshad do zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
pūrvaṃ hi nirdiṣṭaś cakṣuṣo viṣayovarṇaḥsaṃsthānaṃ vijñaptiś ca rūpam sngar ni mig gi yul ni /
kha dog dang dbyibs dang rnam par rig byed kyi gzugs so /
upāttānupāttobhayamahābhūtahetukaḥ śrotrasya viṣayaḥśabdaityādi rna ba'i yul ni sgra ste /
zin pa dang ma zin pa dang gnyi ga'i ste 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa bstan to /
mahābhūtāni yaś ca /
spraṣṭavyasyaikadeśa uktaḥ tat saha mahābhūtaiḥspraṣṭavyāyatanam 		'byung ba chen po dag dang gang reg bya'i phyogs gcig bshad pa ste /
de 'byung ba chen po rnams dang bcas pa ni reg bya'i skye mched do /
tat punaḥ ślakṣṇatvam ityādi de yang 'jam pa nyid la sogs pa'o /
manaāyatanaṃ yo vijñānaskandhaiti /
aṣṭau /
vijñānāni vijñānaskandhaḥ ṣaḍ pravṛttivijñānāniālayavijñānaṃ kliṣṭaṃ ca manaḥ 		yid kyi skye mched ni rnam par shes pa'i phung po gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba la rnam par shes pa brgyad ni rnam par shes pa'i phung po ste /
'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa drug dang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dang nyon mongs pa can gyi yod do /
āyatanavyavasthāyāṃ tuvijñānaskandha eva manaāyatanam ucyate /
dharmāyatanaṃ punar aṣṭaprakāraṃ 		skye mched rnam par gzhag pa la ni rnam par shes pa'i phung po nyid la yid kyi skye mched ces bya'o /
chos kyi skye mched ni rnam pa brgyad de /
vedanāsañjñāsaṃskāraskandhā avijñaptiścāsaṃskṛtāni cacatvāri tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed kyi phung po dang rnam par rig byed ma yin pa dang 'dus ma byas bzhi'o /
tatra /
vedanāsañjñāsaṃskāraskandhā avijñaptiś ca skandhavibhaṅgaevoktāḥ /
asaṃskṛtaṃ tu noktam ity atas tatprabhedabubhutsayā pṛcchati asaṃskṛtaṃ katamad iti 		de la tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed kyi phung po dang rnam par rig byed ma yin pa ni phung po rnam par phye bas bshad pa yin no /
'dus ma byas ni ma bshad de /
de'i phyir de dag rab tu dbye bar 'dod nas /
'dus ma byas gang zhe na zhes dris so /
yan na /
hetupratyayapratibaddhasvarūpam tad asaṃskṛtam ucyate /
ākāśam apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥpratisaṅkhyānirodhas tathatā cety 		gang rgyu dang rkyen la rag las pa ma yin pa'i bdag nyid kyi rang gi ngo bo ni 'dus ma byas zhes bya ste /
nam mkha' dang so sor brtags ba ma yin pa'i 'gog pa dang so so brtags pa'i 'gog pa dang de bzhin nyid do /
asaṃskṛtaprabhedapradarśanam 'dus ma byas kyi rab tu dbye ba ston te /
ākāśaṃ katamad ity /
ākāśasvarūpāvabodhārthaṃ praśnaḥ /
yo rūpāvakāśaiti tatsvarūpanirdeśaḥ 		nam mkha' gang zhe na zhes bya ba ni nam mkha'i rang gi ngo bo khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir 'dri ba'o /
gang gzugs kyi go 'byed pa'o zhes bya ba ni de'i rang gi ngo bo bshad pa'o /
evam apratisaṅkhyānirodhādiṣv api pratyekaṃ vācyam /
sapratighaṃ rūpaṃ yatra pradeśe napratihanyatesa tasyāvakāśaḥ 		de bzhin du so sor brtags pa ma yin pa la sogs pa so sor brjod par bya'o /
phyogs gang du thogs pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs la thogs par mi byed pa ni go 'byed pa'o /
ato rūpiṇāṃ bhāvānāmavakāśadānād ākāśam ity ucyate de'i phyir dngos po gzugs can rnams la skabs 'byed pa nam mkha' zhes bya'o /
ākāśānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt tann irde ś ānant aram evāpratisaṅkhyānirodhasvarūpāvabodhārthaṃ praśnaḥ apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ katama iti nam mkha'i 'og tu bstan pa'i phyir de bshad pa'i 'og tu so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa'i rang gi ngo bo khong du chud par 'dod nas /
so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa gang zhe na zhes dris so /
saṅkhyānaṃ /
tulanaṃ vicayaḥprajñety anarthāntaram /
pratir vīpsārthaḥ 		brtags pa dang gzhal ba dang rnam par 'byed pa dang shes rab ces bya ba ni don gcig go /
so sor zhes bya ba ni spyir bsnyag pa'i don te /
tad uktaṃ bhavati duḥkhādīnām āryasatyānāṃpratipratisaṅkhyānaṃ pratisaṅkhyā de ni 'di ltar sdug bsngal la sogs pa 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la so sor rtog pa ni so sor brtags pa ste /
prajñāviśeṣa ity arthaḥ /
napratisaṅkhyā apratisaṅkhyā /
kā punar asau /
pratyayavaikalyam 		shes rab kyi khyad par zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
so sor ma brtags pa ni so sor brtags pa ma yin pa ste /
de yang gang zhe na /
etad uktaṃ bhavati pratyayavaikalyādanāgatānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yo 'tyantam anutpādaḥ so'pratisaṅkhyānirodhaiti rkyen ma tshang ba'o /
de ni 'di skad du rkyen ma tshang ba'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i chos rnams gtan du mi skye ba gang yin pa de so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
yo nirodho na cavisaṃyogaityādi praśnavyākaraṇam gang 'gog pa la 'bral ba ma yin pa ste zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni 'dri ba'i lan no /
nirodhaśabdo hy atra /
pratisaṅkhyānirodhasamāpattyupapattyanityatānirodheṣv apivartata iti pratisaṅkhyānirodhavyavacchedārtham āha na cavisaṃyoga iti 		'gog pa zhes byas na ni so sor brtags pa ma yin pas 'gog pa bzhin du so sor brtags pa dang; snyoms par 'jug pa dang skye ba dang mi rtag pa'i 'gog pa rnams la yang snyegs pas 'dir so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa rnam par dbye ba'i phyir 'bral ba ma yin pa zhes bya ba smos te /
saṃyogo hy anāgatair dharmair bīje sati teṣāmutpattidharmatām upādāya vyavasthāpyate /
tatpratipakṣeṇasvāśrayāt teṣāṃ bīje 'poddhṛte yo 'tyantam anutpādaḥ pratilabdha itiso 'py apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ prāpnotīty ata āha sa punar yaḥ kleśapratipakṣeṇa vinā skandhānām atyantam anutpāda iti /
etad uktaṃ 		'bral ba ma yin zhes bya ba ni sa bon yod na de dag 'byung ba'i chos nyid yin pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i chos rnams dang phrad par rnam par gzhag ste /
de'i gnyen pos rang gi gnas nas de dag gi sa bon bton bzhin gtan mi skye ba gang yin pa de 'gog pa'o /
de ni 'di skad du sa bon bton la blo sngon du ma btang yang rkyen ma tshang bas ma 'ongs pa'i chos rnams gtan mi skye ba gang yin pa de so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
dgra bcom pa la ni ris gzhan dang 'brel ba'i dge ba dang lung dum bstan pa'i phung po rnams kyis bon yod bzhin du gtan mi skye ba thob pas /
de yang so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog par 'gyur ro zhe na /
de'i phyir /
de ni gang nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po med par phung po rnams gtan du mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba smos te /
de ni 'di skad du /
bhavati ayaṃ hi saty apikuśalākuśalāvyākṛtaskandhabījasadbhāvena vinā kleśapratipakṣeṇa labhyata iti pratisaṅkhyānirodha evāyamnāpratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ 'di la dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i phung po'i sa bon yod du zin kyang /
nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po med par mi thob pas so so brtags pa'i 'gog pa nyid de /
'di ni so sor ma brtags pa'i 'gog pa ma yin no /
evaṃ sopadhiśeṣo nirupadhiśeṣaś canirvāṇadhātuḥ pratisaṅkhyānirodha ity uktaṃ bhavati de ltar na phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa dang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings ni so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa zhes bstan pa yin no /
kleśapratipakṣo 'trānāsravo mārgo 'bhipretaḥ nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po ni 'dir zag pa med pa'i lam du bzhed do /
atyantamanutpāda ity atyantagrahaṇam upapattisamāpattinirodhavyavacchedārtham gtan du mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba la gtan du smos pa ni skye ba dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i 'gog pa las rnam par dbye ba'i phyir ro /
sahy anutpādobhavatina tv atyantam punaś cittacaittotpādasadbhāvāt /
anutpāda ity anityatānirodhāt /
anityatānirodho hi vartamānasyana ca vartamānasyānutpādo 'sti kiṃ tarhy anāgatasyaiveti /
tadyathaikarūpaprakāravyāsaktacakṣurvijñānasya yāni viṣayāntarāṇy utpattimanti rūpaprakārāntarāṇi catadālambanaiḥ pañcabhir vijñānakāyair na śakyam utpattumvartamāneṣu samanantarapratyayābhāvāt atīteṣvālambanapratyayābhāvāt /
atas teṣām apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥprāpyate 		de dag mi skye ba yin la gtan du ma yin pa ste /
sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyang 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba ni mi rtag pa nyid kyi 'gog pa las rnam par 'byed de /
mi rtag pa nyid kyi 'gog pa ni de ltar yod la mi skye ba ni da ltar med pas ma 'ongs pa yin pa nyid de /
dper na gzugs kyi rnam pa gcig la mig gi rnam par shes pa yengs pa yul gzhan dang gzugs kyi rnam pa gzhan 'das pa gang yin pa de dag ni dmigs pa de'i rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga bskyed par mi nus te /
da ltar gyi rnam pa la ni de ma thag pa'i rkyen med cing /
'das pa rnams la ni dmigs pa'i rkyen med pa'i phyir ro /
de'i phyir de dag la so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog par 'gyur ro /
pratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ katama iti so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa gang zhe na zhes bya ba la /
kpratisaṅkhyānaṃ pratisaṅkhyāānantaryamārgasaṅgṛhītaḥprajñāviśeṣa ity arthaḥ /
pratisaṅkhyayā prāpyo nirodhomadhyapadalopāt /
yo nirodhaiti sarvanirodhaprasaṅga ityāha sa cavisaṃyogaiti /
evaṃ hi śeṣebhyaś caturbhyo /
nirodhebhyo vyavacchinno bhavati teṣāmavisaṃyogātmakatvāt 		so sor rtog pa ni so sor brtags pa ste /
bar chad med pa'i lam gyis shes rab kyi khyad par zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
so sor brtags pas thob par bya ba'i 'gog pa ni so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa ste /
tshig bar ma ma smos so /
gang 'gog pa zhes bya ba ni 'gog pa thams cad du thal bar 'gyur bas /
de ni 'brel pa ste zhes bya ba smos so /
de ltar na 'gog pa lhag ma bzhi po las rnam par phye ba yin te /
visaṃyogam eva nirūpayati sapunar yaḥ kleśapratipakṣeṇaskandhānāmatyantam anutpāda iti de dag ni 'bral ba'i bdag nyid ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
de ni nyon mongs pa'i gnyen pos phung po gtan du mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba ni 'bral ba nyid dpyod pa ste /
ayaṃ hy āśrayo /
niravaśeṣatraidhātukakleśabījānusyūtaḥ pravartate 		lus 'di ni khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon nam lus pa dang rjes su 'brel bar 'byung ba'o /
tatra yasyayasya yo yo mārgakṣaṇaḥ pratipakṣaḥ tasmin mārga utpannesa āśrayakṣaṇas tatpraheyakleśabījānugatamnantarasyāśrayasya kṣaṇāntaram utpādayituṃ na śaknotitadutpattiviruddhapratyayasānnidhyāt de la gang dang gang gi gnyen po lam gyi skad cig gang dang gang yin pa'i lam de 'byung na lus kyi skad cig de ni des spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang ldan pa'i phyi ma lus kyi skad cig gzhan 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i rkyen du gyur pa dang phyi ma lus kyi skad cig gzhan skyed par mi nus te /
de 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i rkyen nye bar gyur pa'i phyir ro /
kiṃ tarhitatpraheyakleśabījavyāvṛttyātmakasyaiva kāraṇaṃ bhavati tadutpattyanuguṇapratyayasadbhāvāt 'on kyang des spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon ldog pa bdag nyid kho na'i rgyur 'gyur te /
de byung ba dang mthun pa'i rkyen yod pa'i phyir ro /
sa eva mārgakṣaṇas tatpraheyakleṣabījānugatasya kṣaṇāntarasyotpattaye viguṇaḥpratyayaḥitarasyānuguṇo veditavyaḥ lam gyi skad cig de nyid ni des spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang ldan pa'i skad cig gzhan 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i rkyen du gyur pa dang cig shos dang mthun par brjod par bya'o /
evaṃ yāvadbhāvanāheyasyamṛdumṛdoḥ kleśaprakārasya pratipakṣa utpanne sa āśrayoniravaśeṣatraidhātukadarśanabhāvanāprahātavyakleśabījavyāvṛ ttyātmakasyaiva kṣaṇāntarasya kāraṇībhavati de bzhin du bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i srid pa'i rtse mo'i nyon mongs pa chung du chung ngu'i bar gyi gnyen po byung na lus de khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa mthong ba dang bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i sa bon ma lus par ldog pa'i bdag nyid kho na'i skad cig gzhan gyi rgyur 'gyur ro /
evaṃ yasyayasya kleśasyāśrayāpravṛttito bījam uddhṛtaṃ bhavati tasyatasya tatsamprayuktānāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃkleśapratipakṣeṇātyantam anutpādaḥ prāpto bhavati /
sa capratisaṅkhyānirodho visaṃyogaś cety ucyate 		de bzhin du nyon mongs pa gang dang gang gi lus mi 'byung bas sa bon bton par gyur pa'i nyon mongs pa de dag mtshungs par ldan pa'i chos rnams kyang nyon mongs pa'i gnyen pos gtan du mi skye bar 'byung ste /
so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa de ni 'bral ba zhes bya'o /
pratisaṅkhyānirodhād anantaraṃ tathatoddiṣṭety atastannirdeśānantaraṃ tathatāvabodhārthaṃ praśnaḥ tathatā so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa'i 'og tu de bzhin nyid bstan pas de'i phyir de bshad pa'i 'og tu de bzhin nyid khong du chud par 'dod nas /
de bzhin nyid gang zhe na zhes 'dri'o /
katameti /
yā dharmāṇāṃ dharmatādharmanairātmyamiti tannirdeśaḥ /
ananyathātvenatathatā 		gang chos rnams kyi chos nyid dang chos bdag med pa nyid do zhes bya ba de ni de'i bshad pa ste /
gzhan ma yin pa'i don gyi phyir de bzhin nyid do /
dharmāṇām iti rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānām /
dharmāṇāṃ bhāvo dharmatā yāthātmyaṃ bhūtaprakarṣaḥ 		chos rnams zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams so /
chos rnams kyi dngos bo ni chos nyid de ji lta ba bzhin gyi bdag nyid dang yang dag pa'i mthar thug pa'o /
dharmāṇāṃ kāryānityatādayo 'pi dharmatā vidyanta ity ata āha dharmanairātmyam iti chos nyid ni chos rnams kyi 'bras bu mi rtag pa nyid la sogs pa yang chos rnams la yod de /
de'i phyir chos bdag med pa nyid ces bya ba smos so /
dharmā hi yena rūpeṇajñānābhidhānayor viṣayībhavanti tat teṣām ātmā /
tasmādātmano nirgatā atatsvabhāvatvād itinirātmānaḥ /
tadbhāvodharmanairātmyam /
tat punar bhāvānāṃkalpitasvabhāvaśūnyatā /
atra tu vicāryamāṇe bahu vaktavyaṃjāyata ity alaṃ prasaṅgena prastutam evārabhyate /
kenārthenāyatanāni /
āyatanaśabdo hi cakṣurādiṣu 		chos ni rang bzhin gang gis shes pa dang brjod pa gnyis kyi yul du 'gyur ba de de dag gi bdag ste /
de'i rang bzhin ma yin pa'i phyir bdag de dang bral ba ni bdag med pa'o /
de'i dngos po ni bdag med pa nyid do /
de ni dngos po rnams rnam par brtags pa'i rang bzhin gyi stong pa nyid do /
'di la dpyad na brjod pa mang du 'byung ste /
de thal bar 'gyur bas kyang chog gi skabs nyid brtsam mo /
ci'i phyir skye mched ces bya zhe na zhes bya ba la /
parasparavibhinnarūpeṣv aviśeṣeṇa pravartata ity atas teṣu tenasāmānyam artham upādāya pravartitavyam sa ca na vijñāyataiti praśnaḥ kenārthenāyatananīti /
vijñānāyadvārārtheneti /
āya ucyata āgamaḥ 		skye mched kyi sgra ni mig la sogs pa rang gi ngo bo phan tshun tha dad pa rnams la yang bye brag med par 'byung bas de'i phyir de dag la des spyi'i don rgyur byas nas 'jug go /
de yang mi shes pas ci'i phyir skye mched ces bya zhes 'dri'o /
rnam par shes ba skye ba'i sgo'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la /
skye ba zhes bya ba ni 'byung ba ste /
vijñānānām utpattir ātmalābhaḥ rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung bas bdag nyid thob pa'o /
vijñānāyasya dvāraṃ hetuḥkāraṇaṃ nimittaṃ vijñānāyadvāram rnam par shes pa skye ba'i sgo ni rgyu ste /
byed rgyu dang rgyu mtshan ni rnam par shes pa skye ba'i sgo'o /
de ni 'di skad du /
etad uktaṃ bhavati vijñānotpattikāraṇārthenāyatanānīti /
kathaṃ punar etadvijñāyate 		rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i rgyu'i phyir skye mched rnams zhes bya'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
'di ltar ci mngon zhe na nges pa'i tshig gis mngon te /
nirvacanāt cittacaittānām āyaṃ tanvantivistṛṇvantīty āyatanāni sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi 'byung ba mched par byed cing rgyas par byed pas skye mched rnams te /
ātmalābhaṃ prabandhena sthāpayantīty arthaḥ bdag thob par byed pa rgyun du 'jog ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tatra cakṣū rūpāṇi ca sasamprayogasyacakṣurvijñānasyāyadvāram de la mig dang gzugs rnams ni mig gi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa skye ba'i sgo yin no /
evaṃ yāvan mano dharmāś casasamprayogasya manovijñānasyāyadvāram de bzhin du yid dang chos rnams kyi bar dag kyang yid kyi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'i skye ba'i sgo yin no /
āyatanānantaraṃ dhātavaḥ prabhedataḥ svarūpataś ca vaktavyāity ataḥ prabhedadarśanārtham āha aṣṭādaśa dhātava /
iti 		skye mched kyi 'og tu khams rnams rab tu dbye ba dang rang gi ngo bo brjod bar bya ste /
de bas na rab tu dbye ba bstan pa'i phyir /
khams bco brgyad ni zhes bya ba smos so /
teṣām eva svarūpapradarśanārtham āha cakṣurdhātū rūpadhātuś cakṣurvijñānadhātur evaṃ yāvanmanodhātur dharmadhātur /
manovijñānadhāturiti 		de dag nyid kyi rang rang gi ngo bo bstan pa'i phyir /
mig gi khams dang gzugs kyi khams dang mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang zhes bya ba nas de bzhin du yid kyi khams dang chos kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang zhes bya ba'i bar du smos so /
atra hi rūpaskandhavibhāgeyāni cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanasparśanāni pañcendriyāṇy uktāni pañca ca rūpaśabdagandharasasparśāḥteṣāṃviṣayatvena 'dir yang gzugs kyi phung po rnam par dbye ba ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi dbang po gang yin pa lnga po dag dang gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg pa lnga yang de dag gi yul nyid du bstan to /
āyatanavyavasthāyāṃ tāny eva pañcendriyāṇicakṣurādyāyatanatvenoktāni rūpādayaś ca viṣayārūpādyāyatanatvena skye mched rnam par gzhag par yang dbang po lnga po de dag nyid mig la sogs pa'i skye mched nyid dang gzugs la sogs pa'i yul rnams kyang gzugs la sogs pa'i skye mched nyid bstan to /
dhātuvyavasthāyāṃ ta eva cakṣurdhāturyāvat kāyadhātuḥ rūpadhātur yāvat spraṣṭavyadhātur ityuktam ity ata āha tatra cakṣurādidhātavo /
rūpādidhātavaś ca yathāyatanānīti 		khams rnam par gzhag pa yang de dag nyid mig gi khams nas lus kyi khams kyi bar dang gzugs kyi khams nas reg bya'i khams kyi bar du bstan te /
de'i phyir mig la sogs pa'i khams dang gzugs la sogs pa'i khams ni skye mched rnams ji lta ba bzhin no zhes bya ba smos so /
dharmadhātus tu yad eva dharmāyatanaṃ vedanādayas trayaḥskandhā avijñaptir asaṃskṛtacatuṣṭayaṃ ca chos kyi khams ni chos kyi skye mched tshor ba la sogs pa phung po gsum dang rnam bar rig byed ma yin pa dang 'dus ma byas pa zhi gang yin pa nyid do /
āyatanavyavasthāyāṃ vijñānaskandha eva manaāyatanam skye mched rnam par gzhag pa'i rnam par shes pa'i phung po nyid yid kyi skye mched do /
napunar evaṃdhātuvyavasthāyāṃ manaāyatanam evamanodhātuḥ kiṃ tarhi manaāyatanaṃ dhātuvyavasthāyāṃsapta cittadhātavaḥ /
ata āha ṣaḍ vijñānadhātava /
ityādi 		de bzhin du khams rnam par gzhag par yang yid kyi skye mched nyid kyi khams ma yin te /
yid kyi skye mched kyi khams rnam par gzhag pa na /
sems kye khams bdun no /
de'i phyir /
cakṣurādisanniśritā iticakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanakāyamanaḥsanniśritāḥ rnam par shes pa'i khams drug po dag ni zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
mig la sogs pa la brten te zhes bya ba ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid la brten te'o /
rūpādyālambanā itirūpaśabdagandharasasparśadharmālambanāḥ /
vijñaptaya /
iti vijñānāni 		gzugs la sogs pa la dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dang chos rnams ni dmigs pa'o /
rnam par rig pa'o zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'o /
tatra cakṣurāśrayaṃ rūpālambanaṃcakṣurvijñānaṃ cakṣurvijñānadhātuḥ de la mig la brten cing gzugs la dmigs pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste /
mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
evaṃśrot ragh rāṇarasanasparśanamanaāśrayā ṇ iśabdagandharasasparśadharmālambanāni yathākramaṃśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanovijñānāniśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanovijñānadhātavaḥ de bzhin du rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid la brten cing /
sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg dang chos rnams la go rims bzhin du dmigs pa ni rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams te; rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
manodhātuḥpunaḥ ṣaḍ vijñānavyatirikto na vidyate kiṃ tarhi ta evaṣaḍvijñānadhātavo 'nantaraniruddhā manodhātur ityucyate yid kyi khams ni rnam par shes pa drug las gud na med de /
rnam par shes pa'i khams drug po de dag nyid 'gag sam thog pa la yid kyi khams zhes bya'o /
r snanv evaṃ saptadaśa dhātavaḥ prāpnuvanti dvādaśa vāmanodhātoḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ cā vijñānadhātūnām itaretarāntarbhāvāt /
na prāpnuvanti yasmātṣaṣṭhavijñānāśrayaparidīpanārtham 		de ltar na yid kyi khams dang rnam par shes pa'i khams drug po dag gcig gi nang du gcig 'dus pa'i phyir khams bcu bdun nam bcu gnyis su mi 'gyur ram /
mi 'gyur te 'di ltar rnam par shes pa drug pa'i gnas bstan pa'i phyir /
aṣṭādaśadhātuvyavasthānam de ltar khams bco brgyad du rnam par gzhag go /
evam ityanantaroktaprakārapradarśanam de ltar zhes bya ba ni gong du smos pa'i rnam pa bstan pa'o /
yo rūpaskandha ity /
ekādaśadravyako hi rūpaskandha uktaḥ 		gzugs kyi phung po gang yin pa zhes bya ba la rdzas bcu gcig ni gzugs kyi phung po bstan te /
tatra pañcendriyāṇi cakṣurādīni pañca viṣayā rūpādayaāyatanavyavasthāyāṃdaśāyatanāni dhātuvyavasthāyāṃ daśa dhātavaḥ /
dharmāyatanaikadeśo dharmadhātvekadeśaś cāvijñaptyākhyaḥ /
yo vijñānaskandhaḥ sa 		de la mig la sogs pa dbang po lnga dang gzugs la sogs pa yul lnga ni skye mched rnam par gzhag par skye mched bcu dang; khams rnam par gzhag par khams bcu dang chos kyi skye mched kyi phyogs gcig dang chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig ni rnam par rig byed ma yin pa zhes bya'o /
manaāyatanaṃ cittadhātavaś casapta /
cakṣurvijñānadhātur yāvan manovijñānadhāturiti 		rnam par shes pa'i phung po gang yin pa de ni yid kyi skye mched dang sems kyi khams bdun no zhes bya ba ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams nas yid kyi khams kyi bar du'o /
ye 'nye /
rūpaskandhād vijñānaskandhāc ca trayovedanāsañjñāsaṃskārākhyāḥ skandhārūpaskandhapradeśaś cāvijñaptyākhyaḥ tedharmāyatanaṃ dharmadhātuś ca 		gzugs dang rnam par shes pa'i phung po las gzhan phung po gsum gang yin pa dag tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed ces bya ba'i phung po rnams so /
gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig ni rnam par rig byed ma yin pa zhes bya ste /
sahāsaṃskṛtenākāśādinā /
kenārthena dhātava ity āyatanārthavat vistareṇa /
vācyam /
nirvyāpārasvalakṣaṇadhāraṇārtheneti /
nirvyāpāraṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ dhārayantīti dhātavaḥ 		de dag 'dus ma byas nam mkha' la sogs pa dang bcas pa ni chos kyi skye mched dang chos kyi khams so /
ci'i phyir khams zhes bya zhe na zhes bya ba ni /
skye mched bzhin du rgya cher brjod par bya'o /
byed pa med la rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin pa'i phyir khams so /
na hikṣaṇikānāṃ vyāpāraḥ sambhavatīti pūrvam evoktam /
ya eva dharmāḥ skandhā iti deśitāḥ ta eva punar āyatanatvenadhātutvena cety ataḥ pṛcchati kimarthaṃ /
skandhādideśaneti /
sarvā hi deśanā bhagavatāṃbuddhānāṃ saprayojanā sattvārthapravṛttatvātkleśapratipakṣeṇa ca /
