na cātra prayojanaṃ vijñāyate punaḥpunas teṣām eva dharmāṇām anyenānyena ca prakāreṇadeśanā iti kimarthaṃ skandhādideśaneti prayojanaṃvaktavyam ity ata āha trividhātmagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti 		skad cig rnams la ni byed pa med par mi srid do zhes sngar bstan pa nyid do /
chos gang dag phung po zhes bstan pa de dag nyid skye mched nyid dang khams nyid du yang bshad pas de'i phyir /
ci'i phyir phung po la sogs pa bshad ce na zhes dris so /
sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis bshad pa thams cad ni sems can gyi don du 'gyur ba dang nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po yin pas dgos pa dang bcas pa'o /
'dir ni chos de dag nyid rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan gyis yang dang yang bshad pa'i dgos pa yang mi shes nas /
ci'i phyir phung po la sogs pa bshad ce na zhes bya ba ni dgos pa brjod do /
tatra navijñāyatekatamas trividha ātmagrāhaḥ katamasya vāpratipakṣeṇa katamā deśanety ata āha yathākramaṃ de'i phyir bdag tu 'dzin pa rnam pa gsum gyi gnyen por zhes bya ba smos so /
de la bdag tu 'dzin pa gsum dang gang gi gnyen por bshad pa yang mi shes pas de'i phyir go rims bzhin no zhes bya ba smos te /
trividha ātmagrāha ekatvagrāhobhoktṛtvagrāhaḥ kartṛtvagrāhaś ca /
tatra /
yathākramam iti skandhadeśanaikatvagrāhapratipakṣeṇaāyatanadeśanā bhokṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇadhātudeśanā kartṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti 		bdag tu 'dzin pa rnam pa gsum ni gcig pur 'dzin pa dang za bar 'dzin pa dang byed par 'dzin pa'o /
de la go rims bzhin zhes bya ba la phung po bshad pa ni gcig pur 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o /
skye mched bshad pa ni za bar 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o /
sarve hy ātmavādinaevaṃ pratipannāḥ ya eva paśyati sa eva śṛṇoti jighraty āsvādayatispṛśati ceti /
tatra ya eva vedayate sa eva cetayate sañjānītevijānātīti 		khams bshad pa ni byed par 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o /
bdag tu smra ba thams cad ni mthong ba gang yin pa de nyid thos pa dang snom pa dang ro myong ba dang reg pa yin pa dang de la de nyid sems par byed ba dang 'du shes su byed pa dang rnam par shes par byed pa'o snyam du de ltar 'dzin to /
na hi sattvātmabhāva evaṃ skandhavyatirikto 'nyaḥkaścid ekavyavasthitarūpo vidyatetatsvarūpakāryānupalabdheḥ sems can rnams kyi lus la ni phung po lnga las gud na gcig pur rnam par gnas pa'i ngo bo gang yang med de /
rang gi ngo bo dang 'bras bu mi dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
na cakṣurvyatirekeṇānyo draṣṭā vidyate /
cakṣur eva hi darśanākhyasya vijñānasyāsādhāraṇaṃkāraṇam āśrayaś cetidraṣṭṛtvenopacaryate /
evaṃ pratyekaṃśrotrādiṣu vaktavyam 		mig las gud na lta ba po gzhan med de /
mig nyid mthong ba'o zhes rnam par shes pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rgyu dang gnas yin pas lta ba po zhes gdags so /
de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa so so la yang brjod par bya'o /
evaṃ vedanānubhavātmakatvātvedayate de bzhin du tshor ba ni myong ba'i bdag nyid yin pas myong bar byed /
sañjñaiva nimittodgrahaṇātmikatvāt sañjānītenānyaity evaṃ sarvatra vācyam 'du shes nyid mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid yin pas 'du shes su byed kyi gzhan ni ma yin te /
de ltar thams cad du yang brjod par bya'o /
tasmān nātmabhāvaḥ sattvānāṃ pañcaskandhātmakatvādekavastvātmakaḥ de lta bas na sems can rnams kyi lus ni phung po'i bdag nyid yin pas dngos po du ma'i bdag nyid can no /
na caskandhavyatirikto 'tra eko vidyate 'di la ni phung po lnga las gud na gcig pu med de /
ekatvagrāhe vyāvartiteskandhadeśanayā yas tatraikatvagrāhapūrvaka ātmagrāhaḥasāv api vyāvartita evety ataekatvagrāhapūrvātmagrāhapratipakṣeṇa skandhadeśanā phung po bstan pas gcig pu 'dzin pa ldog pa na de la gcig pur 'dzin pa sngon du 'gro ba'i bdag tu 'dzin pa gang yin pa de yang ldog pa nyid de /
de'i phyir gcig pur 'dzin pa sngon du 'gro ba'i bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gnyen por phung po bshad do /
ekatvagrāhas tu kāraṇe kāryopacāraṃ kṛtvātmagrāha ity uktaḥ gcig pur 'dzin pa ni rgyu la 'bras bu btags nas bdag tu 'dzin pa zhes bya bar bshad do /
bhoktṛgrāhaḥ punaḥ sarvavādināṃ yaḥ śubhāśubhasyakarmaṇa iṣṭāniṣṭaṃ sukhaduḥkhavedanāprabhāvitaṃ phalamupabhuṅkte rūpaśabdādīṃś ca viṣayān sa ātmeti za bar 'dzin pa ni smra ba thams cad ci ltar na las dge ba dang mi dge ba'i 'bras bu 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa dang bde ba dang sdug bsngal gyi tshor bas rab tu phye ba dang gzugs dang sgra la sogs pa yul la gang sbyod pa de bdag go zhes so /
syātmagrāhasya pratipakṣeṇāyatanadeśanā de ltar na bdag tu 'dzin pa 'di'i gnyen por skye mched bshad do /
śubhāśubhakarmaphalasya rūpādīnāṃ ca viṣayāṇāmupabhuktir upalabdhiḥ las dge ba dang mi dge ba'i 'bras bu dang gzugs la sogs pa yul rnams la spyod pa ni dmigs pa ste /
tāṃ yaḥ karotisa karmaphalasyarūpādīnāṃ copabhoktā de byed pa gang yin pa de ni las kyi 'bras bu dang gzugs la sogs pa la spyod do /
tāṃ ṣaṭprakārām upalabdhimāyatanāny eva kurvanti nānyaḥ dmigs pa rnam pa drug de yang skye mched nyid kyis byed kyi gzhan gyis ni ma yin no /
ata eva cakṣurādayorūpādayaś ca vijñānāyadvārārthenāyatanānīty ucyante de'i phyir mig la sogs pa dang gzugs la sogs pa ni rnam par shes pa skye ba'i sgo'i phyir skye mched rnams zhes bya'o /
tasmānnāsti kaścid anyaścakṣurādivyatirekeṇa karmaphalasyaviṣayāṇāṃ copabhoktety evam āyatanadeśanābhoktṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti de lta bas na las kyi 'bras bu dang yul rnams la spyod pa ni mig la sogs pa las gud na gzhan gang yang med de /
de ltar na skye mched bshad pa ni za bar 'dzin pa'i gnyen po zhes bya'o /
kartṛtvagrāhaḥ punar yaḥśubhāśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kartā valganāsphoṭanādīnāṃ casaātmā byed par 'dzin pa ni las dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams 'brel ba dang sprugs bsigs pa la sogs pa byed pa ste /
asyātmagrāhasya pratipakṣeṇa dhātudeśanā bdag tu 'dzin pa 'di'i gnyen por khams bshad do /
tathā hinirvyāpārasvalakṣaṇadhāraṇārthena dhātava uktāḥ /
evaṃkāraṇaṃ sattāmātreṇa kāryotpattiṃ prati vyāpriyate kāryaṃca sattāmātreṇaiva kāraṇam apekṣate 		de ltar na byed pa med la rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin pa'i phyir khams zhes bstan to /
de ltar rgyu yod pa tsam gyis 'bras bu yang 'byung bar byed cing 'bras bu yang rgyu la ltos nas yod pa tsam du zad de /
na cakāryakāraṇasvarūpavyatirekeṇānyā kriyāsti tat pūrvam evapratipāditam /
kriyām antareṇa ca kutaḥ kartā 		rgyu dang 'bras bu'i rang gi ngo bo las ma gtogs par byed pa gzhan med par sngar bstan pa nyid do /
byed pa med par byed pa po ga la yod de /
tasmāt kartṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇa dhātudeśaneti de lta bas na byed par 'dzin pa'i gnyen por khams bshad pa yin no /
idānīṃ dharmapravicayānugrahārthaṃ ya evaskandhāyatanadhātutvena dharmā nirdiṣṭāḥ teṣām evaprakārāś cintyante de ni chos gang dag rab tu rnam par dbye bas phan gdags pa'i phyir phung po dang skye mched dang khams nyid du chos gang dag bstan pa de dag la rnam pa gzhan gyis bsam par bya ste /
tatra dhātuṣu rūpacittayor vibhaktatvenavistarāpadeśāt sāsravaprakārādīnāṃ sukhagamyo nirdeśa iti dhātūn evārabhya cintyate na skandhāyatanānity ata evāha aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ kati rūpiṇa ityādi de la khams rnams kyi nang du gzugs dang sems gnyis rnam par dbye ba lhag par bstan pas zag pa dang bcas pa'i rnam pa la sogs pa bde blag tu rtogs par 'gyur ba'i phyir khams ga las brtsams te /
bsam par bya ba'i phung po dang skye mched rnams la ni ma yin no /
de'i phyir khams bco brgyad la gzugs can du zhe na zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
rūpaṇaṃ rūpaṃ tad eṣām astīti rūpiṇaḥ gzugs su yod pas gzugs te /
'di dag la yod pas gzugs can no /
āśrayāśritaṃ rūpaṃ vā yathāsambhavam eṣām astīti rūpiṇaḥ yang na rten dang brten pa'i gzugs ji ltar mthun mthun du 'di dag la yod pas gzugs can no /
na ca cakṣurādivijñāneṣuprasaṅgaḥ cakṣurādīnām ādhāratvena teṣām anāśrayatvāt mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa la thal bar yang mi 'gyur te /
mig la sogs pa rten gyi dngos po de dag gi gzhi byed pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
ye rūpaskandhasvabhāvā iti /
te punaḥdaśa dhātavaḥ 		gang dag gzugs kyi phung po'i ngo bo nyid do zhes bya ba de dag ni khams bcu ste /
cakṣurdhātur yāvat kāyadhātuḥ rūpadhātur yāvatspraṣṭavyadhātuḥ mig gi khams nas lus kyi bar dang gzugs kyi khams nas reg bya'i khams kyi bar du'o /
avijñaptirūpe saty api na dharmadhātorūpitvaprasaṅgas tasyāśrayāśritarūpābhāvād rūpaṇābhāvādrūpaskandhāsaṅgrahāc ca /
katy arūpiṇaḥ /
śeṣāḥ /
rūpiviparyayeṇa ye 		rnam par rig byed ma yin pa gzugs su yod du zin kyang chos kyi khams gzugs can nyid du thal bar mi 'gyur te /
de la rten dang brten pa'i gzugs med pa dang gzugs su yod pa med pa dang gzugs kyi phung por gtogs su zin kyang gzugs su yod pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
gzugs can ma yin pa du zhe na /
lhag ma rnams so zhes bya ba la gzugs can las ldog pa ni gzugs can ma yin pa ste /
te punar /
aṣṭau sapta cittadhātavo dharmadhātuś ca /
kati sanidarśanā iti /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti 		de dag ni brgyad de /
sems kyi khams bdun dang chos kyi khams so /
bstan du yod pa du zhe na zhes bya ba ni khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas der sbyar ro /
prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate /
eko rūpadhāturiti /
idamihāmutretiayam ayam? eva vyapadeśo nidarśanam /
tena sahavartata iti sanidarśanaḥ sālambanavat 		gzugs kyi khams gcig ste zhes bya ba la 'di ni 'di na'o zhes /
pha bi ni pha bi na'o zhes bstan du rung ba de ni bstan pa'o /
de dang lhan cig pa ni bstan du yod pa ste /
dmigs pa dang bcas pa bzhin no /
idam evanidarśanārthaṃ prabhāvayann āha deśanidarśaneneti /
tasmiṃs tasmin deśe nidarśyate 'neneti deśanidarśanam /
ekasyaiva rūpadhātoḥ sanidarśanatvena parigrahātśeṣāḥsaptadaśa cakṣurādidhātavaḥ pañca śabdādidhātavaś catvārodharmadhātur ekaḥ sapta cittadhātavaḥ anidarśanā itisiddham /
kati sapratighāḥ /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ prakṛtatvāt /
sarvatra sambadhyate 		bstan du yod pa 'di nyid rab tu bstan pa'i phyir /
yul bstan du yod pa'o zhes bya ba smos te /
yul de dang der 'dis bstan du yod pas yul bstan du yod pa'o zhes bya'o /
gzugs kyi khams gcig kho na bstan du yod pa nyid du smos pas lhag ma khams bcu bdun ni bstan du med par grub bo /
thogs pa dang bcas pa du zhen zhes bya ba ni khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas thams cad du yang sbyar ro /
gzugs can ma yin pa rnam par gcad pa'i phyir gzugs can smos so /
dharmadhātāv apyavijñaptirūpasadbhāvād asti rūpivyapadeśa itidaśety āha /
arūpivyavacchedārthaṃrūpigrahaṇam 		chos kyi khams la yang rnam par rig byed ma yin pa'i gzugs yod pas /
gzugs can yod par bstan pa'i phyir bcu zhes bya ba smos so /
te punaścakṣurādīndriyadhātavaḥpañca tadviṣayā rūpādidhātavaś capañca /
pratighātaḥ pratighaḥ /
tena sahavartanta itisapratighāḥ 		de dag kyang mig la sogs pa dbang po'i khams rnams dang de dag gi yul gzugs can gyi khams lnga'o /
go gcod pas thogs pa ste /
de dang lhan cig pa ni thogs pa dang bcas pa'o /
dpratighātas triprakāro viṣayālambanāvaraṇapratighātabhedāt go gcod pa ni yul dang dmigs pa dang sgrib pas go gcod pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa gsum mo /
iha tv āvaraṇapratighātenaiva sapratighatvam iṣṭam itipratipādayann āha yatra yaś ca pratihanyata iti 'dir ni sgrib pa'i go gcod pa nyid thogs pa dang bcas par 'dod pa bstan pa'i phyir gang la gang thogs pa'o zhes bya ba smos so /
āvaraṇapratighāto hi svadeśe parasyotpattipratibandhaḥ sgrib pa'i go gcod pa ni rang gi yul du gzhan 'byung ba'i gegs su gyur pa'o /
evaṃca yenānyasya svadeśa utpattiḥ pratibadhyate yasya ca pratibadhyate tadubhayam api sapratigham iti jñāpitaṃbhavati de ltar na gang gis rang gi yul du gzhan 'byung ba'i gegs byed pa dang gang la gegs byed pa de gnyi ga yang thogs pa dang bcas pa zhes bstan pa yin no /
etena ca daśa rūpiṇo dhātavaḥparasparasya svadeśautpattiṃ pratibadhnantīty āvaraṇapratighātena sapratighāḥśeṣāḥ sapta cittadhātavo dharmadhātuś cāpratighāiti /
siddham /
kati sāsravāḥ /
dhātūnām iti prakṛtam /
pañcadaśa /
trayāṇāṃ ca paścimānāṃ bhāga iti /
cakṣurādayaḥ /
pañcendriyadhātavo rūpādayaḥpañca viṣayadhātavaḥ pañcacakṣurādivijñānadhātavaś ca ete pañcadaśaekāntena sāsravāeva /
ādyāapi trayo vidyante cakṣūrūpacakṣurvijñānadhātavaity ata āha paścimānām iti /
paścimās trayomanodhāturdharmadhātur manovijñānadhātuś ca /
teṣām api bhāgo 'ṃśaḥsāsravaḥ na tu cakṣurādivat sarva eva sāsravāḥ /
teṣāṃ punaryo namārgasatyāsaṃskṛtasvabhāvo bhāgaḥsa eva sāsravaḥ /
sāsravaiḥ saha vartanta iti sāsravāḥ /
ata evāha teṣukleśotpattita iti /
teṣu yasmāt kleśā utpadyante tesāsravāiti 		khams gzugs can bcu po de dag kyang rang rang gi yul du 'byung ba la gcig la gcig gegs byed pas sgrib cing go gcod pa'i phyir thogs pa dang bcas pa rnams so /
lhag ma sems kyi khams bdun dang chos kyi khams ni thogs pa med par grub po zag pa dang bcas pa du zhe na zhes bya ba ni khams kyi skabs yin no /
bco lnga dang tha ma gsum gyi cha ste zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pa dbang po lnga'i khams dang gzugs la sogs pa yul lnga'i khams dang mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa rnam par shes pa'i khams lnga ste /
khams bco lnga po dag ni gcig tu zag pa dang bcas pa nyid do /
dang po la yang gsum yod de /
mig dang gzugs dang mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams yin pas de'i phyir tha ma zhes smos so /
tha ma gsum ni yid kyi khams dang chos kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
de dag gi cha ni cha shas te /
zag pa dang bcas pa'o /
mig la sogs pa bzhin du thams cad zag pa dang bcas pa nyid ni ma yin no /
de dag las kyang lam gyi bden pa dang 'dus ma byas kyi rang bzhin gyi cha ma yin pa de nyid zag pa dang bcas pa ste /
zag pa dang lhan cig pas zag pa dang bcas pa'o /
de'i phyir de dag nyon mongs pa skye ba zhes bya ba smos te /
'di ltar de dag las nyon mongs pa skye bas de'i phyir zag pa dang bcas pa zhes bya'o /
cakṣurādivijñānānām avikalpakatvātkathaṃ rūpādiṣukleśotpattiḥ mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams ni /
rnam par mi rtog pa yin pas ji ltar gzugs la sogs pa rnams la nyon mongs pa skyed ce na /
nocyate cakṣurādivijñānair eva saha rūpādiṣukleśā utpadyanta itikiṃ tarhi pratyakṣagocaratāmupādāya rūpādiṣu kleśotpattir ucyate nyon mongs pa rnams mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams dang lhan cig tu gzugs la sogs pa la 'byung ba zhes mi bya mod kyi /
'on kyang mngon sum gyi spyod yul gyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni gzugs la sogs pas nyon mongs la skyed pa ste /
tathā hi cakṣuś capratītya rūpāṇi ca pratītya cakṣurvijñānam utpadyatecakṣurvijñānānubhūtāni rūpāṇi manovijñānena vikalpyantevikalpāc ca kleśā utpadyante iti /
evaṃ śeṣeṣv api vācyam /
katy anāsravāḥ /
trayāṇāṃ paścimānāṃ /
bhāgaḥ /
manodharmamanovijñānadhātūnāṃ yomārgasatyāsaṃskṛtasaṅgṛhītaḥ pradeśaḥ so 'nāsrava iti /
kati kāmapratisaṃyuktāḥ /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām /
iti sambadhyate /
pañca rūpādayo viṣayāḥ kāmyanta iti kāmāḥ /
tatpradhāno dhātuḥ kāmadhātuḥ /
tatpratisaṃyuktāḥkāmapratisaṃyuktā ity ucyante 		'di ltar mig la brten cing gzugs la sogs pa la brten nas mig gi rnam par shes pa 'byung ste /
mig gi rnam par shes pas myong ba'i gzugs rnams la yid kyi rnam par shes pas rnam par rtog par byed pas rnam par rtog pa las nyon mongs pa 'byung ste /
de bzhin du lhag ma rnams la yang brjod par bya'o /
zag pa med pa du zhe na /
tha ma gsum gyi cha'o zhes bya ba ni yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams rnams kyi'o /
lam gyi bden pa dang 'dus ma byas su gtogs pa'i phyogs gang yin pa de ni zag pa med pa'o /
'dod pa dang ldan pa du zhe na zhes bya ba ni khams bco brgyad ces bya ba dang sbyar te /
gzugs la sogs pa yul lnga ni 'dod par bya ba yin pas 'dod pa rnams te /
de gces su byed pa'i khams rnams ni 'dod pa'i khams su shes par bya'o /
athavākāmadhātupratisaṃyuktā iti vaktavye dhātuśabdalopātkāmapratisaṃyuktā ity uktāḥ yang na 'dod pa'i khams dang ldan pa du zhe na zhes brjod pa'i rigs pa las khams zhes bya ba'i sgra ma smos pa 'dod pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba smos so /
kāmapratisaṃyuktāḥ kāmadhātusaṅgṛhītāḥ kāmadhātusvabhāvā ity arthaḥ 'dod pa'i khams dang ldan pa dag ni 'dod pa'i khams kyis bsdus pa rnams te /
'dod pa'i khams kyi ngo bo nyid ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tathāyatra kāmatṛṣṇāsamudācāraḥ tat sarvaṃkāmadhātusaṅgṛhītam /
te punaḥsarve ṣaḍ indriyadhātavaḥṣaḍ viṣayadhātavaḥ ṣaḍ vijñānadhātavaś ca /
kati rūpapratisaṃyuktāḥ /
caturdaśa 		'di ltar gang du 'dod pa'i sred pa kun du 'byung ba thams cad 'dod pa'i khams su bsdus pa'o /
de dag kyang dbang po'i khams drug dang yul gyi khams drug dang rnam par shes pa'i khams drug go /
gzugs dang ldan pa du zhe na /
bcu bzhi ste /
tatra ṣaḍ /
cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanaindriyadhātavaḥ catvāroviṣayadhātavaḥ tadviṣayavijñānadhātavaś catvāraḥ ete caturdaśa rūpadhātupratisaṃyuktāḥ 		mig dang rna ba dang sna dang; lce dang lus dang yid kyi dbang po'i khams dang yul bzhi dang yul de'i rnam par shes pa'i khams bzhi ste /
bcu bzhi po de dag ni gzugs kyi khams dang ldan pa'o /
kim punaḥ kāraṇaṃgandharasayo rūpadhātau na bhāvas tadvijñānayoś ca ci'i phyir gzugs kyi khams na dri dang ro dang de'i rnam par shes pa gnyis kyang med ce na /
gandharasau hy ekāntenakavaḍīkārāhārasvabhāvāv evana tu sparśavedanāhārasvabhāvau /
api cakavaḍīkārāhāravītarāgāś ca rūpadhātāv upapadyanteyadvītarāgāś ca yatropapadyante tatra tasyābhāvaḥ tadyathārūpavītarāgāṇām ārūpyāpattau cakṣurādīnām /
viṣayābhāvāc cagandharasavijñānayor apy abhāvaḥ 		dri dang ro ni gcig tu kham gyi zas kyi ngo bo nyid yin gyi reg pa dang sems pa'i zas kyi ngo bo nyid ma yin no /
yang kham gyi zas kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams ni gzugs kyi khams su skye ste /
gang gi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams gang du skyes pa de na med de /
dper na /
'dod chags dang bral ba gzugs med par skyes pa'i mig la sogs pa bzhin du yul med pa'i phyir dri dang ro'i rnam par shes pa gnyis kyang med do /
katy ārūpyapratisaṃyuktāḥ /
paścimās /
trayaḥ 		gzugs med pa dang ldan pa du zhe na /
tha ma gsum zhes bya ba ni /
manodhātur dharmadhātur manovijñānadhātuś ca yid kyi khams dang; chos kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
rūpavītarāgā hy ārūpyadhātāv utpadyante /
atas tatra daśarūpasvabhāvā dhātavas tadāśrayālambanāś ca pañcavijñānadhātavo na santi /
katy apratisaṃyuktāḥ /
ye'nāsravāḥ /
ye /
kāmarūpārūpyatṛṣṇābhir nālambyante 		gzugs kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams ni gzugs med pa'i khams su skye ste /
de'i phyir de na gzugs kyi ngo bo nyid kyi khams bcu dang de la brten pa dang dmigs pa rnam par shes pa'i khams lnga med do /
mi ldan pa du zhe na gsum gyi cha'o zhes bya ba ni gang dag 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i sred pa rnams kyis ma dmigs pa ste /
dhātutrayaviyuktatvādapratisaṃyuktāḥ /

kati kuśalāḥ /
katy akuśalāḥ /
katy /
avyākṛtāḥ 		khams gsum dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i phyir mi ldan pa'o /
lam gyi bden pa dang 'dus ma byas kyi ngo bo nyid gang yin pa'i yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams de dag ni zag pa med pa'o /
dge ba du /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate mi dge ba du /
lung du ma bstan pa du zhe na /
khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas der sbyar ro /
tatra kutsitāc chalitam iti kuśalam gatam ityarthaḥ /
kuśeti vā prajñāparyāyaḥ /
lā ādāne 		de la ngan pa bsnyil ba'i phyir dge ba ste /
song zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
yang na ku sha ni shes rab kyi rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o /
la ni len pa ste /
prajñāparigṛhītāḥ prajñāparigrāhakā vā kuśalāḥ /
kutsitena vākāreṇa śerata itikuśāḥ chedakā vedhakāś ceti /
lā ādāne 		shes rab kyis yongs su zin pa'am /
shes rab yongs su 'dzin pa ni dge ba rnams so /
yang na ngan pa'i rnam par 'dug pa ni rtsva ku sha ste /
yaśchedanavedhanaparihāreṇa kuśān ādatte sa kuśala ity ucyate /
evam anyo 'pi yasyāṃ kriyāyāṃ praśaṃsām arhati sa kuśalastatrocyate 		gcod pa dang 'bigs pa'o /
la ni len pa ste /
su zhig gcod pa dang 'bigs pa spangs te /
rtsva ku sha rnams len pa de ni mkhas pa zhes bya'o /
de bzhin du gzhan bya ba gang la bsngags par 'os pa de ni dge ba zhes bya'o /
etenākuśalaṃ vyākhyātam /
kuśalākuśalabhāvenāvyākaraṇād avyākṛtāḥ 		'dis mi dge ba bzlog ste bshad do /
dge ba dang mi dge ba'i dngos por lung du bstan pa med pas ma bstan pa'o /
daśa trividhā /
iti kuśalā apy akuśalā apy avyākṛtā api 		bcu ni rnam pa gsum char te zhes bya ba ni dge ba yang yin /
mi dge ba yang yin /
lung du ma bstan pa yang yin no /
te tu na vijñāyantaaṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ katame daśety āha saptacittadhātavor srūpaśabdadharmadhātavaśceti khams pa co brgyad kyi nang nas bcu gang zhes bya ba de dag kyang mi shes nas /
sems kyi khams bdun dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos kyi khams so zhes bya ba smos so /
atra cittadhātūnāṃ samprayogataḥ kuśalākuśalatvam na svataḥ kuśalākuśalamūlānāṃ ceti de la sems kyi khams rnams ni mtshungs par ldan pas dge ba dang mi dge ba nyid yin gyi /
ngo bo nyid kyi ni ma yin te /
dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams dang mtshungs par ldan pas so /
tatra sapta cittadhātavo 'lobhādveṣāmohasamprayuktāḥ kuśalāḥ de la sems kyi khams bdun ma chags pa dang zhe sdang med pa dang gti mug med pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa rnams ni dge ba'o /
lobhadveṣamohasamprayuktāakuśalāḥ chags pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug dang mtshungs par ldan pa rnams ni mi dge ba'o /
anya avyākṛtāḥ gzhan dag ni lung du ma bstan pa'o /
rūpaśabdadhātū kuśalākuśalacittasamutthāpitau kuśalākuśalaukāyavāgvijñaptisaṅgṛhītau /
ato 'nyāv avyākṛtau 		gzugs dang sgra'i khams lus dang ngag gi rnam par rig byed du bsdus pa dge ba dang mi dge ba'i sems kyis kun nas bslang ba ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'o /
de las gzhan pa ni lung du ma bstan pa'o /
dharmadhāturalobhādisvabhāvasamprayuktasamutthaḥ pratisaṅkhyānirodhastathatā ca kuśalaḥ chos kyi khams kyang ma chags pa la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang kun nas bslang ba dang so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa dang de bzhin nyid ni dge ba'o /
lobhādisvabhāvasamprayuktasamuttho'kuśalaḥ chags pa la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang kun nas bslang ba ni mi dge ba'o /
tato'nyo 'vyākṛtaḥ /

brgyad ni lung du ma bstan pa ste /
gandharasasparśāḥ pañca cakṣurādayaḥ /

de dag ni lung du ma bstan pa nyid de /
don dam pa dang ngo bo nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang kun nas bslang bas dge ba dang mi dge ba ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
katy ādhyātmikāḥ /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti 		nang gi du zhe na; khams bco brgyad ces bya bar sbyar ro /
sambadhyate /
dvādaśa /
te tu na prajñāyante katamedvādaśety āha rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyadharmadhāt /
ūn sthāpayitveti /
śeṣāḥṣaḍ indriyadhātavaḥ ṣaḍvijñānadhātava ity ete dvādaśādhyātmikāḥ 		bcu gnyis te bcu gnyis gang yin pa de dag kyang mi shes pas /

lhag ma dbang po'i khams drug dang rnam par shes pa'i khams drug ste /

ṣaṭ /

ye sthāpitāḥ /

de dag kyang mi shes nas /
de'i phyir gang dag ma gtogs pa rnams so zhes bya ba smos so /
'di dag ni phyi'i yin par shes par bya'o /
ke ca sthāpitāḥ /
rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyadharmadhātavaḥ 		ma gtogs pa rnams gang zhe na /
gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dang chos kyi khams rnams so /
adhy ātmānam adhyātmam /
adhyātmam evādhyātmikam 		bdag gi dbang du byas pa ni nang zhes bya ba ste /
nang nyid nang ngo /
ātmanyasati katham ādhyātmikaṃ bāhyaṃ vābhavati bdag nyid med na nang ngam phyi zhes bya bar ji ltar 'gyur te /
na hi śīle 'satyadhiśīlaṃ śikṣā yujyate tshul khrims med na tshul khrims kyi dbang du byas pa'i bslab pa mi rung ba bzhin no zhe na /
ahaṅkārasanniśritatvāc cittam ātmety upacaryate ngar 'dzin pa'i gnas yin pa'i phyir sems la bdag ces 'dogs so /
ahaṅkārasanniśrayo hy ātmavādibhir ātmetyabhidhīyate /
tathā hy ātmaguṇatvenātmaviṣayatvenacāhaṅkāraṃ pratipannāḥ 		ngar 'dzin pa'i gzhi ni bdag tu smra ba rnams kyis bdag ces brjod de /
'di ltar bdag gi yon tan nam /
bdag yul nyid du ngar 'dzin pa rtogs so /
ahaṅkāraś ca cittasanniśritastadvyatiriktātmābhāvāt /
āhito 'haṃmāna etasminn ity ātmā 		ngar 'dzin pa yang sems la brten pa ste /
de las gud na bdag med pa'i phyir ro /
de la nga'o snyam du nga rgyal skyed pas bdag ste /
cittam eva caittānām āśraya iti cittam evātmatvenopacaryate /
kathaṃ punar etad gamyate 'trātmatvena cittam abhipretam iti 		sems nyid sems las byung ba rnams kyi gnas yin pas sems nyid la bdag tu 'dogs so /
'dir sems la bdag ces bya bar bzhed par 'di ci mngon zhe na /
uktaṃ hi bhagavatā ātmanā hi sudāntena svargaṃ prāpnotipaṇḍitaiti bcom ldan 'das kyis /
bdag ni legs par dul gyur na /
mkhas pas mtho ris thob par 'gyur /
zhes gsungs so /
cittasya cānyatra damanam uktam cittasyadamanaṃ sādhu cittaṃ dāntaṃ sukhāvahamiti gzhan nas kyang sems 'dul ba gsungs te /
sems 'dul ba ni legs pa ste /
sems 'dul bde ba thob par byed /
ce'o /
atra hi cittasyadamanaṃ cittam eva dāntaṃ sukhāvaham ity uktam 'dir sems 'dul ba dang sems nyid dul na bde ba thob par byed /
ces gsungs pas de'i phyir /
ato 'trāpy ātmanā hi sudāntena svargaṃ prāpnoti paṇḍita iti cittamevābhipretam iti vijñāyate bdag ni legs par dul gyur na /
mkhas pas mtho ris thob par 'gyur /
zhes bya ba 'dir yang sems nyid la bya bar bzhed par mngon no /
ataś cātmabhūtasyacittasyāśrayabhāvena pratyāsannatvāc cakṣurādīnāmādhyātmikatvam de'i phyir bdag tu lta ba'i sems kyi rten gyi dngos por nye bar gyur pa'i phyir mig la sogs pa ni nang gi nyid do /
rūpādīnāṃ ca viṣayabhāvād bāhyatvam gzugs la sogs pa yul gyi dngos por gyur pa ni phyi'i nyid do /
evaṃ tarhi ṣaḍ vijñānadhātava ādhyātmikā na prāpnuvanti nahy ete manodhātutvam aprāptāś cittasyāśrayībhavantīti /
yadātadā ta eva te bhavantīti lakṣaṇaṃ nātivartantaiti 		de ltar na ni rnam par shes pa'i khams drug nang gir mi 'gyur te /
de dag yid kyi khams nyid du ma gyur gyi bar du sems kyi rten du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro zhe na /
nam du yang rung ste /
de dag nyid nad yin pas mtshan nyid las 'da' ba med do /
kati sālambanādhātava iti prakṛtam /
ata āha sapteti 		dmigs pa dang bcas pa du zhe na zhes bya ba ni khams kyi skabs yin pas de'i phyir bdun zhes bya ba smos so /
te 'pi na jñāyante katamesaptety ata āha cittadhātavaiti /
kim eta eva sālambanāḥ /
na kiṃ tarhidharmadhātupradeśaśca 		bdun po de dag kyang gang yin mi shes pas de'i phyir sems kyi khams zhes bya ba smos so /

ma yin te /
chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig kyang yin te /

astyamīṣām ālambanam iti sālambanāḥ 		kyang gi sgra ni bsdu'o /

'di dag la dmigs pa yod pas dmigs pa dang bcas pa'o /

śeṣāḥ 		sems kyi khams bdun ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa rnams so /

pañcendriyadhātavaś cakṣurādayaḥ pañca viṣayadhātavorūpādayo dharmadhātupradeśaś cayo nacaitasikasvabhāvaḥ /
kati vikalpakāḥ 		mig la sogs pa dbang po'i khams lnga dang gzugs la sogs pa yul gyi khams lnga'o /

rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa du zhe na /

etau /
hy abhinirūpaṇānusmaraṇavikalpābhyāṃ samprayuktau tāveva vikalpakau netarau tābhyām asamprayogāt /
dharmadhātupradeśo 'pi samprayuktaḥ netaraḥ 		'di gnyis ni mngon par dpyod pa dang rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa ste /
de nyid rnam par rtog pa yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin te /
de gnyis dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
chos kyi khams kyi phyogs ni mtshungs par ldan pa can te /
gzhan ni ma yin no /
tatrānusmaraṇavikalpaḥ smṛtir eva mānasy anub hūtā lamb anās ampr amoṣ ākār ā de la rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni dran pa nyid la bya ste /
yid kyi myong ba'i dmigs pa ma brjed pa rnams so /
traiyadhvikaparokṣārthābhyūhanākāra idam evaṃ naivam itiprajñāviśeṣaś cetanā vā 'bhirūpaṇāvikalpaḥ dus gsum gyi don lkog tu gyur pa la mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam pa 'di ni 'di lta yin gyi de lta ma yin no zhes bya ba shes rab kyi khyad par la'am /
sems pa ni mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa ste /
yathoktam abhidharmasamuccaye anusmaraṇavikalpaḥ katamaḥ /
yo'nubhūtapūrvasaṃskārākāraḥ 		chos mngon pa kun las btus pa las ji skad du /
rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang zhe na /
gang sngon myong ba la 'du byed bskyed pa'o /
abhinirūpaṇāvikalpaḥ katamaḥ mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang zhe na /
yo 'tītānāgatavartamāneṣu viparokṣeṣv abhyūhanākārovikalpaḥ gang 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi don lkog tu gyur pa rnams la mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o zhes bshad pa lta bu'o /
śeṣā avikalpakā iti siddham lhag ma rnams ni rnam par mi rtog par 'grub ste /
te punaḥ pañcadaśa dhātavo /
dharmadhātoś ca pradeśaḥ /
ete hy avikalpakā eva 		de dag kyang khams bco lnga ste /
chos kyi khams kyi phyogs te /
de dag ni rnam par mi rtog pa nyid do /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃkaty upāttāḥ /
pañcādhyātmikāḥ 		khams bco brgyad las zin pa du zhe na /
nang gi lnga ste /
te punaścakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanakāyadhātavaḥ /
ete hy upāttā eva /
nanu cānyatraite dvidhā nirdiṣṭāḥ 		de dag ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi khams te /
de dag ni zin pa nyid do /
gzhan las 'di dag gnyis su ma bstan tam /
satyaṃ nirdiṣṭāḥ tatra hyatītānāgatā anupāttāuktāḥ te ca na santy eva bstan mod kyi de la yang 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa ni zin pa ma yin par brjod de /
de ni med pa nyid do /
na cāsataupāttatvam anupāttatvaṃ vā yujyate med pa ni zin pa'am ma zin pa yin par brjod du mi rung ngo /
vartamānās tusvasattādhyāsitatvāt cittacaittaiś copāttatvād upāttā evacakṣurādayaḥ nānupāttāḥ da ltar ni rang yod par gnas pa dang sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyis zin pa'i phyir zin pa nyid de /
mig la sogs pa ni ma zin pa ma yin no /
kiṃ cakṣurādaya eva pañcopāttāḥ ci mig la sogs pa lnga po nyid zin pa dag gang zhe na /
ma yin te /
na kiṃ tarhi caturṇāṃ ca pradeśaḥ /
katameṣāṃcaturṇām ity atra āha rūparasagandhaspraṣṭavyānām iti 		bzhi'i phyogs te /
bzhi po de dag gang yin snyam pa la de'i phyir /
gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg bya rnams kyi'o zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra ye /
srūpagandharasaspraṣṭavyadhātava indriyāvinirbhāgavartinaḥte indriyavad upāttāḥ 		de la gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg bya'i khams dbang po las tha dad du mi 'jug pa gang dag yin pa de dag dbang po dag bzhin du zin pa rnams so /
gzhan dag ni ma zin pa dag ste /
anye 'nupāttāḥ tadyathā mūlavarjyeṣukeśaromanakhadanteṣu viṇmūtrakheṭasiṅghāṇakaśoṇitādiṣubhūmyudakādiṣu ca 'di lta ste /
drung ma gtogs pa'i skra dang spu dang sen mo dang so dang phyi sa dang gcin dang mchil ma dang snabs dang khrag la sogs pa dang sa dang chu la sogs pa rnams so /
upāttam iti ko 'rthaḥ /
yac cittacaittairadhiṣṭhānabhāvenopagṛhītam anugrahopaghātābhyāmanyonyānuvidhānāt /
yal lokesacetanam ity ucyate /
katy anupāttāḥ 		zin pa zhes bya ba'i don ci zhe na /
phan pa dang gnod pa gnyis kyis phan tshun rjes su 'gyur ba'i phyir gang sems dang sems las byung ba de rnams kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i gnas kyi dngos por zin pa dang 'jig rten na sems bcas pa zhes bya'o /
zin pa ma yin pa du zhe na /
śeṣā navacaturṇāṃ ca /
pradeśaḥ /
upayuktebhyo ye 'nye te śeṣāḥ /
ataḥsaptacittadhātavo dharmadhātuḥ śabdadhātuś ca 		lhag ma dgu dang bzhi'i phyogs zhes bya ba ni bshad zin pa rnams las gzhan gang yin pa de dag lhag ma'o /
de'i phyir sems kyi khams bdun dang chos kyi khams dang sgra'i khams so; /
caturṇāṃ capradeśa iti rūpagandharasasparśānām /
sa punar yaindriyāvinirbhāgavartinaṃ bhāgaṃ sthāpayitvā mūlavarjyeṣu keśaromādiṣu vartate /
kati sabhāgāḥ /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti prakṛtatvād /
abhisambadhyate /
tepañcādhyātmikā iti 		bzhi'i phyogs zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg pa rnams kyi'o /
de yang dbang po dang tha dad du mi 'jug pa'i cha ma gtogs pa dang drung ma gtogs pa'i skra dang spu la sogs pa yod pa'o /
sten pa mtshungs pa du zhe na /
khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas der sbyar ro /
dvādaśādhyātmikā uktāḥ /
teṣāṃ na vijñāyate katamepañcetyata āha rūpiṇaiti te punaś cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanasparśanadhātavaḥ 		nang gi gzugs can lnga zhes bya ba ni nang gi bcu gnyis bstan pas de dag gi nang na gang yin pa gtol med pas lnga zhes bya ba smos so /
gzugs can zhes bya ba de dag ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi khams so /
kasya sabhāgāḥ kena prakāreṇa sabhāgā iti na vijñāyate ata āha svavijñānair viṣayasāmānyatām upādāyeti gang gi sten pa mtshungs pa dang rnam pa gang gis sten pa mtshungs pa yang mi shes pas de'i phyir /
rang gi rnam par shes pa dag dang yul thun mong ba nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so /
tatra cakṣuṣaḥ svavijñānaṃ cakṣurvijñānam de la mig gi rang gi rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste /
tena svavijñānena cakṣuḥ svaviṣayeṇa rūpeṇa samānam rang gi rnam par shes pa de dang mig rang gi yul gzugs su mtshungs te /
dvayor api cakṣurvijñānotpattāv anuguṇatvāt samānam gnyi ga yang /
mig gi rnam par shes pa skye ba dang mthun pa'i phyir mtshungs pa'o /
sāmānyatāmupādāyeti gṛhītvā cakṣuḥ svaviṣayeṇa rūpeṇa sabhāgam ucyate thun mong pa nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba ni bzung ba ste /
mig gi rang gi yul gzugs dang sten pa mtshungs pa zhes bya'o /
evaṃ śrotrādīnām api svaviṣayaiḥ sabhāgatā vaktavyā de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa yang /
rang gi yul rnams dang sten pa mtshungs pa zhes brjod par bya'o /
etaduktaṃ bhavati ye cakṣurādayaḥ svavijñānair adhyāsitāḥ tesabhāgāḥ /
taeva cakṣurādayaḥ svavijñānaśūnyās /
tatsabhāgāḥ /
kimarthaṃ punas te tatsabhāgā ity ucyante /
svajātisāmānyatām upādāyeti 		de ni 'di skad du /
mig la sogs pa gang dag rang gi rnam par shes pa rnams dang gnas pa de dag sten pa mtshungs pa zhes bstan par 'gyur ro; /
de dag dang mtshungs pa du zhe na /
mig la sogs pa de dag nyid rang gi rnam par shes pas stong pa nyid de de dag dang mtshungs pa'o /
ci'i phyir de dag ni de dag dang mtshungs pa zhes bya zhe na /
rang gi rigs dang mthun pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste /
svavijñānaśūnyāś /
cakṣurādayas te sabhāgānāṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ cakṣurādijātyāsamānā iti taiḥ sadṛśatvāt tatsabhāgā ity ucyante /
ete hyasādhāraṇatvād ya ekasya sabhāgās tatsabhāgā vā tesarvasattvānām apīti niyatam eṣāṃ sabhāgatatsabhāgatvam /
rūpādīnāṃ tu pratisantāne sabhāgatatsabhāgatvam itynavasthitam /
na ca vijñānād anyat kāritram astīti nānyeṣāṃsabhāgatatsabhāgatvam uktam /
pañcaskandhakavibhāṣā samāptā /
kṛtir ācāryasthiramateḥ 		rang gi rnam par shes pa stong pa'i mig la sogs pa de dag ni sten pa mtshungs pa'i mig la sogs pa dang mig la sogs par ris mthun pa ste /
de dag dang 'dra ba'i phyir de dag dang mtshungs pa zhes bya'o /
de dag ni thun mong ma yin pa'i phyir gcig gi sten pa mtshungs pa dang de dag dang mtshungs pa gang yin pa de dag ni /
sems can thams cad kyi yang yin pas /
'di dag gi sten pa mtshungs pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa ni nges pa'o /
gzugs la sogs pa ni so so'i rgyud la sten pa mtshungs pa dang de dag dang mtshungs pa nyid du gnas so /
rnam par shes pa las byed pa gzhan med pa'i phyir /
gzhan dag la ni sten pa mtshungs pa de dang de dag dang mtshungs pa zhes ma brjod do /
phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa bye brag tu bshad pa /
slob dpon blo gros brtan pa sthi ra ma tis mdzad pa rdzogs so /
